Unifying Group-Relative and Self-Distillation Policy Optimization via Sample Routing
Authors: Gengsheng Li, Tianyu Yang, Junfeng Fang, Mingyang Song, Mao Zheng, Haiyun Guo, Dan Zhang, Jinqiao Wang, Tat-Seng Chua
First: 2026-04-02T17:29:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T17:29:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has become a standard paradigm for post-training large language models. While Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is widely adopted, its coarse credit assignment uniformly penalizes failed rollouts, lacking the token-level focus needed to efficiently address specific deviations. Self-Distillation Policy Optimization (SDPO) addresses this by providing denser, more targeted logit-level supervision that facilitates rapid early improvement, yet it frequently collapses during prolonged training. We trace this late-stage instability to two intrinsic flaws: self-distillation on already-correct samples introduces optimization ambiguity, and the self-teacher's signal reliability progressively degrades. To resolve these issues, we propose Sample-Routed Policy Optimization (SRPO), a unified on-policy framework that routes correct samples to GRPO's reward-aligned reinforcement and failed samples to SDPO's targeted logit-level correction. SRPO further incorporates an entropy-aware dynamic weighting mechanism to suppress high-entropy, unreliable distillation targets while emphasizing confident ones. Evaluated across five benchmarks and two model scales, SRPO achieves both the rapid early improvement of SDPO and the long-horizon stability of GRPO. It consistently surpasses the peak performance of both baselines, raising the five-benchmark average on Qwen3-8B by 3.4% over GRPO and 6.3% over SDPO, while simultaneously yielding moderate response lengths and lowering per-step compute cost by up to 17.2%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过样本路由统一组相对与自蒸馏策略优化
基于可验证奖励的强化学习已成为大语言模型后训练的标准范式。组相对策略优化虽被广泛采用，但其粗粒度的信用分配会均匀惩罚失败的轨迹，缺乏针对特定偏差所需的词元级聚焦。自蒸馏策略优化通过提供更密集、更具针对性的对数级监督来解决此问题，促进了早期快速改进，但在长期训练中常出现崩溃。我们将后期不稳定性归因于两个内在缺陷：对已正确样本的自蒸馏引入优化模糊性，且自教师信号的可靠性逐渐下降。为解决这些问题，我们提出样本路由策略优化，这是一个统一的同策略框架，将正确样本路由至组相对优化的奖励对齐强化，将失败样本路由至自蒸馏的针对性对数级修正。该框架进一步引入熵感知动态加权机制，以抑制高熵、不可靠的蒸馏目标，同时强调高置信度目标。在五个基准测试和两种模型规模上的评估表明，样本路由策略优化同时实现了自蒸馏的早期快速改进和组相对优化的长期稳定性，持续超越两个基线的峰值性能，在Qwen3-8B模型上将五个基准平均性能较组相对优化提升3.4%，较自蒸馏提升6.3%，同时生成适中长度的响应，并将单步计算成本降低达17.2%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) methods, where Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) lacks token-level precision and Self-Distillation Policy Optimization (SDPO) suffers from late-stage instability, this paper introduces Sample-Routed Policy Optimization (SRPO) as a unified on-policy framework. The method routes correct samples to GRPO for reward-aligned reinforcement and failed samples to SDPO for targeted logit-level correction, incorporating an entropy-aware dynamic weighting mechanism to prioritize reliable distillation targets. Experimental results across five benchmarks and two model scales show that SRPO combines the rapid early improvement of SDPO with the long-term stability of GRPO, surpassing both baselines' peak performance—raising the average benchmark score on Qwen3-8B by 3.4% over GRPO and 6.3% over SDPO—while also reducing per-step compute cost by up to 17.2% and moderating response lengths.
本文的动机源于现有可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）方法的局限：组相对策略优化（GRPO）缺乏令牌级精度，而自蒸馏策略优化（SDPO）存在后期训练不稳定的问题。为此，研究提出了样本路由策略优化（SRPO）这一统一的在线策略框架，其方法是将正确样本路由至GRPO进行奖励对齐的强化，将失败样本路由至SDPO进行针对性的对数级校正，并引入熵感知动态加权机制以强调可靠的蒸馏目标。在五个基准测试和两种模型规模上的实验结果表明，SRPO结合了SDPO的早期快速改进与GRPO的长期稳定性，性能超越了两者的峰值——在Qwen3-8B模型上将五个基准平均得分较GRPO提升3.4%，较SDPO提升6.3%——同时降低了每步计算成本达17.2%，并生成了长度适中的响应。
SKILL0: In-Context Agentic Reinforcement Learning for Skill Internalization
Authors: Zhengxi Lu, Zhiyuan Yao, Jinyang Wu, Chengcheng Han, Qi Gu, Xunliang Cai, Weiming Lu, Jun Xiao, Yueting Zhuang, Yongliang Shen
First: 2026-04-02T17:03:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T17:03:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Agent skills, structured packages of procedural knowledge and executable resources that agents dynamically load at inference time, have become a reliable mechanism for augmenting LLM agents. Yet inference-time skill augmentation is fundamentally limited: retrieval noise introduces irrelevant guidance, injected skill content imposes substantial token overhead, and the model never truly acquires the knowledge it merely follows. We ask whether skills can instead be internalized into model parameters, enabling zero-shot autonomous behavior without any runtime skill retrieval. We introduce SKILL0, an in-context reinforcement learning framework designed for skill internalization. SKILL0 introduces a training-time curriculum that begins with full skill context and progressively withdraws it. Skills are grouped offline by category and rendered with interaction history into a compact visual context, teaching he model tool invocation and multi-turn task completion. A Dynamic Curriculum then evaluates each skill file's on-policy helpfulness, retaining only those from which the current policy still benefits within a linearly decaying budget, until the agent operates in a fully zero-shot setting. Extensive agentic experiments demonstrate that SKILL0 achieves substantial improvements over the standard RL baseline (+9.7\% for ALFWorld and +6.6\% for Search-QA), while maintaining a highly efficient context of fewer than 0.5k tokens per step. Our code is available at https://github.com/ZJU-REAL/SkillZero.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SKILL0：面向技能内化的上下文智能体强化学习
智能体技能作为程序性知识与可执行资源的结构化封装包，在推理时动态加载，已成为增强大语言模型智能体的可靠机制。但推理时的技能增强存在根本性局限：检索噪声会引入无关指导，注入的技能内容带来大量标记开销，且模型从未真正掌握其仅被动遵循的知识。我们提出能否将技能内化至模型参数中，实现无需运行时技能检索的零样本自主行为。为此，我们提出SKILL0——一个专为技能内化设计的上下文强化学习框架。SKILL0引入训练阶段的课程学习机制：从完整技能上下文开始，逐步撤除技能支持。技能按类别离线分组，并与交互历史共同编码为紧凑的视觉上下文，以指导模型进行工具调用和多轮任务完成。动态课程评估每个技能文件在策略上的有效性，仅在线性衰减的预算内保留当前策略仍能受益的技能，直至智能体完全在零样本环境下运行。大量智能体实验表明，SKILL0相比标准强化学习基线取得显著提升（ALFWorld任务提升9.7%，Search-QA任务提升6.6%），同时保持每步少于0.5千标记的高效上下文占用。代码已开源：https://github.com/ZJU-REAL/SkillZero。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitations of inference-time skill augmentation for LLM agents, such as retrieval noise and token overhead, and aims to internalize skills into model parameters for zero-shot autonomous behavior. The method, SKILL0, employs an in-context reinforcement learning framework with a training-time curriculum that gradually withdraws skill context, groups skills by category into a compact visual format, and uses a Dynamic Curriculum to retain only beneficial skills within a decaying budget. Experimental results show substantial improvements over standard RL baselines, with gains of +9.7% on ALFWorld and +6.6% on Search-QA, while maintaining efficient context usage under 0.5k tokens per step.
本文的动机是针对LLM智能体在推理时技能增强的局限性，如检索噪声和令牌开销，旨在将技能内化到模型参数中，以实现零样本自主行为。方法SKILL0采用上下文内强化学习框架，通过训练时课程逐步撤出技能上下文，将技能按类别分组为紧凑的视觉格式，并利用动态课程在衰减预算内仅保留有益技能。实验结果表明，相比标准RL基线有显著提升，在ALFWorld上提高9.7%，在Search-QA上提高6.6%，同时保持每步少于0.5k令牌的高效上下文使用。
Model-Based Reinforcement Learning for Control under Time-Varying Dynamics
Authors: Klemens Iten, Bruce Lee, Chenhao Li, Lenart Treven, Andreas Krause, Bhavya Sukhija
First: 2026-04-02T16:52:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T16:52:59+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 5 figues, 2 tables. This work has been submitted to the IEEE for possible publication
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning-based control methods typically assume stationary system dynamics, an assumption often violated in real-world systems due to drift, wear, or changing operating conditions. We study reinforcement learning for control under time-varying dynamics. We consider a continual model-based reinforcement learning setting in which an agent repeatedly learns and controls a dynamical system whose transition dynamics evolve across episodes. We analyze the problem using Gaussian process dynamics models under frequentist variation-budget assumptions. Our analysis shows that persistent non-stationarity requires explicitly limiting the influence of outdated data to maintain calibrated uncertainty and meaningful dynamic regret guarantees. Motivated by these insights, we propose a practical optimistic model-based reinforcement learning algorithm with adaptive data buffer mechanisms and demonstrate improved performance on continuous control benchmarks with non-stationary dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：时变动态下基于模型的强化学习控制方法
基于学习的控制方法通常假设系统动态是平稳的，然而在实际系统中，由于漂移、磨损或运行条件变化，这一假设常被违背。本研究探讨时变动态下的强化学习控制问题。我们考虑一种持续的基于模型强化学习场景：智能体需反复学习并控制一个其转移动态随任务周期演化的动态系统。我们采用高斯过程动态模型，在频率学派变差预算假设下分析该问题。分析表明，持续的非平稳性要求显式限制过时数据的影响，以维持校准后的不确定性度量和有效的动态遗憾保证。基于这些发现，我们提出一种实用的乐观型基于模型强化学习算法，该算法配备自适应数据缓冲机制，并在具有非平稳动态的连续控制基准测试中展现出更优性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of applying reinforcement learning to control systems with time-varying dynamics, which violate the common assumption of stationary dynamics due to factors like wear or changing conditions. The authors study a continual model-based reinforcement learning setting where an agent repeatedly interacts with a system whose dynamics evolve across episodes, analyzing the problem using Gaussian process models under frequentist variation-budget assumptions. Their analysis reveals that persistent non-stationarity necessitates limiting the influence of outdated data to maintain calibrated uncertainty and achieve meaningful dynamic regret guarantees. Motivated by this, they propose a practical optimistic model-based reinforcement learning algorithm with adaptive data buffer mechanisms, demonstrating improved performance on continuous control benchmarks with non-stationary dynamics.
本文针对强化学习在时变动力学控制系统中的应用挑战展开研究，这类系统因磨损或条件变化而违背了常见的稳态动力学假设。作者研究了一种持续基于模型的强化学习设置，其中智能体反复与动力学随任务演变的系统交互，并基于频率主义变化预算假设使用高斯过程模型进行分析。分析表明，持续的时变性需要明确限制过时数据的影响，以保持校准的不确定性和实现有意义的动态遗憾保证。基于此，他们提出了一种实用的乐观模型强化学习算法，采用自适应数据缓冲机制，并在具有非稳态动力学的连续控制基准测试中展示了性能提升。
One Sample to Rule Them All: Extreme Data Efficiency in Multidiscipline Reasoning with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yiyuan Li, Zhen Huang, Yanan Wu, Weixun Wang, Xuefeng Li, Yijia Luo, Wenbo Su, Bo Zheng, Pengfei Liu
First: 2026-01-06T15:41:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T16:27:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The reasoning ability of large language models (LLMs) can be unleashed with reinforcement learning (RL) (OpenAI, 2024; DeepSeek-AI et al., 2025a; Zeng et al., 2025). The success of existing RL attempts in LLMs usually rely on high-quality samples of large volumes. In this paper, we challenge conventional assumptions about data requirements in RL for LLMs by demonstrating the effectiveness of one-shot reinforcement learning. Specifically, we introduce polymath learning, a framework for designing one training sample that elicits multidisciplinary reasoning improvement. We present three key findings: (1) A single, strategically selected math reasoning sample can produce significant performance improvements across multiple domains, including physics, chemistry, and biology; (2) Analysis of salient mathematical skills provides insight into the characteristics associated with effective polymath samples; and (3) An engineered synthetic sample that integrates multidisciplinary elements and broader skill coverage achieves stronger performance than naturally occurring individual samples. Across various reasoning benchmarks, polymath learning achieves stronger performance than larger datasets, demonstrating that reasoning structure and skills in samples, rather than quantity, may be the key to unlock enhanced reasoning capabilities in language models. Our results suggest a shift, dubbed as sample engineering, toward precision engineering of samples that complements simply increasing data volume.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一例统御全局：强化学习在多学科推理中的极致数据效率
大型语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力可通过强化学习（RL）得以释放（OpenAI, 2024；深度求索AI等, 2025a；Zeng等, 2025）。现有LLMs强化学习尝试的成功通常依赖于大量高质量样本。本文通过展示单样本强化学习的有效性，挑战了关于LLMs强化学习数据需求的传统假设。具体而言，我们提出博学学习框架，通过设计单个训练样本来激发多学科推理能力的提升。我们呈现三项关键发现：（1）单个经策略性选取的数学推理样本可在物理、化学、生物等多个领域产生显著的性能提升；（2）对关键数学技能的分析揭示了有效博学样本的特征关联；（3）整合多学科要素与更广泛技能覆盖的工程化合成样本，其性能优于自然存在的单一样本。在多项推理基准测试中，博学学习以少于大规模数据集的样本量实现了更强性能，表明样本中的推理结构与技能（而非数量）可能是解锁语言模型增强推理能力的关键。我们的研究成果指向一种被称为“样本工程”的范式转变——通过精准的样本工程设计来补充单纯增加数据量的传统路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high data demands of conventional reinforcement learning for large language models, this paper challenges the need for large volumes by proposing polymath learning, a one-shot reinforcement learning framework that uses a single, strategically engineered training sample to improve multidisciplinary reasoning. The method involves designing a sample that integrates key mathematical skills and multidisciplinary elements, with experimental results showing that this single sample significantly boosts performance across physics, chemistry, and biology benchmarks, outperforming larger datasets and highlighting the importance of sample quality and structure over quantity.
本文针对大语言模型强化学习通常需要大量高质量数据的问题，提出了一种名为博学学习的单样本强化学习框架，旨在通过精心设计的单个训练样本来提升多学科推理能力。该方法通过构建一个融合多学科要素和广泛数学技能的合成样本，实验结果表明，该单一样本能在物理、化学和生物学等多个推理基准上带来显著性能提升，其效果优于使用更大数据集的方法，从而强调了样本结构和技能覆盖比数据量更为关键。
Reflection of Episodes: Learning to Play Game from Expert and Self Experiences
Authors: Xiaojie Xu, Zongyuan Li, Chang Lu, Runnan Qi, Yanan Ni, Lumin Jiang, Xiangbei Liu, Xuebo Zhang, Yongchun Fang, Kuihua Huang, Xian Guo, Zhanghua Wu, Zhenya Li
First: 2025-02-19T02:53:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T16:24:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
StarCraft II is a complex and dynamic real-time strategy (RTS) game environment, which is very suitable for artificial intelligence and reinforcement learning research. To address the problem of Large Language Model(LLM) learning in complex environments through self-reflection, we propose a Reflection of Episodes(ROE) framework based on expert experience and self-experience. This framework first obtains key information in the game through a keyframe selection method, then makes decisions based on expert experience and self-experience. After a game is completed, it reflects on the previous experience to obtain new self-experience. Finally, in the experiment, our method beat the robot under the Very Hard difficulty in TextStarCraft II. We analyze the data of the LLM in the process of the game in detail, verified its effectiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：片段反思：基于专家与自身经验学习游戏对战
《星际争霸II》作为复杂动态的即时战略游戏环境，非常适合人工智能与强化学习研究。针对大语言模型在复杂环境中通过自我反思进行学习的问题，我们提出基于专家经验与自身经验的片段反思框架。该框架首先通过关键帧选择方法获取游戏关键信息，随后依据专家经验与自身经验进行决策。单局游戏结束后，通过对先前经验的反思获得新的自身经验。实验表明，本方法在TextStarCraft II的极难难度下战胜了机器人。我们详细分析了大语言模型在游戏过程中的数据，验证了该框架的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to enhance Large Language Model (LLM) learning in complex environments like StarCraft II through self-reflection, this paper introduces the Reflection of Episodes (ROE) framework. The method leverages both expert and self-experience by first extracting key game information via keyframe selection, then making decisions based on this combined experience, and finally reflecting post-game to generate new self-experience. Experimentally, the approach successfully defeated the Very Hard difficulty bot in TextStarCraft II, with detailed game data analysis confirming its effectiveness.
本文旨在解决大型语言模型在复杂环境中通过自我反思进行学习的问题，为此提出了基于专家经验和自我经验的反思片段框架。该方法首先通过关键帧选择获取游戏中的关键信息，然后结合专家与自我经验进行决策，并在游戏结束后通过反思生成新的自我经验。实验结果表明，该方法在TextStarCraft II中击败了最高难度机器人，并通过详细的过程数据分析验证了其有效性。
When to ASK: Uncertainty-Gated Language Assistance for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Juarez Monteiro, Nathan Gavenski, Gianlucca Zuin, Adriano Veloso
First: 2026-04-02T16:19:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T16:19:20+00:00
Comments: In Proceedings of International Joint Conference on Neural Networks (IJCNN)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) agents often struggle with out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios, leading to high uncertainty and random behavior. While language models (LMs) contain valuable world knowledge, larger ones incur high computational costs, hindering real-time use, and exhibit limitations in autonomous planning. We introduce Adaptive Safety through Knowledge (ASK), which combines smaller LMs with trained RL policies to enhance OOD generalization without retraining. ASK employs Monte Carlo Dropout to assess uncertainty and queries the LM for action suggestions only when uncertainty exceeds a set threshold. This selective use preserves the efficiency of existing policies while leveraging the language model's reasoning in uncertain situations. In experiments on the FrozenLake environment, ASK shows no improvement in-domain, but demonstrates robust navigation in transfer tasks, achieving a reward of 0.95. Our findings indicate that effective neuro-symbolic integration requires careful orchestration rather than simple combination, highlighting the need for sufficient model scale and effective hybridization mechanisms for successful OOD generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：何时询问：面向强化学习的不确定性门控语言辅助
强化学习（RL）智能体常因分布外（OOD）场景而表现不佳，导致高不确定性和随机行为。虽然语言模型（LM）蕴含丰富的世界知识，但大型模型计算成本高昂，难以实时应用，且在自主规划方面存在局限。我们提出基于知识的自适应安全（ASK）方法，将小型语言模型与训练好的强化学习策略相结合，无需重新训练即可提升OOD泛化能力。ASK采用蒙特卡洛Dropout评估不确定性，仅当不确定性超过设定阈值时才向语言模型查询行动建议。这种选择性调用机制在保持现有策略效率的同时，能有效利用语言模型在不确定情境下的推理能力。在FrozenLake环境实验中，ASK在域内任务未表现提升，但在迁移任务中展现出稳健的导航能力，获得0.95的奖励值。研究表明，有效的神经符号集成需要精细协调而非简单组合，同时强调足够的模型规模和有效的混合机制对实现成功OOD泛化的重要性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of reinforcement learning (RL) agents performing poorly in out-of-distribution (OOD) scenarios, where they exhibit high uncertainty and random actions. To leverage the world knowledge of language models (LMs) without the computational cost of large models or full retraining, the authors propose Adaptive Safety through Knowledge (ASK), a method that gates LM assistance based on the agent's uncertainty. ASK uses Monte Carlo Dropout to estimate uncertainty and queries a smaller LM for action suggestions only when this uncertainty exceeds a predefined threshold, thereby combining efficient RL policy execution with on-demand symbolic reasoning. Experimental results in the FrozenLake environment show that while ASK provides no in-domain benefit, it achieves robust OOD generalization in transfer tasks, attaining a reward of 0.95, underscoring that successful neuro-symbolic integration requires careful orchestration of when to use language assistance.
本文针对强化学习智能体在分布外场景中表现不佳、不确定性高且行为随机的问题展开研究。为利用语言模型的世界知识，同时避免大型模型的高计算成本或重新训练，作者提出了自适应知识安全方法，该方法根据智能体的不确定性来门控语言模型的辅助。ASK采用蒙特卡洛丢弃法来估计不确定性，仅当不确定性超过预设阈值时才查询较小的语言模型以获取行动建议，从而将高效的强化学习策略执行与按需的符号推理相结合。在FrozenLake环境中的实验表明，ASK在域内没有提升，但在迁移任务中实现了鲁棒的分布外泛化，获得了0.95的奖励，这证明成功的神经符号集成需要精心设计语言辅助的使用时机。
Planning in Branch-and-Bound: Model-Based Reinforcement Learning for Exact Combinatorial Optimization
Authors: Paul Strang, Zacharie Alès, Côme Bissuel, Olivier Juan, Safia Kedad-Sidhoum, Emmanuel Rachelson
First: 2025-11-12T11:28:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T16:17:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Mixed-Integer Linear Programming (MILP) lies at the core of many real-world combinatorial optimization (CO) problems, traditionally solved by branch-and-bound (B&B). A key driver influencing B&B solvers efficiency is the variable selection heuristic that guides branching decisions. Looking to move beyond static, hand-crafted heuristics, recent work has explored adapting traditional reinforcement learning (RL) algorithms to the B&B setting, aiming to learn branching strategies tailored to specific MILP distributions. In parallel, RL agents have achieved remarkable success in board games, a very specific type of combinatorial problems, by leveraging environment simulators to plan via Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS). Building on these developments, we introduce Plan-and-Branch-and-Bound (PlanB&B), a model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) agent that leverages a learned internal model of the B&B dynamics to discover improved branching strategies. Computational experiments empirically validate our approach, with our MBRL branching agent outperforming previous state-of-the-art RL methods across four standard MILP benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分支定界中的规划：基于模型的强化学习在精确组合优化中的应用
混合整数线性规划（MILP）是许多现实世界组合优化问题的核心，传统上通过分支定界法求解。影响分支定界求解器效率的关键因素是指导分支决策的变量选择启发式方法。为超越静态人工设计的启发式方法，近期研究探索将传统强化学习算法应用于分支定界框架，旨在学习针对特定MILP分布定制的分支策略。与此同时，强化学习智能体通过利用环境模拟器进行蒙特卡洛树搜索规划，在棋盘游戏这类特定组合问题上取得了显著成功。基于这些进展，我们提出Plan-and-Branch-and-Bound（PlanB&B）——一种基于模型的强化学习智能体，它利用学习得到的分支定界动态内部模型来发现更优的分支策略。计算实验通过四个标准MILP基准测试验证了本方法的有效性，我们的基于模型强化学习分支智能体在性能上超越了所有先前的先进强化学习方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to move beyond static heuristics for variable selection in branch-and-bound (B&B) solvers for Mixed-Integer Linear Programming (MILP), this paper introduces PlanB&B, a model-based reinforcement learning (MBRL) agent that uses a learned internal model of B&B dynamics to plan and discover improved branching strategies. The method leverages environment simulation for planning, akin to techniques used in board games, to tailor branching decisions to specific MILP distributions. Experimental results demonstrate that PlanB&B outperforms previous state-of-the-art RL methods across four standard MILP benchmarks, validating its effectiveness in enhancing solver efficiency.
本文旨在超越混合整数线性规划（MILP）分支定界求解器中静态手工设计的变量选择启发式方法，提出了PlanB&B，这是一种基于模型的强化学习（MBRL）智能体，它通过学习分支定界动态的内部模型来规划并发现改进的分支策略。该方法借鉴了棋盘游戏中利用环境模拟进行规划的思路，针对特定MILP分布定制分支决策。计算实验结果表明，PlanB&B在四个标准MILP基准测试中优于先前最先进的强化学习方法，有效提升了求解器效率。
Unsupervised Behavioral Compression: Learning Low-Dimensional Policy Manifolds through State-Occupancy Matching
Authors: Andrea Fraschini, Davide Tenedini, Riccardo Zamboni, Mirco Mutti, Marcello Restelli
First: 2026-03-27T23:16:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T16:05:51+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) is widely recognized as sample-inefficient, a limitation attributable in part to the high dimensionality and substantial functional redundancy inherent to the policy parameter space. A recent framework, which we refer to as Action-based Policy Compression (APC), mitigates this issue by compressing the parameter space $Θ$ into a low-dimensional latent manifold $\mathcal Z$ using a learned generative mapping $g:\mathcal Z \to Θ$. However, its performance is severely constrained by relying on immediate action-matching as a reconstruction loss, a myopic proxy for behavioral similarity that suffers from compounding errors across sequential decisions. To overcome this bottleneck, we introduce Occupancy-based Policy Compression (OPC), which enhances APC by shifting behavior representation from immediate action-matching to long-horizon state-space coverage. Specifically, we propose two principal improvements: (1) we curate the dataset generation with an information-theoretic uniqueness metric that delivers a diverse population of policies; and (2) we propose a fully differentiable compression objective that directly minimizes the divergence between the true and reconstructed mixture occupancy distributions. These modifications force the generative model to organize the latent space around true functional similarity, promoting a latent representation that generalizes over a broad spectrum of behaviors while retaining most of the original parameter space's expressivity. Finally, we empirically validate the advantages of our contributions across multiple continuous control benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无监督行为压缩：通过状态占用匹配学习低维策略流形
深度强化学习（DRL）普遍被认为样本效率低下，这一局限部分归因于策略参数空间的高维性和显著的功能冗余。近期提出的基于动作的策略压缩（APC）框架通过生成映射 $g:\mathcal Z \to Θ$ 将参数空间 $Θ$ 压缩至低维潜流形 $\mathcal Z$ 以缓解该问题，但其性能因依赖即时动作匹配作为重构损失而严重受限——这种短视的行为相似性代理会在序列决策中产生累积误差。为突破此瓶颈，我们提出基于占用的策略压缩（OPC），通过将行为表征从即时动作匹配转向长时程状态空间覆盖来增强APC。具体改进包括：（1）采用信息论独特性指标优化数据集生成，以获取多样化的策略种群；（2）提出完全可微的压缩目标，直接最小化真实与重构混合占用分布之间的散度。这些改进迫使生成模型围绕真实功能相似性组织潜空间，形成能泛化至广泛行为谱系、同时保留原参数空间大部分表达能力的潜表征。最后，我们在多个连续控制基准任务中实证验证了所提方法的优势。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the sample inefficiency of deep reinforcement learning due to high-dimensional policy parameter spaces, this paper addresses the limitations of Action-based Policy Compression (APC), which suffers from compounding errors by focusing on immediate action-matching. The method introduces Occupancy-based Policy Compression (OPC), which shifts to long-horizon state-space coverage by curating a diverse policy dataset using an information-theoretic uniqueness metric and optimizing a differentiable compression objective that minimizes divergence between true and reconstructed mixture occupancy distributions. Experimental results across continuous control benchmarks demonstrate that OPC organizes the latent space around functional similarity, improving generalization and retaining expressivity compared to APC.
本文针对深度强化学习中因策略参数空间高维导致的样本效率低下问题，指出基于动作的策略压缩（APC）方法因依赖即时动作匹配而存在复合误差的局限。方法上提出了基于占用度的策略压缩（OPC），通过信息论独特性指标构建多样化策略数据集，并采用可微压缩目标最小化真实与重建混合占用分布之间的差异，从而转向长期状态空间覆盖。在连续控制基准测试中的实验结果表明，OPC能围绕功能相似性组织潜在空间，相比APC在广泛行为上提升了泛化能力并保持了表达性。
Multi-Agent Video Recommenders: Evolution, Patterns, and Open Challenges
Authors: Srivaths Ranganathan, Abhishek Dharmaratnakar, Anushree Sinha, Debanshu Das
Venue: WSDM
First: 2026-04-02T16:04:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T16:04:52+00:00
Comments: Accepted for publication in The Nineteenth ACM International Conference on Web Search and Data Mining (WSDM Companion 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Video recommender systems are among the most popular and impactful applications of AI, shaping content consumption and influencing culture for billions of users. Traditional single-model recommenders, which optimize static engagement metrics, are increasingly limited in addressing the dynamic requirements of modern platforms. In response, multi-agent architectures are redefining how video recommender systems serve, learn, and adapt to both users and datasets. These agent-based systems coordinate specialized agents responsible for video understanding, reasoning, memory, and feedback, to provide precise, explainable recommendations. In this survey, we trace the evolution of multi-agent video recommendation systems (MAVRS). We combine ideas from multi-agent recommender systems, foundation models, and conversational AI, culminating in the emerging field of large language model (LLM)-powered MAVRS. We present a taxonomy of collaborative patterns and analyze coordination mechanisms across diverse video domains, ranging from short-form clips to educational platforms. We discuss representative frameworks, including early multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) systems such as MMRF and recent LLM-driven architectures like MACRec and Agent4Rec, to illustrate these patterns. We also outline open challenges in scalability, multimodal understanding, incentive alignment, and identify research directions such as hybrid reinforcement learning-LLM systems, lifelong personalization and self-improving recommender systems.
中文标题/摘要
标题：多智能体视频推荐系统：演进、模式与开放挑战
视频推荐系统是人工智能最受欢迎且最具影响力的应用之一，影响着数十亿用户的内容消费与文化形态。传统单模型推荐系统以静态参与度指标为优化目标，日益难以满足现代平台的动态需求。为此，多智能体架构正在重新定义视频推荐系统服务用户、学习数据及适应环境的方式。这类基于智能体的系统通过协调负责视频理解、推理、记忆与反馈的专用智能体，提供精准且可解释的推荐。本文追溯了多智能体视频推荐系统的演进历程，融合多智能体推荐系统、基础模型与对话式人工智能的研究思路，最终聚焦于新兴的大语言模型驱动多智能体推荐系统领域。我们提出协作模式的分类体系，分析从短视频片段到教育平台等多元视频领域的协调机制，并通过早期多智能体强化学习系统（如MMRF）与近期大语言模型驱动架构（如MACRec、Agent4Rec）等代表性框架阐释这些模式。同时，我们概述了可扩展性、多模态理解、激励对齐等开放挑战，并指出混合强化学习-大语言模型系统、终身个性化及自进化推荐系统等研究方向。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of traditional single-model video recommenders in handling dynamic platform needs, this survey explores the evolution of multi-agent video recommendation systems (MAVRS) that coordinate specialized agents for tasks like understanding and reasoning to deliver precise, explainable recommendations. The method involves tracing MAVRS development, integrating concepts from multi-agent systems, foundation models, and conversational AI, and presenting a taxonomy of collaborative patterns and coordination mechanisms across video domains. Key experimental results highlight representative frameworks, from early multi-agent reinforcement learning systems like MMRF to recent LLM-driven architectures such as MACRec and Agent4Rec, while also outlining open challenges in scalability and multimodal understanding, pointing to future research directions like hybrid reinforcement learning-LLM systems.
本文的动机在于传统单模型视频推荐系统难以满足现代平台的动态需求，因此探讨了多智能体视频推荐系统（MAVRS）的演进，该系统通过协调负责视频理解、推理等任务的专门智能体来提供精准、可解释的推荐。方法上，本文追溯了MAVRS的发展历程，融合了多智能体推荐系统、基础模型和对话式AI的思想，并提出了一种跨视频领域（从短视频到教育平台）的协作模式分类和协调机制分析。主要实验结果展示了代表性框架，包括早期的多智能体强化学习系统如MMRF和近期的大语言模型驱动架构如MACRec和Agent4Rec，同时指出了可扩展性、多模态理解等开放挑战，并指明了混合强化学习-大语言模型系统等未来研究方向。
Olaf: Bringing an Animated Character to Life in the Physical World
Authors: David Müller, Espen Knoop, Dario Mylonopoulos, Agon Serifi, Michael A. Hopkins, Ruben Grandia, Moritz Bächer
First: 2025-12-18T16:10:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T16:03:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Animated characters often move in non-physical ways and have proportions that are far from a typical walking robot. This provides an ideal platform for innovation in both mechanical design and stylized motion control. In this paper, we bring Olaf to life in the physical world, relying on reinforcement learning guided by animation references for control. To create the illusion of Olaf's feet moving along his body, we hide two asymmetric legs under a soft foam skirt. To fit actuators inside the character, we use spherical and planar linkages in the arms, mouth, and eyes. Because the walk cycle results in harsh contact sounds, we introduce additional rewards that noticeably reduce impact noise. The large head, driven by small actuators in the character's slim neck, creates a risk of overheating, amplified by the costume. To keep actuators from overheating, we feed temperature values as additional inputs to policies, introducing new rewards to keep them within bounds. We validate the efficacy of our modeling in simulation and on hardware, demonstrating an unmatched level of believability for a costumed robotic character.
中文标题/摘要
标题：奥拉夫：将动画角色带入现实世界的物理实体
动画角色常以非物理方式运动，其身体比例与典型行走机器人相去甚远，这为机械设计和风格化运动控制提供了创新平台。本文通过动画参考引导的强化学习控制，将奥拉夫在物理世界中具象化。为实现其双脚沿身体移动的视觉错觉，我们在软质泡沫裙下隐藏了两条非对称腿部结构；为在角色内部容纳执行器，于手臂、嘴部和眼部采用球面与平面连杆机构。针对行走周期产生的剧烈接触噪音，我们引入额外奖励函数以显著降低冲击声。角色纤细颈部内的小型执行器驱动其硕大头部，加之服装包裹，存在过热风险。为此，我们将温度值作为策略的附加输入，通过新增奖励机制确保执行器温度处于安全范围。通过仿真与硬件实验验证了建模有效性，实现了迄今最高可信度的服装机器人角色表现。
Summary / 总结
The motivation is to physically realize an animated character with non-physical proportions and motion, requiring innovation in mechanical design and control. The method involves using reinforcement learning guided by animation references for control, designing hidden asymmetric legs under a soft skirt to create the illusion of feet moving along the body, and employing spherical and planar linkages to fit actuators in the arms, mouth, and eyes. Experimental results show that additional rewards reduce impact noise during walking, temperature-aware policies prevent actuator overheating, and both simulation and hardware validation demonstrate an unmatched level of believability for a costumed robotic character.
该研究的动机是实现一个具有非物理比例和运动的动画角色的物理化，这需要在机械设计和控制方面进行创新。方法包括使用基于动画参考的强化学习进行控制，设计隐藏在软质裙摆下的不对称腿部以营造脚沿身体移动的错觉，并采用球形和平面的连杆机构将执行器集成到手臂、嘴巴和眼睛中。实验结果表明，额外的奖励函数显著降低了行走时的冲击噪音，温度感知策略防止了执行器过热，仿真和硬件验证均证明了该装扮机器人角色实现了前所未有的逼真度。
Learning to Play Blackjack: A Curriculum Learning Perspective
Authors: Amirreza Alasti, Efe Erdal, Yücel Celik, Theresa Eimer
First: 2026-03-31T15:54:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T15:28:21+00:00
Comments: Accepted as an oral presentation at the International Conference on Distributed Artificial Intelligence (DAI 2025). 16 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) agents often struggle with efficiency and performance in complex environments. We propose a novel framework that uses a Large Language Model (LLM) to dynamically generate a curriculum over available actions, enabling the agent to incorporate each action individually. We apply this framework to the game of Blackjack, where the LLM creates a multi-stage training path that progressively introduces complex actions to a Tabular Q-Learning and a Deep Q-Network (DQN) agent. Our evaluation in a realistic 8-deck simulation over 10 independent runs demonstrates significant performance gains over standard training methods. The curriculum-based approach increases the DQN agent's average win rate from 43.97% to 47.41%, reduces the average bust rate from 32.9% to 28.0%, and accelerates the overall workflow by over 74%, with the agent's full training completing faster than the baseline's evaluation phase alone. These results validate that LLM-guided curricula can build more effective, robust, and efficient RL agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习玩二十一点：课程学习的视角
强化学习智能体在复杂环境中常面临效率与性能的挑战。本文提出一种创新框架，利用大语言模型动态生成可用动作的课程，使智能体能够逐个掌握每个动作。我们将该框架应用于二十一点游戏，通过大语言模型为表格Q学习和深度Q网络智能体设计多阶段训练路径，逐步引入复杂动作。在8副牌的真实模拟环境中进行10次独立实验评估，结果显示该方法较标准训练方式取得显著性能提升：基于课程的训练使DQN智能体平均胜率从43.97%提升至47.41%，平均爆牌率从32.9%降至28.0%，整体工作流加速超74%，其完整训练耗时甚至短于基线方法的单一评估阶段。这些结果验证了LLM引导的课程能够构建更高效、鲁棒且性能优越的强化学习智能体。

Motivated by the inefficiency of standard reinforcement learning in complex settings, this paper introduces a novel framework where a Large Language Model dynamically generates a training curriculum over actions to improve learning. The method applies this LLM-guided curriculum to Blackjack, progressively introducing complex actions to both Tabular Q-Learning and Deep Q-Network agents during training. Experimental results in an 8-deck simulation show significant gains: the DQN agent's average win rate increased from 43.97% to 47.41%, the bust rate dropped from 32.9% to 28.0%, and overall training workflow accelerated by over 74%, demonstrating more effective and efficient RL agents.

Auction-Based Online Policy Adaptation for Evolving Objectives
Authors: Guruprerana Shabadi, Kaushik Mallik
First: 2026-04-02T15:17:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T15:17:20+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider multi-objective reinforcement learning problems where objectives come from an identical family -- such as the class of reachability objectives -- and may appear or disappear at runtime. Our goal is to design adaptive policies that can efficiently adjust their behaviors as the set of active objectives changes. To solve this problem, we propose a modular framework where each objective is supported by a selfish local policy, and coordination is achieved through a novel auction-based mechanism: policies bid for the right to execute their actions, with bids reflecting the urgency of the current state. The highest bidder selects the action, enabling a dynamic and interpretable trade-off among objectives. Going back to the original adaptation problem, when objectives change, the system adapts by simply adding or removing the corresponding policies. Moreover, as objectives arise from the same family, identical copies of a parameterized policy can be deployed, facilitating immediate adaptation at runtime. We show how the selfish local policies can be computed by turning the problem into a general-sum game, where the policies compete against each other to fulfill their own objectives. To succeed, each policy must not only optimize its own objective, but also reason about the presence of other goals and learn to produce calibrated bids that reflect relative priority. In our implementation, the policies are trained concurrently using proximal policy optimization (PPO). We evaluate on Atari Assault and a gridworld-based path-planning task with dynamic targets. Our method achieves substantially better performance than monolithic policies trained with PPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向动态演化的目标：基于拍卖机制的在线策略自适应方法
本文研究多目标强化学习问题，其中目标来自同一家族（如可达性目标类），并可能在运行时动态出现或消失。我们旨在设计能够随活跃目标集变化而高效调整行为的自适应策略。为此，我们提出一种模块化框架：每个目标由一个自私的局部策略支持，并通过新型拍卖机制实现协调——各策略通过竞价争夺行动执行权，出价反映当前状态的紧迫性。最高出价者选择行动，实现目标间动态且可解释的权衡。当目标发生变化时，系统仅需增删对应策略即可完成适应。由于目标源自同一家族，可部署参数化策略的相同副本，实现运行时即时适应。我们将自私局部策略的计算转化为一般和博弈问题，策略间通过竞争实现各自目标。每个策略不仅需优化自身目标，还需推理其他目标的存在，并学习生成反映相对优先级的校准出价。在实现中，我们使用近端策略优化（PPO）并行训练策略。通过在Atari《Assault》游戏和基于网格世界的动态目标路径规划任务上的评估，本方法性能显著优于使用PPO训练的单一策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses multi-objective reinforcement learning where objectives from a common family, like reachability, can dynamically appear or disappear during runtime, necessitating adaptive policies. The proposed method employs a modular auction-based framework: each objective is managed by a selfish local policy that bids for action control based on current urgency, with the highest bidder selecting the action to enable dynamic trade-offs; when objectives change, policies are simply added or removed, and since objectives share a family, parameterized copies allow immediate adaptation. Experimental results on Atari Assault and a gridworld path-planning task with dynamic targets show that this approach significantly outperforms monolithic policies trained with proximal policy optimization (PPO).
本文研究多目标强化学习问题，其中目标来自同一类别（如可达性目标），并可能在运行时动态出现或消失，需要设计自适应策略。所提出的方法采用模块化的拍卖机制：每个目标由一个自私的局部策略管理，该策略根据当前紧急程度出价以争取行动控制权，出价最高者选择行动，实现动态权衡；当目标变化时，只需添加或移除相应策略，且由于目标属于同一类别，参数化副本可实现即时适应。在Atari Assault和基于网格世界的动态目标路径规划任务上的实验结果表明，该方法显著优于使用近端策略优化（PPO）训练的整体策略。
Optimizing RAG Rerankers with LLM Feedback via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yuhang Wu, Xiangqing Shen, Fanfan Wang, Cangqi Zhou, Zhen Wu, Xinyu Dai, Rui Xia
First: 2026-04-02T14:19:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T14:19:47+00:00
Comments: 16 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rerankers play a pivotal role in refining retrieval results for Retrieval-Augmented Generation. However, current reranking models are typically optimized on static human annotated relevance labels in isolation, decoupled from the downstream generation process. This isolation leads to a fundamental misalignment: documents identified as topically relevant by information retrieval metrics often fail to provide the actual utility required by the LLM for precise answer generation. To bridge this gap, we introduce ReRanking Preference Optimization (RRPO), a reinforcement learning framework that directly aligns reranking with the LLM's generation quality. By formulating reranking as a sequential decision-making process, RRPO optimizes for context utility using LLM feedback, thereby eliminating the need for expensive human annotations. To ensure training stability, we further introduce a reference-anchored deterministic baseline. Extensive experiments on knowledge-intensive benchmarks demonstrate that RRPO significantly outperforms strong baselines, including the powerful list-wise reranker RankZephyr. Further analysis highlights the versatility of our framework: it generalizes seamlessly to diverse readers (e.g., GPT-4o), integrates orthogonally with query expansion modules like Query2Doc, and remains robust even when trained with noisy supervisors.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习利用大语言模型反馈优化RAG重排序器
重排序器在优化检索增强生成的检索结果中起着关键作用。然而，当前重排序模型通常仅基于静态人工标注的相关性标签进行独立优化，与下游生成过程脱节。这种隔离导致根本性错位：信息检索指标判定为话题相关的文档，往往无法为大语言模型提供生成精确答案所需的实际效用。为弥合这一差距，我们提出重排序偏好优化（RRPO）——一种通过强化学习直接对齐重排序与大语言模型生成质量的框架。通过将重排序构建为序列决策过程，RRPO利用大语言模型反馈优化上下文效用，从而无需昂贵的人工标注。为确保训练稳定性，我们进一步引入基于参考的确定性基线。在知识密集型基准测试上的大量实验表明，RRPO显著优于包括强大的列表式重排序器RankZephyr在内的基线模型。进一步分析凸显了本框架的普适性：可无缝泛化至不同阅读器（如GPT-4o），与Query2Doc等查询扩展模块正交集成，即使在噪声监督下训练仍保持鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the misalignment between traditional rerankers optimized on static relevance labels and the actual utility required by LLMs for precise answer generation in Retrieval-Augmented Generation systems. To bridge this gap, the authors introduce ReRanking Preference Optimization (RRPO), a reinforcement learning framework that formulates reranking as a sequential decision-making process and optimizes it directly using LLM feedback on generation quality, thereby eliminating the need for costly human annotations. Experimental results on knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that RRPO significantly outperforms strong baselines like RankZephyr, and further analysis demonstrates its versatility in generalizing to diverse readers, integrating with query expansion modules, and maintaining robustness with noisy supervisors.
本文针对检索增强生成系统中传统重排序器基于静态相关性标签优化与大型语言模型生成精确答案所需实际效用之间的错位问题，提出了一种解决方案。作者引入了重排序偏好优化框架，该框架通过强化学习将重排序建模为序列决策过程，并直接利用大型语言模型对生成质量的反馈进行优化，从而避免了对昂贵人工标注的依赖。在知识密集型基准测试上的实验结果表明，该框架显著优于包括RankZephyr在内的强大基线，进一步分析凸显了其多功能性：能够无缝泛化至不同阅读器、与查询扩展模块正交集成，并在噪声监督下保持鲁棒性。
Reinforcement Learning for Speculative Trading under Exploratory Framework
Authors: Yun Zhao, Alex S. L. Tse, Harry Zheng
First: 2026-04-02T13:41:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T13:41:05+00:00
Comments: 37 pages, 14 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study a speculative trading problem within the exploratory reinforcement learning (RL) framework of Wang et al. [2020]. The problem is formulated as a sequential optimal stopping problem over entry and exit times under general utility function and price process. We first consider a relaxed version of the problem in which the stopping times are modeled by the jump times of Cox processes driven by bounded, non-randomized intensity controls. Under the exploratory formulation, the agent's randomized control is characterized via the probability measure over the jump intensities, and their objective function is regularized by Shannon's differential entropy. This yields a system of the exploratory HJB equations and Gibbs distributions in closed-form as the optimal policy. Error estimates and convergence of the RL objective to the value function of the original problem are established. Finally, an RL algorithm is designed, and its implementation is showcased in a pairs-trading application.
中文标题/摘要
标题：探索性框架下投机交易的强化学习研究
我们在Wang等人[2020]提出的探索性强化学习框架下研究投机交易问题。该问题被表述为在一般效用函数和价格过程下，针对入场与出场时机的序列最优停止问题。首先考虑该问题的松弛版本，其中停止时间由有界、非随机化强度控制驱动的Cox过程跳变时间建模。在探索性框架下，智能体的随机化控制通过跳跃强度上的概率测度表征，其目标函数通过香农微分熵进行正则化处理。由此推导出封闭形式的探索性HJB方程组和吉布斯分布作为最优策略。建立了强化学习目标函数向原问题值函数的误差估计与收敛性证明。最后设计了一种强化学习算法，并通过配对交易案例展示了其实现过程。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the speculative trading problem by framing it as a sequential optimal stopping challenge for entry and exit times, motivated by the need to apply exploratory reinforcement learning to financial decision-making under general utility and price processes. The method involves relaxing the problem to model stopping times via Cox processes with bounded intensity controls, then reformulating it within an exploratory RL framework where randomized control is characterized by probability measures over intensities and regularized by Shannon entropy, leading to a tractable system of exploratory Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman equations and closed-form Gibbs distributions for optimal policy. Key experimental results include establishing error bounds and convergence of the RL objective to the original problem's value function, and demonstrating the algorithm's efficacy through a pairs-trading application with supporting figures.
本文研究投机交易问题，将其构建为针对入场和出场时间的序列最优停止问题，动机在于将探索性强化学习应用于通用效用和价格过程下的金融决策。方法上，首先通过有界强度控制的Cox过程对停止时间建模以放松原问题，然后在探索性强化学习框架中重新表述，其中随机化控制由强度上的概率测度表征并通过香农熵正则化，从而导出了可处理的探索性Hamilton-Jacobi-Bellman方程系统和闭式吉布斯分布作为最优策略。主要实验结果包括建立了强化学习目标向原问题值函数的误差估计与收敛性，并通过配对交易应用展示了算法的有效性，辅以相关图示。
Systematic Analyses of Reinforcement Learning Controllers in Signalized Urban Corridors
Authors: Xiaofei Song, Kerstin Eder, Jonathan Lawry, R. Eddie Wilson
First: 2026-04-02T13:32:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T13:32:52+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this work, we extend our systematic capacity region perspective to multi-junction traffic networks, focussing on the special case of an urban corridor network. In particular, we train and evaluate centralized, fully decentralized, and parameter-sharing decentralized RL controllers, and compare their capacity regions and ATTs together with a classical baseline MaxPressure controller. Further, we show how the parametersharing controller may be generalised to be deployed on a larger network than it was originally trained on. In this setting, we show some initial findings that suggest that even though the junctions are not formally coordinated, traffic may self organise into `green waves'.
中文标题/摘要
标题：信号控制城市走廊中强化学习控制器的系统分析
本研究将系统容量区域视角拓展至多交叉口交通网络，重点关注城市走廊网络这一特例。具体而言，我们训练并评估了集中式、完全分散式及参数共享分散式强化学习控制器，将其容量区域与平均行程时间同经典基准MaxPressure控制器进行对比。进一步，我们展示了参数共享控制器如何推广至比原始训练规模更大的网络进行部署。在此场景下，初步研究发现：即使交叉口未进行形式化协同，交通流仍可能自组织形成‘绿波带’。

Motivated by the need to systematically evaluate traffic control strategies in complex urban networks, this study extends a capacity region analysis to multi-junction corridors, comparing reinforcement learning (RL) controllers against a classical MaxPressure baseline. The method involves training and assessing centralized, fully decentralized, and parameter-sharing decentralized RL controllers, with the parameter-sharing approach further generalized for deployment on larger networks than those used in training. Experimental results reveal that these RL controllers can achieve competitive capacity regions and average travel times (ATTs), and notably, the parameter-sharing decentralized controller exhibits emergent self-organization, facilitating 'green wave' patterns even without formal coordination between junctions.
本研究旨在系统评估复杂城市路网中的交通控制策略，将容量区域分析扩展至多交叉口走廊场景，比较了强化学习控制器与经典MaxPressure基准方法。研究方法包括训练和评估集中式、完全分散式及参数共享分散式强化学习控制器，并将参数共享控制器推广应用于比训练规模更大的路网。实验结果表明，这些强化学习控制器能实现具有竞争力的容量区域和平均行程时间，且参数共享分散式控制器展现出 emergent 自组织特性，即使交叉口间无正式协调，也能促成“绿波”交通模式。
Apriel-Reasoner: RL Post-Training for General-Purpose and Efficient Reasoning
Authors: Rafael Pardinas, Ehsan Kamalloo, David Vazquez, Alexandre Drouin
First: 2026-04-02T13:10:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T13:10:27+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 4 tables, 6 figures, appendix included
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Building general-purpose reasoning models using reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) across diverse domains has been widely adopted by frontier open-weight models. However, their training recipes and domain mixtures are often not disclosed. Joint optimization across domains poses significant challenges: domains vary widely in rollout length, problem difficulty and sample efficiency. Further, models with long chain-of-thought traces increase inference cost and latency, making efficiency critical for practical deployment. We present Apriel-Reasoner, trained with a fully reproducible multi-domain RL post-training recipe on Apriel-Base, a 15B-parameter open-weight LLM, across five domains using public datasets: mathematics, code generation, instruction following, logical puzzles and function calling. We introduce an adaptive domain sampling mechanism that preserves target domain ratios despite heterogeneous rollout dynamics, and a difficulty-aware extension of the standard length penalty that, with no additional training overhead, encourages longer reasoning for difficult problems and shorter traces for easy ones. Trained with a strict 16K-token output budget, Apriel-Reasoner generalizes to 32K tokens at inference and improves over Apriel-Base on AIME 2025, GPQA, MMLU-Pro, and LiveCodeBench while producing 30-50% shorter reasoning traces. It matches strong open-weight models of similar size at lower token cost, thereby pushing the Pareto frontier of accuracy versus token budget.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Apriel-Reasoner：基于强化学习的通用高效推理后训练方法
前沿开源模型广泛采用可验证奖励的强化学习技术构建跨领域通用推理模型，但其训练方案与领域混合策略常未公开。跨领域联合优化面临显著挑战：各领域在推演长度、问题难度与样本效率上差异巨大。此外，长思维链模型会推高推理成本与延迟，使效率成为实际部署的关键。本文提出Apriel-Reasoner，基于15B参数开源模型Apriel-Base，在数学、代码生成、指令跟随、逻辑谜题和函数调用五个公开数据集上，采用完全可复现的多领域强化学习后训练方案。我们引入自适应领域采样机制以保持目标领域比例，并提出无需额外训练开销的难度感知长度惩罚扩展方法，促使模型对难题进行长推理、对简单问题缩短思维链。在严格16K令牌输出预算下训练的Apriel-Reasoner，推理时可泛化至32K令牌，在AIME 2025、GPQA、MMLU-Pro和LiveCodeBench上超越Apriel-Base，同时生成缩短30-50%的推理链。该模型以更低令牌成本匹配同规模强开源模型，从而推进准确率与令牌预算的帕累托前沿。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to address the challenges of building efficient and general-purpose reasoning models via reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), where joint optimization across diverse domains is difficult due to varying rollout lengths, problem difficulty, and sample efficiency, and long reasoning traces increase inference costs. The method introduces Apriel-Reasoner, a 15B-parameter model trained with a reproducible multi-domain RL post-training recipe across five domains using public datasets, featuring an adaptive domain sampling mechanism to handle heterogeneous rollout dynamics and a difficulty-aware length penalty that adjusts reasoning trace length without extra training overhead. The main experimental results show that, trained with a 16K-token output budget, Apriel-Reasoner generalizes to 32K tokens at inference, improves over the base model on benchmarks like AIME 2025 and MMLU-Pro, produces 30-50% shorter reasoning traces, and matches strong open-weight models of similar size at lower token cost, advancing the Pareto frontier of accuracy versus token budget.
本研究的动机在于解决通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）构建高效通用推理模型所面临的挑战，即跨领域联合优化因推理长度、问题难度和样本效率的差异而困难重重，且长推理链会增加推理成本。方法上提出了Apriel-Reasoner，这是一个基于15B参数开源模型、使用公开数据集在五个领域进行可复现多领域RL后训练的模型，采用了自适应领域采样机制以处理异构的推理动态，以及一种难度感知的长度惩罚方法，可在无额外训练开销下根据问题难度调整推理链长度。主要实验结果表明，在16K令牌输出预算下训练后，Apriel-Reasoner在推理时能泛化至32K令牌，在AIME 2025和MMLU-Pro等基准测试上超越了基础模型，同时生成短30-50%的推理链，并以更低的令牌成本匹配了同类规模的开源模型，从而推进了准确性与令牌预算的帕累托前沿。
ProCeedRL: Process Critic with Exploratory Demonstration Reinforcement Learning for LLM Agentic Reasoning
Authors: Jingyue Gao, Yanjiang Guo, Xiaoshuai Chen, Jianyu Chen
First: 2026-04-02T13:10:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T13:10:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) significantly enhances the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs), yet applying it to multi-turn agentic tasks remains challenging due to the long-horizon nature of interactions and the stochasticity of environmental feedback. We identify a structural failure mode in agentic exploration: suboptimal actions elicit noisy observations into misleading contexts, which further weaken subsequent decision-making, making recovery increasingly difficult. This cumulative feedback loop of errors renders standard exploration strategies ineffective and susceptible to the model's reasoning and the environment's randomness. To mitigate this issue, we propose ProCeedRL: Process Critic with Explorative Demonstration RL, shifting exploration from passive selection to active intervention. ProCeedRL employs a process-level critic to monitor interactions in real time, incorporating reflection-based demonstrations to guide agents in stopping the accumulation of errors. We find that this approach significantly exceeds the model's saturated exploration performance, demonstrating substantial exploratory benefits. By learning from exploratory demonstrations and on-policy samples, ProCeedRL significantly improves exploration efficiency and achieves superior performance on complex deep search and embodied tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ProCeedRL：面向大语言模型智能体推理的流程评判与探索性演示强化学习
强化学习（RL）显著提升了大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但由于交互的长时程特性与环境反馈的随机性，将其应用于多轮智能体任务仍具挑战。我们识别出智能体探索中的结构性失效模式：次优动作会引入噪声观测形成误导性语境，进一步削弱后续决策能力，使状态恢复愈发困难。这种错误的累积反馈循环导致标准探索策略失效，且易受模型推理与环境随机性的影响。为缓解此问题，我们提出ProCeedRL：流程评判与探索性演示强化学习，将探索从被动选择转向主动干预。ProCeedRL采用流程级评判器实时监控交互，结合基于反思的演示来引导智能体终止错误累积。实验表明该方法显著超越模型的饱和探索性能，展现出实质性的探索优势。通过从探索性演示和同策略样本中学习，ProCeedRL大幅提升探索效率，并在复杂深度搜索与具身任务中取得卓越性能。

The motivation for this work is to address the challenge of applying reinforcement learning to multi-turn agentic tasks with large language models, where long-horizon interactions and stochastic environmental feedback lead to a structural failure mode: suboptimal actions create misleading contexts that degrade subsequent decisions, making recovery difficult. The method proposed, ProCeedRL, shifts exploration from passive selection to active intervention by employing a process-level critic to monitor interactions in real time and incorporating reflection-based demonstrations to guide agents in halting error accumulation. Experimental results show that this approach significantly surpasses the model's saturated exploration performance, improving exploration efficiency and achieving superior outcomes on complex deep search and embodied tasks.
本研究的动机在于解决将强化学习应用于大型语言模型的多轮代理任务时所面临的挑战，这些任务因长时程交互和环境反馈的随机性而存在结构性失效模式：次优行动会产生误导性上下文，削弱后续决策，使恢复变得困难。所提出的方法ProCeedRL将探索从被动选择转向主动干预，通过采用过程级批评器实时监控交互，并结合基于反思的演示来引导代理停止错误累积。实验结果表明，该方法显著超越了模型的饱和探索性能，提高了探索效率，并在复杂的深度搜索和具身任务上实现了优越的性能。
MemFactory: Unified Inference & Training Framework for Agent Memory
Authors: Ziliang Guo, Ziheng Li, Bo Tang, Feiyu Xiong, Zhiyu Li
First: 2026-03-31T09:38:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T12:20:29+00:00
Comments: v3:fixed Figure 1 typos, clarified ambiguous wording in the abstract, added 1 missing citation, Code: https://github.com/Valsure/MemFactory
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Memory-augmented Large Language Models (LLMs) are essential for developing capable, long-term AI agents. Recently, applying Reinforcement Learning (RL) to optimize memory operations, such as extraction, updating, and retrieval, has emerged as a highly promising research direction. However, existing implementations remain highly fragmented and task-specific, lacking a unified infrastructure to streamline the integration, training, and evaluation of these complex pipelines. To address this gap, we present MemFactory, the first unified, highly modular training and inference framework specifically designed for memory-augmented agents. Inspired by the success of unified fine-tuning frameworks like LLaMA-Factory, MemFactory abstracts the memory lifecycle into atomic, plug-and-play components, enabling researchers to seamlessly construct custom memory agents via a "Lego-like" architecture. Furthermore, the framework natively integrates Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to fine-tune internal memory management policies driven by multi-dimensional environmental rewards. MemFactory provides out-of-the-box support for recent cutting-edge paradigms, including Memory-R1, RMM, and MemAgent. We empirically validate MemFactory on the open-source MemAgent architecture using its publicly available training and evaluation data. Across the evaluation sets, MemFactory improves performance over the corresponding base models on average, with relative gains of up to 14.8%. By providing a standardized, extensible, and easy-to-use infrastructure, MemFactory significantly lowers the barrier to entry, paving the way for future innovations in memory-driven AI agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MemFactory：面向智能体记忆的统一推理与训练框架
记忆增强型大语言模型是开发具备长期能力的AI智能体的关键。近期，运用强化学习优化记忆操作（如提取、更新与检索）已成为极具前景的研究方向。然而现有实现方案高度碎片化且局限于特定任务，缺乏统一的基础设施来整合、训练与评估这些复杂流程。为填补这一空白，我们推出MemFactory——首个专为记忆增强型智能体设计的统一化、高模块化训练与推理框架。受LLaMA-Factory等统一微调框架的启发，MemFactory将记忆生命周期抽象为原子化即插即用组件，使研究者能通过“乐高式”架构无缝构建定制化记忆智能体。该框架原生集成群体相对策略优化方法，可通过多维环境奖励驱动内部记忆管理策略的微调。MemFactory为Memory-R1、RMM、MemAgent等前沿范式提供开箱即用支持。我们在开源MemAgent架构上使用其公开训练与评估数据进行了实证验证：在全部评估集中，MemFactory相较基线模型平均性能提升最高达14.8%。通过提供标准化、可扩展、易用的基础设施，MemFactory显著降低了研究门槛，为记忆驱动型AI智能体的未来创新铺平道路。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces MemFactory, a unified framework motivated by the need to streamline the fragmented development of memory-augmented LLM agents, which use reinforcement learning to optimize memory operations. The method abstracts the memory lifecycle into modular components, allowing flexible agent construction, and integrates Group Relative Policy Optimization for training memory policies with environmental rewards. Experimental validation on the MemAgent architecture shows average performance improvements over base models, with relative gains up to 14.8%, demonstrating its effectiveness in enhancing agent capabilities.
本文提出了MemFactory框架，其动机在于解决当前基于强化学习优化记忆操作（如提取、更新和检索）的记忆增强大语言模型代理开发中存在碎片化、缺乏统一基础设施的问题。该方法将记忆生命周期抽象为模块化组件，支持通过类似积木的结构灵活构建定制代理，并集成了群体相对策略优化来利用多维环境奖励训练内部记忆管理策略。在MemAgent架构上的实验验证表明，该框架相比基础模型平均性能有所提升，相对增益最高达14.8%，有效提升了代理能力。
MOON3.0: Reasoning-aware Multimodal Representation Learning for E-commerce Product Understanding
Authors: Junxian Wu, Chenghan Fu, Zhanheng Nie, Daoze Zhang, Bowen Wan, Wanxian Guan, Chuan Yu, Jian Xu, Bo Zheng
First: 2026-04-01T05:55:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T12:17:15+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the rapid growth of e-commerce, exploring general representations rather than task-specific ones has attracted increasing attention. Although recent multimodal large language models (MLLMs) have driven significant progress in product understanding, they are typically employed as feature extractors that implicitly encode product information into global embeddings, thereby limiting their ability to capture fine-grained attributes. Therefore, we argue that leveraging the reasoning capabilities of MLLMs to explicitly model fine-grained product attributes holds significant potential. Nevertheless, achieving this goal remains non-trivial due to several key challenges: (i) long-context reasoning tends to dilute the model's attention to salient information in the raw input; (ii) supervised fine-tuning (SFT) primarily encourages rigid imitation, limiting the exploration of effective reasoning strategies; and (iii) fine-grained details are progressively attenuated during forward propagation. To address these issues, we propose MOON3.0, the first reasoning-aware MLLM-based model for product representation learning. Our method (1) employs a multi-head modality fusion module to adaptively integrate raw signals; (2) incorporates a joint contrastive and reinforcement learning framework to autonomously explore more effective reasoning strategies; and (3) introduces a fine-grained residual enhancement module to progressively preserve local details throughout the network. Additionally, we release a large-scale multimodal e-commerce benchmark MBE3.0. Experimentally, our model demonstrates state-of-the-art zero-shot performance across various downstream tasks on both our benchmark and public datasets.

标题：MOON3.0：面向电商产品理解的推理感知多模态表征学习
随着电子商务的快速发展，探索通用表征而非任务特定表征日益受到关注。尽管近期多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）在商品理解方面取得了显著进展，但它们通常被用作特征提取器，将商品信息隐式编码为全局嵌入，从而限制了捕捉细粒度属性的能力。因此，我们认为利用MLLMs的推理能力显式建模细粒度商品属性具有重要潜力。然而，实现这一目标仍面临关键挑战：（i）长上下文推理易稀释模型对原始输入显著信息的注意力；（ii）监督微调（SFT）主要鼓励机械模仿，限制了有效推理策略的探索；（iii）细粒度细节在前向传播过程中逐渐衰减。为解决这些问题，我们提出了MOON3.0——首个基于MLLM的推理感知商品表征学习模型。我们的方法（1）采用多头模态融合模块自适应整合原始信号；（2）结合联合对比与强化学习框架自主探索更有效的推理策略；（3）引入细粒度残差增强模块，在网络中渐进式保留局部细节。此外，我们发布了大规模多模态电商基准MBE3.0。实验表明，该模型在我们的基准及公共数据集的各种下游任务中均实现了最先进的零样本性能。

Predicting LLM Output Length via Entropy-Guided Representations
Authors: Huanyi Xie, Yubin Chen, Liangyu Wang, Lijie Hu, Di Wang
First: 2026-02-12T10:49:04+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T12:15:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The long-tailed distribution of sequence lengths in LLM serving and reinforcement learning (RL) sampling causes significant computational waste due to excessive padding in batched inference. Existing methods rely on auxiliary models for static length prediction, but they incur high overhead, generalize poorly, and fail in stochastic "one-to-many" sampling scenarios. We introduce a lightweight framework that reuses the main model's internal hidden states for efficient length prediction. Our framework features two core components: 1) Entropy-Guided Token Pooling (EGTP), which uses on-the-fly activations and token entropy for highly accurate static prediction with negligible cost, and 2) Progressive Length Prediction (PLP), which dynamically estimates the remaining length at each decoding step to handle stochastic generation. To validate our approach, we build and release ForeLen, a comprehensive benchmark with long-sequence, Chain-of-Thought, and RL data. On ForeLen, EGTP achieves state-of-the-art accuracy, reducing MAE by 29.16\% over the best baseline. Integrating our methods with a length-aware scheduler yields significant end-to-end throughput gains. Our work provides a new technical and evaluation baseline for efficient LLM inference.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于熵引导表征的大语言模型输出长度预测
大语言模型服务与强化学习采样中的序列长度长尾分布，因批处理推理中过度填充导致显著计算浪费。现有方法依赖辅助模型进行静态长度预测，但存在开销大、泛化性差、无法适应随机'一对多'采样场景等问题。我们提出一种轻量级框架，复用主模型内部隐藏状态实现高效长度预测。该框架包含两个核心组件：1）熵引导词元池化（EGTP），利用实时激活值与词元熵实现高精度静态预测且成本可忽略；2）渐进式长度预测（PLP），在解码步骤中动态估计剩余长度以处理随机生成。为验证方法，我们构建并开源了包含长序列、思维链和强化学习数据的综合基准测试集ForeLen。在ForeLen上，EGTP达到最优精度，较最佳基线平均绝对误差降低29.16%。将本方法与长度感知调度器结合，可实现显著的端到端吞吐量提升。本研究为高效大语言模型推理提供了新的技术与评估基准。

This work is motivated by the computational inefficiency caused by the long-tailed distribution of sequence lengths in batched LLM inference and reinforcement learning sampling, where excessive padding leads to waste. To address the high overhead and poor generalization of existing auxiliary models, the authors propose a lightweight framework that reuses the model's internal hidden states, featuring Entropy-Guided Token Pooling (EGTP) for accurate static prediction and Progressive Length Prediction (PLP) for dynamic estimation in stochastic generation. Experimental results on the newly introduced ForeLen benchmark show that EGTP reduces mean absolute error by 29.16% compared to the best baseline, and integration with a length-aware scheduler yields significant throughput improvements, establishing a new baseline for efficient LLM inference.

Captioning Daily Activity Images in Early Childhood Education: Benchmark and Algorithm
Authors: Sixing Li, Zhibin Gu, Ziqi Zhang, Weiguo Pan, Bing Li, Ying Wang, Hongzhe Liu
First: 2026-04-02T12:01:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T12:01:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Image captioning for Early Childhood Education (ECE) is essential for automated activity understanding and educational assessment. However, existing methods face two key challenges. First, the lack of large-scale, domain-specific datasets limits the model's ability to capture fine-grained semantic concepts unique to ECE scenarios, resulting in generic and imprecise descriptions. Second, conventional training paradigms exhibit limitations in enhancing professional object description capability, as supervised learning tends to favor high-frequency expressions, while reinforcement learning may suffer from unstable optimization on difficult samples. To address these limitations, we introduce ECAC, a large-scale benchmark for ECE daily activity image captioning, comprising 256,121 real-world images annotated with expert-level captions and fine-grained labels. ECAC is further equipped with a domain-oriented evaluation protocol, the Teaching Toy Recognition Score (TTS), to explicitly measure professional object naming accuracy. Furthermore, we propose RSRS (Reward-Conditional Switch of Reinforcement Learning and Supervised Fine-Tuning), a hybrid training framework that dynamically alternates between RL and supervised optimization. By rerouting hard samples with zero rewards to supervised fine-tuning, RSRS effectively mitigates advantage collapse and enables stable optimization for fine-grained recognition. Leveraging ECAC and RSRS, we develop KinderMM-Cap-3B, a domain-adapted multimodal large language model. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our model achieves a TTS of 51.06, substantially outperforming state-of-the-art baselines while maintaining superior caption quality, highlighting its potential for specialized educational applications.

The Rank and Gradient Lost in Non-stationarity: Sample Weight Decay for Mitigating Plasticity Loss in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zihao Wu, Hongyao Tang, Yi Ma, Jiashun Liu, Yan Zheng, Jianye Hao
Venue: ICLR
First: 2026-04-02T11:29:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T11:29:46+00:00
Comments: ICLR
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep reinforcement learning (RL) suffers from plasticity loss severely due to the nature of non-stationarity, which impairs the ability to adapt to new data and learn continually. Unfortunately, our understanding of how plasticity loss arises, dissipates, and can be dissolved remains limited to empirical findings, leaving the theoretical end underexplored.To address this gap, we study the plasticity loss problem from the theoretical perspective of network optimization. By formally characterizing the two culprit factors in online RL process: the non-stationarity of data distributions and the non-stationarity of targets induced by bootstrapping, our theory attributes the loss of plasticity to two mechanisms: the rank collapse of the Neural Tangent Kernel (NTK) Gram matrix and the $Θ(\frac{1}{k})$ decay of gradient magnitude. The first mechanism echoes prior empirical findings from the theoretical perspective and sheds light on the effects of existing methods, e.g., network reset, neuron recycle, and noise injection. Against this backdrop, we focus primarily on the second mechanism and aim to alleviate plasticity loss by addressing the gradient attenuation issue, which is orthogonal to existing methods. We propose Sample Weight Decay -- a lightweight method to restore gradient magnitude, as a general remedy to plasticity loss for deep RL methods based on experience replay. In experiments, we evaluate the efficacy of \methodName upon TD3, \myadded{Double DQN} and SAC with SimBa architecture in MuJoCo, \myadded{ALE} and DeepMind Control Suite tasks. The results demonstrate that \methodName effectively alleviates plasticity loss and consistently improves learning performance across various configurations of deep RL algorithms, UTD, network architectures, and environments, achieving SOTA performance on challenging DMC Humanoid tasks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非平稳性中的秩与梯度衰减：缓解强化学习中可塑性损失的样本权重衰减方法
深度强化学习（RL）因非平稳性本质而严重遭受可塑性损失，削弱了适应新数据与持续学习的能力。现有对可塑性损失产生、消散及消除机制的理解多局限于实证研究，理论层面探索不足。为填补这一空白，我们从网络优化的理论视角研究可塑性损失问题。通过形式化分析在线RL过程中的两个关键因素——数据分布的非平稳性与自举目标值的非平稳性，我们的理论将可塑性损失归因于两种机制：神经正切核（NTK）格拉姆矩阵的秩崩溃，以及梯度幅值的$Θ(\frac{1}{k})$衰减。第一种机制从理论角度呼应了先前的实证发现，并揭示了现有方法（如网络重置、神经元回收和噪声注入）的作用机制。在此背景下，我们主要聚焦第二种机制，旨在通过解决梯度衰减问题（与现有方法正交）来缓解可塑性损失。我们提出样本权重衰减——一种恢复梯度幅值的轻量级方法，作为基于经验回放的深度RL方法应对可塑性损失的通用解决方案。实验中，我们在MuJoCo、ALE及DeepMind Control Suite任务中，结合SimBa架构对TD3、Double DQN和SAC算法评估了该方法的有效性。结果表明，该方法能有效缓解可塑性损失，并在不同深度RL算法配置、UTD参数、网络架构和环境中持续提升学习性能，在具有挑战性的DMC Humanoid任务中达到了最先进水平。
