This paper investigates the problem of plasticity loss in deep reinforcement learning, where non-stationary data and bootstrapped targets impair an agent's ability to learn continually. The authors theoretically attribute this loss to two mechanisms: the rank collapse of the Neural Tangent Kernel Gram matrix and the decay of gradient magnitude. To address the gradient attenuation issue, they propose Sample Weight Decay, a lightweight method applied with experience replay. Experimental results on TD3, Double DQN, and SAC across MuJoCo, ALE, and DeepMind Control Suite tasks show that the method effectively mitigates plasticity loss and improves learning performance, achieving state-of-the-art results on challenging DMC Humanoid tasks.
本文研究了深度强化学习中因数据分布和目标函数的非平稳性导致的塑性丧失问题。作者从网络优化的理论视角出发，将塑性丧失归因于神经正切核格拉姆矩阵的秩崩溃和梯度幅值的衰减两种机制。针对梯度衰减问题，他们提出了一种轻量级的样本权重衰减方法，可与经验回放结合使用。在TD3、Double DQN和SAC算法上，于MuJoCo、ALE和DeepMind Control Suite环境中的实验结果表明，该方法有效缓解了塑性丧失，提升了学习性能，并在具有挑战性的DMC Humanoid任务上达到了最先进的水平。
When does learning pay off? A study on DRL-based dynamic algorithm configuration for carbon-aware scheduling
Authors: Andrea Mencaroni, Robbert Reijnen, Yingqian Zhang, Dieter Claeys
First: 2026-04-02T10:47:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T10:47:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep reinforcement learning (DRL) has recently emerged as a promising tool for Dynamic Algorithm Configuration (DAC), enabling evolutionary algorithms to adapt their parameters online rather than relying on static tuned configurations. While DRL can learn effective control policies, training is computationally expensive. This cost may be justified if learned policies generalize, allowing the training effort to transfer across instance types and problem scales. Yet, for real-world optimization problems, it remains unclear whether this promise holds in practice and under which conditions the investment in learning pays off. In this work, we investigate this question in the context of the carbon-aware permutation flow-shop scheduling problem. We develop a DRL-based DAC framework and train it exclusively on small, simple instances. We then deploy the learned policy on both similar and more complex unseen instances and compare its performance against a static tuned baseline, which provides a fair point of comparison. Our findings show that the proposed method provides a strong dynamic algorithm control policy that can be effectively transferred to different unseen problem instances. Notably, on simple and cheap to compute instances, similar to those observed during training and tuning, DRL performs comparably with the statically tuned baseline. However, as instance characteristics diverge and computational complexities increase, the DRL-learned policy continuously outperforms static tuning. These results confirm that DRL can acquire robust and generalizable control policies which are effective beyond the training instance distributions. This ability to generalize across instance types makes the initial computational investment worthwhile, particularly in settings where static tuning struggles to adapt to changing problem scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习何时产生回报？基于深度强化学习的碳感知调度动态算法配置研究
深度强化学习（DRL）近年来已成为动态算法配置（DAC）的有力工具，使进化算法能够在线调整参数，而非依赖静态调优配置。尽管DRL能习得有效的控制策略，但其训练过程计算成本高昂。若习得策略具备泛化能力，使训练成果能迁移至不同实例类型和问题规模，则此成本或可被证明合理。然而，对于现实世界优化问题，这种潜力是否在实践中成立、以及学习投资在何种条件下能产生回报，仍不明确。本研究以碳感知置换流水车间调度问题为背景探讨该问题。我们开发了基于DRL的DAC框架，并仅使用小型简单实例进行训练，随后将习得策略部署于相似及更复杂的未见实例，并与静态调优基线进行性能对比（该基线提供了公平的比较基准）。研究结果表明：所提方法能生成强健的动态算法控制策略，可有效迁移至不同的未见问题实例。值得注意的是，在简单且计算成本低的实例（与训练和调优阶段观察到的实例相似）上，DRL表现与静态调优基线相当；但随着实例特征差异增大和计算复杂度提升，DRL习得策略持续优于静态调优。这些结果证实DRL能够获得强健且可泛化的控制策略，其有效性超越训练实例分布。这种跨实例类型的泛化能力使得初始计算投资具有价值，尤其在静态调优难以适应动态问题场景的情境中。
Summary / 总结
This study investigates whether the computational cost of training deep reinforcement learning (DRL) for dynamic algorithm configuration (DAC) is justified by the generalization of learned policies to unseen problem instances, focusing on carbon-aware permutation flow-shop scheduling. The method involves developing a DRL-based DAC framework trained exclusively on small, simple instances and deploying it on both similar and more complex unseen instances, with performance compared against a statically tuned baseline. Experimental results show that the DRL-learned policy performs comparably to the baseline on instances similar to training data but continuously outperforms it as instance characteristics diverge and computational complexity increases, confirming that DRL can acquire robust, generalizable control policies that make the initial training investment worthwhile, especially where static tuning struggles to adapt.
本研究探讨了为动态算法配置（DAC）训练深度强化学习（DRL）的计算成本是否因学习策略对未见问题实例的泛化能力而合理，聚焦于碳感知置换流水车间调度问题。方法上，开发了一个基于DRL的DAC框架，仅在小规模简单实例上训练，并将其部署到相似和更复杂的未见实例上，与静态调优基线进行性能比较。实验结果表明，在类似训练数据的实例上，DRL学习策略与基线表现相当，但随着实例特征差异增大和计算复杂度提高，其性能持续优于静态调优，证实了DRL能够获得鲁棒且可泛化的控制策略，这使得初始训练投入物有所值，特别是在静态调优难以适应变化问题场景的情况下。
Constraint-Aware Reinforcement Learning via Adaptive Action Scaling
Authors: Murad Dawood, Usama Ahmed Siddiquie, Shahram Khorshidi, Maren Bennewitz
First: 2025-10-13T14:59:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T10:40:14+00:00
Comments: Accepted in 8th Annual Learning for Dynamics & Control Conference (L4DC)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safe reinforcement learning (RL) seeks to mitigate unsafe behaviors that arise from exploration during training by reducing constraint violations while maintaining task performance. Existing approaches typically rely on a single policy to jointly optimize reward and safety, which can cause instability due to conflicting objectives, or they use external safety filters that override actions and require prior system knowledge. In this paper, we propose a modular cost-aware regulator that scales the agent's actions based on predicted constraint violations, preserving exploration through smooth action modulation rather than overriding the policy. The regulator is trained to minimize constraint violations while avoiding degenerate suppression of actions. Our approach integrates seamlessly with off-policy RL methods such as SAC and TD3, and achieves state-of-the-art return-to-cost ratios on Safety Gym locomotion tasks with sparse costs, reducing constraint violations by up to 126 times while increasing returns by over an order of magnitude compared to prior methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自适应动作缩放的约束感知强化学习
安全强化学习旨在通过减少约束违反同时保持任务性能，以缓解训练期间探索引发的不安全行为。现有方法通常依赖单一策略联合优化奖励与安全性，可能因目标冲突导致不稳定，或使用需先验系统知识且会覆盖动作的外部安全过滤器。本文提出一种模块化的成本感知调节器，基于预测的约束违反缩放智能体动作，通过平滑的动作调制而非策略覆盖来保持探索性。该调节器经训练以最小化约束违反，同时避免动作的退化抑制。本方法可无缝集成SAC、TD3等离策略强化学习方法，并在稀疏成本的Safety Gym运动任务上实现了最优的回报-成本比，与先前方法相比，约束违反减少高达126倍，回报提升超过一个数量级。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of safe reinforcement learning, where traditional methods often suffer from instability due to conflicting reward and safety objectives or rely on external safety filters that require prior knowledge. The authors propose a modular cost-aware regulator that adaptively scales the agent's actions based on predicted constraint violations, enabling smooth action modulation to preserve exploration without overriding the policy. Experimental results on Safety Gym locomotion tasks with sparse costs show that the method achieves state-of-the-art return-to-cost ratios, reducing constraint violations by up to 126 times and increasing returns by over an order of magnitude compared to prior approaches, while integrating seamlessly with off-policy RL algorithms like SAC and TD3.
本文针对安全强化学习中的挑战，即传统方法常因奖励与安全目标冲突导致不稳定，或依赖需要先验知识的外部安全过滤器。作者提出了一种模块化的成本感知调节器，根据预测的约束违规自适应缩放智能体的动作，通过平滑的动作调制保持探索性而不覆盖策略。在具有稀疏成本的Safety Gym运动任务上的实验结果表明，该方法实现了最先进的回报-成本比，与先前方法相比，将约束违规减少了高达126倍，并将回报提高了一个数量级以上，同时能与SAC和TD3等离策略强化学习算法无缝集成。
Reinforcement Learning-based Task Offloading in the Internet of Wearable Things
Authors: Waleed Bin Qaim, Aleksandr Ometov, Claudia Campolo, Antonella Molinaro, Elena Simona Lohan, Jari Nurmi
First: 2025-10-08T19:36:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T10:01:22+00:00
Comments: Withdrawn by the authors. A revised version is under preparation
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Over the years, significant contributions have been made by the research and industrial sectors to improve wearable devices towards the Internet of Wearable Things (IoWT) paradigm. However, wearables are still facing several challenges. Many stem from the limited battery power and insufficient computation resources available on wearable devices. On the other hand, with the popularity of smart wearables, there is a consistent increase in the development of new computationally intensive and latency-critical applications. In such a context, task offloading allows wearables to leverage the resources available on nearby edge devices to enhance the overall user experience. This paper proposes a framework for Reinforcement Learning (RL)-based task offloading in the IoWT. We formulate the task offloading process considering the tradeoff between energy consumption and task accomplishment time. Moreover, we model the task offloading problem as a Markov Decision Process (MDP) and utilize the Q-learning technique to enable the wearable device to make optimal task offloading decisions without prior knowledge. We evaluate the performance of the proposed framework through extensive simulations for various applications and system configurations conducted in the ns-3 network simulator. We also show how varying the main system parameters of the Q-learning algorithm affects the overall performance in terms of average task accomplishment time, average energy consumption, and percentage of tasks offloaded.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的可穿戴物联网任务卸载框架
多年来，研究与工业界为推进可穿戴设备向可穿戴物联网（IoWT）范式发展做出了重要贡献。然而，可穿戴设备仍面临诸多挑战，主要源于其有限的电池续航与计算资源。与此同时，随着智能可穿戴设备的普及，对计算密集且延迟敏感的新型应用需求持续增长。在此背景下，任务卸载技术使可穿戴设备能够利用邻近边缘设备的资源以提升整体用户体验。本文提出了一种基于强化学习（RL）的IoWT任务卸载框架，通过权衡能耗与任务完成时间来构建卸载流程，并将该问题建模为马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），利用Q学习技术使可穿戴设备能在无先验知识的情况下做出最优卸载决策。通过在ns-3网络模拟器中针对多种应用与系统配置进行广泛仿真，评估了所提框架的性能，并分析了Q学习算法关键参数对平均任务完成时间、平均能耗及任务卸载比例的整体影响。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limited battery and computational resources of wearable devices in the Internet of Wearable Things (IoWT) and the growing demand for latency-sensitive applications, this paper proposes a reinforcement learning-based framework for task offloading. The method formulates the offloading process as a Markov Decision Process (MDP) that balances energy consumption and task completion time, and employs Q-learning to enable devices to make optimal offloading decisions autonomously. Experimental simulations in the ns-3 network simulator demonstrate the framework's performance across various applications and configurations, analyzing the impact of Q-learning parameters on average task time, energy consumption, and offloading rates.
本文针对可穿戴设备在物联网可穿戴设备（IoWT）中电池和计算资源有限，以及对延迟敏感应用需求增长的问题，提出了一种基于强化学习的任务卸载框架。该方法将卸载过程建模为权衡能耗与任务完成时间的马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），并利用Q学习使设备能够自主做出最优卸载决策。通过在ns-3网络模拟器中对多种应用和配置进行广泛仿真，实验评估了该框架的性能，分析了Q学习主要参数对平均任务时间、平均能耗和任务卸载百分比的影响。
Not All Tokens See Equally: Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization for Large Vision-Language Models
Authors: Zekai Ye, Qiming Li, Xiaocheng Feng, Ruihan Chen, Ziming Li, Haoyu Ren, Kun Chen, Dandan Tu, Bing Qin
First: 2026-04-02T09:53:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T09:53:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
While Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has advanced reasoning in Large Vision-Language Models (LVLMs), prevailing frameworks suffer from a foundational methodological flaw: by distributing identical advantages across all generated tokens, these methods inherently dilute the learning signals essential for optimizing the critical, visually-grounded steps of multimodal reasoning. To bridge this gap, we formulate \textit{Token Visual Dependency}, quantifying the causal information gain of visual inputs via the Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence between visual-conditioned and text-only predictive distributions. Revealing that this dependency is highly sparse and semantically pivotal, we introduce Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization (PGPO), which is a novel fine-grained credit assignment framework that dynamically reshapes advantages at the token level. Through a threshold-gated, mass-conserving mechanism, PGPO actively amplifies learning signals for visually-dependent tokens while suppressing gradient noise from linguistic priors. Extensive experiments based on the Qwen2.5-VL series across seven challenging multimodal reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PGPO boosts models by 18.7% on average. Both theoretical and empirical analyses confirm that PGPO effectively reduces gradient variance, prevents training collapse, and acts as a potent regularizer for robust, perception-grounded multimodal reasoning. Code will be published on https://github.com/Yzk1114/PGPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：并非所有词元皆平等：面向大型视觉语言模型的感知驱动策略优化
尽管基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）推动了大型视觉语言模型（LVLM）的推理能力发展，但现有框架存在根本性方法缺陷：通过为所有生成词元分配相同的优势值，这些方法本质上稀释了优化多模态推理关键视觉步骤所需的学习信号。为弥补这一差距，我们提出“词元视觉依赖性”概念，通过视觉条件预测分布与纯文本预测分布间的KL散度量化视觉输入的因果信息增益。研究发现该依赖性具有高度稀疏性和语义关键性，据此我们提出感知驱动策略优化（PGPO）——一种细粒度信用分配框架，可在词元层面动态重塑优势值。通过阈值门控的质量守恒机制，PGPO主动增强视觉依赖词元的学习信号，同时抑制语言先验带来的梯度噪声。基于Qwen2.5-VL系列模型在七个挑战性多模态推理基准上的大量实验表明，PGPO平均提升模型性能18.7%。理论与实证分析均证实，PGPO能有效降低梯度方差、防止训练崩溃，并作为强正则化器促进鲁棒的感知驱动多模态推理。代码将发布于https://github.com/Yzk1114/PGPO。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the flaw in existing Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) frameworks that distribute identical advantages across all tokens, diluting learning signals for visually-grounded reasoning, this paper introduces Perception-Grounded Policy Optimization (PGPO). The method quantifies Token Visual Dependency via KL divergence to identify sparse, critical visual tokens and employs a threshold-gated mechanism to dynamically reshape token-level advantages, amplifying signals for visually-dependent tokens while suppressing noise from linguistic priors. Experimental results on the Qwen2.5-VL series across seven benchmarks show an average performance boost of 18.7%, with analyses confirming reduced gradient variance, prevention of training collapse, and robust perception-grounded reasoning.
针对现有基于可验证奖励的强化学习框架对所有令牌分配相同优势、从而稀释视觉推理关键学习信号的方法缺陷，本文提出了感知驱动的策略优化方法。该方法通过KL散度量化令牌视觉依赖性，识别稀疏但关键的视觉令牌，并采用阈值门控机制动态重塑令牌级优势，增强视觉依赖令牌的学习信号，同时抑制语言先验的梯度噪声。在Qwen2.5-VL系列模型上的七个多模态推理基准测试表明，平均性能提升18.7%，分析证实该方法有效降低了梯度方差，防止训练崩溃，并作为正则化器促进了鲁棒的感知驱动多模态推理。
Physics Informed Reinforcement Learning with Gibbs Priors for Topology Control in Power Grids
Authors: Pantelis Dogoulis, Maxime Cordy
First: 2026-04-02T09:45:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T09:45:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Topology control for power grid operation is a challenging sequential decision making problem because the action space grows combinatorially with the size of the grid and action evaluation through simulation is computationally expensive. We propose a physics-informed Reinforcement Learning framework that combines semi-Markov control with a Gibbs prior, that encodes the system's physics, over the action space. The decision is only taken when the grid enters a hazardous regime, while a graph neural network surrogate predicts the post action overload risk of feasible topology actions. These predictions are used to construct a physics-informed Gibbs prior that both selects a small state-dependent candidate set and reweights policy logits before action selection. In this way, our method reduces exploration difficulty and online simulation cost while preserving the flexibility of a learned policy. We evaluate the approach in three realistic benchmark environments of increasing difficulty. Across all settings, the proposed method achieves a strong balance between control quality and computational efficiency: it matches oracle-level performance while being approximately $6\times$ faster on the first benchmark, reaches $94.6\%$ of oracle reward with roughly $200\times$ lower decision time on the second one, and on the most challenging benchmark improves over a PPO baseline by up to $255\%$ in reward and $284\%$ in survived steps while remaining about $2.5\times$ faster than a strong specialized engineering baseline. These results show that our method provides an effective mechanism for topology control in power grids.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于吉布斯先验的物理信息强化学习在电网拓扑控制中的应用
电网运行中的拓扑控制是一个具有挑战性的序贯决策问题，其动作空间随电网规模组合增长，且通过仿真评估动作的计算成本高昂。本文提出一种物理信息强化学习框架，将半马尔可夫控制与吉布斯先验相结合，该先验在动作空间编码了系统物理规律。仅当电网进入危险状态时才触发决策，同时通过图神经网络代理模型预测可行拓扑动作的后置过载风险。这些预测用于构建物理信息吉布斯先验，既筛选出小型状态相关候选动作集，又在动作选择前重新调整策略对数概率。该方法在保持学习策略灵活性的同时，降低了探索难度与在线仿真成本。我们在三个难度递增的真实基准环境中评估该方法。所有实验表明，所提方法在控制质量与计算效率间取得优异平衡：在首个基准中匹配理想性能且提速约6倍；在第二个基准中获得94.6%的理想奖励且决策时间降低约200倍；在最复杂的基准中，相比PPO基线奖励提升达255%，存活步数增加284%，同时比专业工程基线快约2.5倍。这些结果证明该方法为电网拓扑控制提供了高效机制。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the computationally expensive and combinatorially complex problem of power grid topology control by proposing a physics-informed reinforcement learning framework that integrates semi-Markov control with a Gibbs prior to encode system physics. The method triggers decisions only during hazardous grid regimes, using a graph neural network surrogate to predict post-action overload risks, which then informs a Gibbs prior to narrow down action candidates and reweight policy logits, thereby reducing exploration difficulty and simulation costs. Experimental results across three increasingly difficult benchmark environments demonstrate that the approach balances control quality and efficiency, matching or exceeding oracle performance while being significantly faster, with improvements of up to 255% in reward and 284% in survival steps over baseline methods.
该论文针对电网拓扑控制中计算成本高、组合复杂度大的问题，提出了一种物理信息强化学习框架，结合半马尔可夫控制与吉布斯先验来编码系统物理规律。该方法仅在电网进入危险状态时触发决策，利用图神经网络代理预测可行拓扑动作后的过载风险，进而构建物理信息吉布斯先验以缩小动作候选集并重新加权策略对数，从而降低探索难度和仿真成本。在三个难度递增的基准环境中的实验结果表明，该方法在控制质量与效率之间取得了良好平衡，性能达到或接近理论最优水平，同时速度显著提升，相比基线方法在奖励和生存步数上最高分别提升了255%和284%。
Computationally efficient Gauss-Newton reinforcement learning for model predictive control
Authors: Dean Brandner, Sebastien Gros, Sergio Lucia
First: 2025-08-04T14:00:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T09:41:05+00:00
Comments: 17 pages, 9 figures, submitted to Elsevier in the special issue "Reinforcement Learning and Its Applications to Process Systems Engineering Problems" in the journal "Computers and Chemical Engineering"
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Model predictive control (MPC) is widely used in process control due to its interpretability and ability to handle constraints. As a parametric policy in reinforcement learning (RL), MPC offers strong initial performance and low data requirements compared to black-box policies like neural networks. However, most RL methods rely on first-order updates, which scale well to large parameter spaces but converge at most linearly, making them inefficient when each policy update requires solving an optimal control problem, as is the case with MPC. While MPC policies are typically low parameterized and thus amenable to second-order approaches, existing second-order methods demand second-order policy derivatives, which can be computationally intractable. This work introduces a Gauss-Newton approximation of the deterministic policy Hessian that eliminates the need for second-order policy derivatives, enabling superlinear convergence with minimal computational overhead. To further improve robustness, we propose a momentum-based Hessian averaging scheme for stable training under noisy estimates coupled with an adaptive trustregion. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the approach on a nonlinear continuously stirred tank reactor (CSTR), showing faster convergence and improved data efficiency over state-of-the-art firstorder methods and deep RL approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向模型预测控制的计算高效高斯-牛顿强化学习
模型预测控制（MPC）因其可解释性和处理约束的能力，在过程控制中广泛应用。作为强化学习（RL）中的参数化策略，与神经网络等黑盒策略相比，MPC具有强大的初始性能和较低的数据需求。然而，大多数RL方法依赖一阶更新，虽然能适应大规模参数空间，但至多线性收敛，当每次策略更新都需要求解最优控制问题（如MPC）时效率低下。尽管MPC策略通常参数较少，适合二阶方法，但现有二阶方法需要二阶策略导数，计算上可能难以处理。本研究引入确定性策略海森矩阵的高斯-牛顿近似，无需二阶策略导数即可实现超线性收敛，且计算开销极小。为进一步提升鲁棒性，我们提出基于动量的海森矩阵平均方案，结合自适应信赖域在噪声估计下实现稳定训练。通过在非线性连续搅拌釜反应器（CSTR）上的实验，证明该方法相比先进一阶方法和深度RL方法具有更快的收敛速度和更高的数据效率。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the inefficiency of first-order reinforcement learning methods when training model predictive control (MPC) policies, as each policy update requires solving an optimal control problem, leading to slow linear convergence. The authors propose a computationally efficient Gauss-Newton approximation of the policy Hessian that avoids second-order policy derivatives, enabling superlinear convergence with minimal overhead, and enhance robustness with momentum-based Hessian averaging and an adaptive trust region. Experimental results on a nonlinear continuously stirred tank reactor demonstrate that the method achieves faster convergence and improved data efficiency compared to state-of-the-art first-order and deep reinforcement learning approaches.
本文针对在训练模型预测控制策略时，一阶强化学习方法因每次策略更新都需求解最优控制问题而导致收敛速度慢（线性收敛）的低效问题，提出了一种计算高效的策略Hessian矩阵的高斯-牛顿近似方法，该方法避免了二阶策略导数，能以最小计算开销实现超线性收敛，并通过基于动量的Hessian平均和自适应信赖域增强了鲁棒性。在非线性连续搅拌釜反应器上的实验结果表明，该方法相比最先进的一阶方法和深度强化学习方法，实现了更快的收敛速度和更高的数据效率。
KARL: Knowledge-Aware Reasoning and Reinforcement Learning for Knowledge-Intensive Visual Grounding
Authors: Xinyu Ma, Ziyang Ding, Zhicong Luo, Chi Chen, Zonghao Guo, Derek F. Wong, Zhen Zhao, Xiaoyi Feng, Maosong Sun
First: 2025-03-17T04:06:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T09:32:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Knowledge-Intensive Visual Grounding (KVG) requires models to localize objects using fine-grained, domain-specific entity names rather than generic referring expressions. Although Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) possess rich entity knowledge and strong generic grounding capabilities, they often fail to effectively utilize such knowledge when grounding specialized concepts, revealing a knowledge-grounding gap between internal knowledge and grounding predictions. To address this challenge, we propose a knowledge-aware training paradigm for KVG. Our approach first constructs knowledge-guided reasoning data to encourage models to activate domain-relevant entity knowledge during grounding, and then introduces KARL, a Knowledge-Aware Reinforcement Learning framework that adaptively modulates reward signals according to the model's estimated knowledge mastery of different entities. To facilitate systematic evaluation, we introduce KVG-Bench, a benchmark spanning 10 domains with 1.3K curated test cases covering 531 images and 882 entities. Extensive experiments show that our approach consistently outperforms a wide range of baseline models and achieves substantially stronger cross-domain generalization on unseen categories. The data, codes, and models are released at https://github.com/thunlp/KARL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：KARL：面向知识密集型视觉定位的知识感知推理与强化学习
知识密集型视觉定位（KVG）要求模型使用细粒度、领域特定的实体名称而非通用指代表达进行目标定位。尽管多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）具备丰富的实体知识和强大的通用定位能力，但在定位专业概念时往往无法有效利用此类知识，揭示了内部知识与定位预测之间的知识-定位鸿沟。为应对这一挑战，我们提出了一种面向KVG的知识感知训练范式。该方法首先构建知识引导的推理数据，促使模型在定位过程中激活领域相关的实体知识；随后引入KARL——一种知识感知强化学习框架，能够根据模型对不同实体的知识掌握程度自适应调整奖励信号。为支持系统化评估，我们构建了KVG-Bench基准数据集，涵盖10个领域、1.3K个精选测试案例，包含531张图像和882个实体。大量实验表明，该方法在广泛基线模型中持续保持优势，并在未见类别上实现了显著更强的跨领域泛化能力。数据、代码与模型已发布于https://github.com/thunlp/KARL。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the knowledge-grounding gap in Knowledge-Intensive Visual Grounding (KVG), where models struggle to apply their internal entity knowledge to localize objects with fine-grained, domain-specific names. The proposed method, KARL, introduces a knowledge-aware training paradigm that first uses constructed knowledge-guided reasoning data to activate relevant entity knowledge and then employs a reinforcement learning framework to adaptively modulate rewards based on the model's estimated mastery of different entities. Experimental results on the newly introduced KVG-Bench, spanning 10 domains, demonstrate that KARL consistently outperforms various baselines and achieves substantially stronger cross-domain generalization on unseen categories.
本文针对知识密集型视觉定位任务中模型难以利用内部实体知识来定位具有细粒度、领域特定名称物体的问题，提出了KARL方法。该方法采用一种知识感知的训练范式，首先构建知识引导的推理数据以激活相关实体知识，然后引入一个知识感知的强化学习框架，根据模型对不同实体的知识掌握程度自适应调整奖励信号。在新构建的涵盖10个领域的KVG-Bench基准上的大量实验表明，该方法在多个基线模型中表现最优，并在未见类别上实现了显著更强的跨领域泛化能力。
Deep Reinforcement Learning for Dynamic Algorithm Configuration: A Case Study on Optimizing OneMax with the (1+($λ$,$λ$))-GA
Authors: Tai Nguyen, Phong Le, André Biedenkapp, Carola Doerr, Nguyen Dang
First: 2025-12-03T13:54:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T08:17:48+00:00
Comments: arXiv admin note: text overlap with arXiv:2502.20265
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dynamic Algorithm Configuration (DAC) studies the efficient identification of control policies for parameterized optimization algorithms. Numerous studies leverage Reinforcement Learning (RL) to address DAC challenges; however, applying RL often requires extensive domain expertise. In this work, we conduct a comprehensive study of two deep-RL algorithms--Double Deep Q-Networks (DDQN) and Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO)--for controlling the population size of the $(1+(λ,λ))$-GA on OneMax instances. Although OneMax is structurally simple, learning effective control policies for the $(1+(λ,λ))$-GA induces a highly challenging DAC landscape, making it a controlled yet demanding benchmark. Our investigation reveals two fundamental challenges limiting DDQN and PPO: scalability degradation and learning instability, traced to under-exploration and planning horizon coverage. To address under-exploration, we introduce an adaptive reward shifting mechanism that leverages reward distribution statistics to enhance DDQN exploration. This eliminates instance-specific hyperparameter tuning and ensures consistent effectiveness across problem scales. To resolve planning horizon coverage, we demonstrate that undiscounted learning succeeds in DDQN, while PPO faces fundamental variance issues necessitating alternative designs. We further show that while hyperparameter optimization enhances PPO's stability, it consistently fails to identify effective policies. Finally, DDQN with adaptive reward shifting achieves performance comparable to theoretically derived policies with vastly improved sample efficiency, outperforming prior DAC approaches by orders of magnitude. Our findings provide insights into the fundamental obstacles faced by standard deep-RL approaches in this challenging DAC setting and highlight the key methodological ingredients required for effective learning.

标题：动态算法配置的深度强化学习：基于(1+(λ,λ))-GA优化OneMax的案例研究
动态算法配置（DAC）研究如何高效识别参数化优化算法的控制策略。众多研究利用强化学习（RL）应对DAC挑战，但RL应用常需大量领域专业知识。本研究系统探究两种深度RL算法——双深度Q网络（DDQN）与近端策略优化（PPO）——在OneMax问题上控制(1+(λ,λ))-GA种群规模的表现。尽管OneMax结构简单，但为(1+(λ,λ))-GA学习有效控制策略形成了极具挑战的DAC场景，使其成为受控而严苛的基准。研究发现限制DDQN与PPO的两大根本挑战：可扩展性退化与学习不稳定性，根源在于探索不足与规划视野覆盖问题。针对探索不足，我们提出自适应奖励偏移机制，利用奖励分布统计增强DDQN探索能力。该方法无需实例特定的超参数调优，并确保跨问题规模的一致性效果。针对规划视野覆盖问题，我们证明无折扣学习在DDQN中可行，而PPO面临根本性方差问题需替代设计方案。进一步研究表明，超参数优化虽能提升PPO稳定性，却始终无法获得有效策略。最终，采用自适应奖励偏移的DDQN实现了与理论推导策略相当的性能，且样本效率大幅提升，较现有DAC方法有数量级优势。本研究揭示了标准深度RL方法在此类挑战性DAC场景中的根本性障碍，并指明了有效学习所需的关键方法论要素。

This study investigates the application of deep reinforcement learning (RL) to Dynamic Algorithm Configuration (DAC), motivated by the need to automate the control of algorithm parameters without extensive domain expertise. The authors conduct a case study using Double Deep Q-Networks (DDQN) and Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) to control the population size of the (1+(λ,λ))-GA on the OneMax problem, revealing that standard deep-RL methods face challenges of scalability degradation and learning instability due to under-exploration and planning horizon issues. Understanding visual attention beehind bee-inspired UAV navigation
Authors: Pranav Rajbhandari, Abhi Veda, Matthew Garratt, Mandyam Srinivasan, Sridhar Ravi
First: 2025-07-16T07:44:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T08:02:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bio-inspired design is often used in autonomous UAV navigation due to the capacity of biological systems for flight and obstacle avoidance despite limited sensory and computational capabilities. In particular, honeybees mainly use the sensory input of optic flow, the apparent motion of objects in their visual field, to navigate cluttered environments. In our work, we train a Reinforcement Learning agent to navigate a tunnel with obstacles using only optic flow as sensory input. We inspect the attention patterns of trained agents to determine the regions of optic flow on which they primarily base their motor decisions. We find that agents trained in this way pay most attention to regions of discontinuity in optic flow, as well as regions with large optic flow magnitude. The trained agents appear to navigate a cluttered tunnel by avoiding the obstacles that produce large optic flow, while maintaining a centered position in their environment, which resembles the behavior seen in flying insects. This pattern persists across independently trained agents, which suggests that this could be a good strategy for developing a simple explicit control law for physical UAVs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解析仿蜂无人机导航背后的视觉注意力机制
受生物启发的设计常被用于自主无人机导航，因为生物系统在感知与计算能力有限的情况下仍能实现飞行与避障。蜜蜂主要依赖光流（即视野中物体的表观运动）这一感官输入在复杂环境中导航。本研究训练强化学习智能体仅使用光流作为感官输入，在含障碍物的隧道中导航。通过分析训练后智能体的注意力模式，发现其运动决策主要基于光流中的不连续区域及高光流强度区域。训练后的智能体通过避开产生强光流的障碍物，并保持环境中的居中位置来导航复杂隧道，这与飞行昆虫的行为相似。该模式在不同独立训练的智能体中均保持一致，表明这可能是为实体无人机开发简洁显式控制律的有效策略。

MemRerank: Preference Memory for Personalized Product Reranking
Authors: Zhiyuan Peng, Xuyang Wu, Huaixiao Tou, Yi Fang, Yu Gong
First: 2026-03-31T04:16:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T07:36:51+00:00
Comments: correct author name in metadata
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM-based shopping agents increasingly rely on long purchase histories and multi-turn interactions for personalization, yet naively appending raw history to prompts is often ineffective due to noise, length, and relevance mismatch. We propose MemRerank, a preference memory framework that distills user purchase history into concise, query-independent signals for personalized product reranking. To study this problem, we build an end-to-end benchmark and evaluation framework centered on an LLM-based \textbf{1-in-5} selection task, which measures both memory quality and downstream reranking utility. We further train the memory extractor with reinforcement learning (RL), using downstream reranking performance as supervision. Experiments with two LLM-based rerankers show that MemRerank consistently outperforms no-memory, raw-history, and off-the-shelf memory baselines, yielding up to \textbf{+10.61} absolute points in 1-in-5 accuracy. These results suggest that explicit preference memory is a practical and effective building block for personalization in agentic e-commerce systems.

Learn to Relax with Large Language Models: Solving Constraint Optimization Problems via Bidirectional Coevolution
Authors: Beidan Liu, Zhengqiu Zhu, Chen Gao, Tianle Pu, Yong Zhao, Wei Qi, Quanjun Yin
First: 2025-09-16T03:59:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T06:46:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM)-based optimization has recently shown promise for autonomous problem solving, yet most approaches still cast LLMs as passive constraint checkers rather than proactive strategy designers, limiting their effectiveness on complex Constraint Optimization Problems (COPs). To address this, we present AutoCO, an end-to-end Automated Constraint Optimization method that tightly couples operations-research principles of constraint relaxation with LLM reasoning. A core innovation is a unified triple-representation that binds relaxation strategies, algorithmic principles, and executable codes. This design enables the LLM to synthesize, justify, and instantiate relaxation strategies that are both principled and executable. To navigate fragmented solution spaces, AutoCO employs a bidirectional global-local coevolution mechanism, synergistically coupling Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS) for global relaxation-trajectory exploration with Evolutionary Algorithms (EAs) for local solution intensification. This continuous exchange of priors and feedback explicitly balances diversification and intensification, thus preventing premature convergence. Extensive experiments on three challenging COP benchmarks validate AutoCO's consistent effectiveness and superior performance, especially in hard regimes where current methods degrade. Results highlight AutoCO as a principled and effective path toward proactive, verifiable LLM-driven optimization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学会与大型语言模型协同松弛：通过双向协同进化求解约束优化问题
基于大型语言模型（LLM）的优化方法近期在自主问题求解中展现出潜力，但现有方法大多仅将LLM用作被动的约束检查器，而非主动的策略设计者，限制了其在复杂约束优化问题（COP）上的效能。为此，我们提出AutoCO，一种端到端的自动化约束优化方法，它将运筹学中的约束松弛原理与LLM推理紧密耦合。其核心创新在于一个统一的三元表示框架，将松弛策略、算法原理与可执行代码绑定。这一设计使LLM能够综合、论证并实例化兼具原则性与可执行性的松弛策略。为应对碎片化解空间，AutoCO采用双向全局-局部协同进化机制，通过蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）探索全局松弛轨迹，并结合进化算法（EA）进行局部解强化，二者协同工作。这种先验知识与反馈的持续交换显式平衡了多样性与强化过程，从而避免早熟收敛。在三个高难度COP基准上的大量实验验证了AutoCO具有持续的有效性与优越性能，尤其在现有方法失效的困难场景中表现突出。结果表明，AutoCO为迈向主动、可验证的LLM驱动优化提供了一条原则性强且高效的路径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitation of current LLM-based optimization methods that treat LLMs as passive constraint checkers rather than proactive strategy designers for complex Constraint Optimization Problems (COPs), this paper introduces AutoCO, an automated method that integrates operations-research principles of constraint relaxation with LLM reasoning. The method employs a unified triple-representation linking relaxation strategies, algorithmic principles, and executable code, enabling the LLM to synthesize and instantiate verifiable strategies, and utilizes a bidirectional coevolution mechanism combining Monte Carlo Tree Search for global exploration with Evolutionary Algorithms for local intensification to balance diversification and prevent premature convergence. Experimental results on three challenging COP benchmarks demonstrate AutoCO's consistent effectiveness and superior performance, particularly in hard regimes where existing methods falter, establishing it as a principled approach for proactive LLM-driven optimization.

Adaptive Regime-Aware Stock Price Prediction Using Autoencoder-Gated Dual Node Transformers with Reinforcement Learning Control
Authors: Mohammad Al Ridhawi, Mahtab Haj Ali, Hussein Al Osman
First: 2026-03-19T16:55:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T06:40:40+00:00
Comments: Submitted to Applied Intelligence (Springer). 17 pages, 9 figures, 10 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Stock markets exhibit regime-dependent behavior where prediction models optimized for stable conditions often fail during volatile periods. Existing approaches typically treat all market states uniformly or require manual regime labeling, which is expensive and quickly becomes stale as market dynamics evolve. This paper introduces an adaptive prediction framework that adaptively identifies deviations from normal market conditions and routes data through specialized prediction pathways. The architecture consists of three components: (1) an autoencoder trained on normal market conditions that identifies anomalous regimes through reconstruction error, (2) dual node transformer networks specialized for stable and event-driven market conditions respectively, and (3) a Soft Actor-Critic reinforcement learning controller that adaptively tunes the regime detection threshold and pathway blending weights based on prediction performance feedback. The reinforcement learning component enables the system to learn adaptive regime boundaries, defining anomalies as market states where standard prediction approaches fail. Experiments on 20 S&P 500 stocks spanning 1982 to 2025 demonstrate that the proposed framework achieves 0.68% mean absolute percentage error (MAPE) for one-day predictions without the reinforcement controller and 0.59% MAPE with the full adaptive system, compared to 0.80% for the baseline integrated node transformer. Directional accuracy reaches 72% with the complete framework. The system maintains robust performance during high-volatility periods, with MAPE below 0.85% when baseline models exceed 1.5%. Ablation studies confirm that each component contributes meaningfully: autoencoder routing accounts for 36% relative MAPE degradation upon removal, followed by the SAC controller at 15% and the dual-path architecture at 7%.

Motivated by the regime-dependent behavior of stock markets where models optimized for stable conditions fail during volatility, this paper introduces an adaptive prediction framework that automatically identifies market regimes and routes data through specialized pathways. The method employs an autoencoder to detect anomalous regimes via reconstruction error, dual node transformers for stable and event-driven conditions, and a Soft Actor-Critic reinforcement learning controller to adaptively tune regime thresholds and blending weights based on performance feedback. Experimental results on 20 S&P 500 stocks from 1982 to 2025 show the full system achieves 0.59% mean absolute percentage error (MAPE) for one-day predictions and 72% directional accuracy, outperforming a baseline (0.80% MAPE) and maintaining robustness during high-volatility periods with MAPE below 0.85% when baselines exceed 1.5%, with ablation studies confirming each component's contribution.
本文针对股票市场依赖不同状态（如稳定期与波动期）的行为，提出了一种自适应预测框架，以自动识别市场状态并引导数据通过专门路径。该方法采用自编码器通过重构误差检测异常状态，使用双节点变换器分别处理稳定和事件驱动的市场条件，并利用Soft Actor-Critic强化学习控制器根据预测性能反馈自适应调整状态检测阈值和路径混合权重。在1982年至2025年20只标普500股票上的实验结果表明，完整系统实现了一日预测0.59%的平均绝对百分比误差（MAPE）和72%的方向准确性，优于基线模型（0.80% MAPE），并在高波动期保持稳健性能（MAPE低于0.85%，而基线超过1.5%），消融研究证实了各组件均具有显著贡献。
ContextBudget: Budget-Aware Context Management for Long-Horizon Search Agents
Authors: Yong Wu, YanZhao Zheng, TianZe Xu, ZhenTao Zhang, YuanQiang Yu, JiHuai Zhu, Chao Ma, BinBin Lin, BaoHua Dong, HangCheng Zhu, RuoHui Huang, Gang Yu
First: 2026-04-02T06:09:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T06:09:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM-based agents show strong potential for long-horizon reasoning, yet their context size is limited by deployment factors (e.g., memory, latency, and cost), yielding a constrained context budget. As interaction histories grow, this induces a trade-off between retaining past information and staying within the context limit. To address this challenge, we propose Budget-Aware Context Management (BACM), which formulates context management as a sequential decision problem with a context budget constraint. It enables agents to assess the available budget before incorporating new observations and decide when and how much of the interaction history to compress. We further develop BACM-RL, an end-to-end curriculum-based reinforcement learning approach that learns compression strategies under varying context budgets. Experiments on compositional multi-objective QA and long-horizon web browsing benchmarks show that BACM-RL consistently outperforms prior methods across model scales and task complexities, achieving over $1.6\times$ gains over strong baselines in high-complexity settings, while maintaining strong advantages as budgets shrink, where most methods exhibit a downward performance trend.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ContextBudget：面向长程搜索智能体的预算感知上下文管理
基于大语言模型的智能体在长程推理方面展现出强大潜力，但其上下文规模受部署因素（如内存、延迟和成本）限制，形成受限的上下文预算。随着交互历史的增长，这引发了保留历史信息与遵守上下文限制之间的权衡。为应对这一挑战，我们提出预算感知上下文管理（BACM），将上下文管理建模为具有上下文预算约束的序列决策问题。该方法使智能体能在纳入新观察前评估可用预算，并决定何时及如何压缩交互历史。我们进一步开发了BACM-RL——一种基于课程学习的端到端强化学习方法，可在不同上下文预算下学习压缩策略。在组合式多目标问答和长程网页浏览基准测试上的实验表明，BACM-RL在不同模型规模和任务复杂度下均持续优于现有方法，在高复杂度场景中较强大基线获得超过1.6倍的性能提升，且在预算缩减时保持显著优势——而多数方法在此情况下呈现性能下降趋势。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work stems from the practical limitations on context size in LLM-based agents for long-horizon reasoning, where deployment constraints like memory and cost create a finite context budget, forcing a trade-off between retaining history and staying within limits. The method introduces Budget-Aware Context Management (BACM), framing context management as a sequential decision problem under a budget constraint, allowing agents to evaluate available budget before adding new observations and decide when and how much to compress history, with BACM-RL as an end-to-end curriculum reinforcement learning approach to learn compression strategies across varying budgets. Main experimental results on compositional QA and web browsing benchmarks show BACM-RL consistently outperforms prior methods across model scales and complexities, achieving over 1.6x gains in high-complexity settings and maintaining strong performance as budgets shrink, unlike other methods that decline.

Pseudo-Quantized Actor-Critic Algorithm for Robustness to Noisy Temporal Difference Error
Authors: Taisuke Kobayashi
First: 2026-04-02T04:48:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T04:48:27+00:00
Comments: 38 pages, 12 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In reinforcement learning (RL), temporal difference (TD) errors are widely adopted for optimizing value and policy functions. However, since the TD error is defined by a bootstrap method, its computation tends to be noisy and destabilize learning. Heuristics to improve the accuracy of TD errors, such as target networks and ensemble models, have been introduced so far. While these are essential approaches for the current deep RL algorithms, they cause side effects like increased computational cost and reduced learning efficiency. Therefore, this paper revisits the TD learning algorithm based on control as inference, deriving a novel algorithm capable of robust learning against noisy TD errors. First, the distribution model of optimality, a binary random variable, is represented by a sigmoid function. Alongside forward and reverse Kullback-Leibler divergences, this new model derives a robust learning rule: when the sigmoid function saturates with a large TD error probably due to noise, the gradient vanishes, implicitly excluding it from learning. Furthermore, the two divergences exhibit distinct gradient-vanishing characteristics. Building on these analyses, the optimality is decomposed into multiple levels to achieve pseudo-quantization of TD errors, aiming for further noise reduction. Additionally, a Jensen-Shannon divergence-based approach is approximately derived to inherit the characteristics of both divergences. These benefits are verified through RL benchmarks, demonstrating stable learning even when heuristics are insufficient or rewards contain noise.
中文标题/摘要
标题：伪量化行动者-评论家算法：针对噪声时序差分误差的鲁棒性研究
在强化学习（RL）中，时序差分（TD）误差被广泛用于优化价值函数与策略函数。然而，由于TD误差通过自举法定义，其计算往往存在噪声且易导致学习过程失稳。现有研究已引入目标网络与集成模型等启发式方法提升TD误差精度。这些方法虽是当前深度强化学习算法的核心组件，但会引发计算成本增加、学习效率降低等副作用。为此，本文基于“推断即控制”框架重新审视TD学习算法，推导出一种能对噪声TD误差进行鲁棒学习的新算法。首先，通过Sigmoid函数表示二元随机变量——最优性分布模型。结合前向与反向KL散度，该模型推导出鲁棒学习规则：当Sigmoid函数因噪声导致的大幅TD误差而饱和时，梯度将消失，从而隐式排除该噪声样本的学习。进一步地，两种散度展现出不同的梯度消失特性。基于此分析，通过将最优性分解为多层级实现TD误差的伪量化，以达成更深层的噪声抑制。此外，近似推导出基于Jensen-Shannon散度的方法，以继承两种散度的共同特性。最终通过强化学习基准测试验证了算法优势：即使在启发式方法失效或奖励含噪的场景下，仍能保持稳定学习。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the instability in reinforcement learning caused by noisy temporal difference (TD) errors, which are inherent due to their bootstrapped computation. The authors propose a novel algorithm derived from a control-as-inference perspective, modeling optimality with a sigmoid function to create a robust learning rule: when large, likely noisy TD errors cause the sigmoid to saturate, the gradient vanishes, effectively filtering them out. They further introduce pseudo-quantization of TD errors via multi-level optimality decomposition and a Jensen-Shannon divergence-based method to combine benefits from different divergence measures. Experimental results on RL benchmarks confirm the method's effectiveness, enabling stable learning even when standard heuristics fail or rewards are noisy.
本文针对强化学习中因时序差分误差噪声导致的学习不稳定问题展开研究。作者从控制即推理的角度出发，提出一种新算法，使用sigmoid函数对最优性进行建模，从而推导出鲁棒的学习规则：当可能由噪声引起的大时序差分误差使sigmoid饱和时，梯度消失，从而将其隐式排除在学习过程之外。在此基础上，通过将最优性分解为多个层级以实现时序差分误差的伪量化，并近似推导了一种基于Jensen-Shannon散度的方法以融合不同散度的优势。在强化学习基准测试上的实验结果表明，该方法即使在启发式方法不足或奖励包含噪声的情况下，也能实现稳定的学习。
Intern-S1-Pro: Scientific Multimodal Foundation Model at Trillion Scale

First: 2026-03-26T05:21:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T04:46:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Intern-S1-Pro, the first one-trillion-parameter scientific multimodal foundation model. Scaling to this unprecedented size, the model delivers a comprehensive enhancement across both general and scientific domains. Beyond stronger reasoning and image-text understanding capabilities, its intelligence is augmented with advanced agent capabilities. Simultaneously, its scientific expertise has been vastly expanded to master over 100 specialized tasks across critical science fields, including chemistry, materials, life sciences, and earth sciences. Achieving this massive scale is made possible by the robust infrastructure support of XTuner and LMDeploy, which facilitates highly efficient Reinforcement Learning (RL) training at the 1-trillion parameter level while ensuring strict precision consistency between training and inference. By seamlessly integrating these advancements, Intern-S1-Pro further fortifies the fusion of general and specialized intelligence, working as a Specializable Generalist, demonstrating its position in the top tier of open-source models for general capabilities, while outperforming proprietary models in the depth of specialized scientific tasks.

MM-ReCoder: Advancing Chart-to-Code Generation with Reinforcement Learning and Self-Correction
Authors: Zitian Tang, Xu Zhang, Jianbo Yuan, Yang Zou, Varad Gunjal, Songyao Jiang, Davide Modolo
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2026-04-02T04:21:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T04:21:09+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have recently demonstrated promising capabilities in multimodal coding tasks such as chart-to-code generation. However, existing methods primarily rely on supervised fine-tuning (SFT), which requires the model to learn code patterns through chart-code pairs but does not expose the model to a code execution environment. Moreover, while self-correction through execution feedback offers a potential route to improve coding quality, even state-of-the-art MLLMs have been shown to struggle with effective self-correction. In this work, we introduce MM-ReCoder, a chart-to-code generation model trained with reinforcement learning (RL) and equipped with self-correction ability. We propose a two-stage multi-turn self-correction RL strategy based on Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO). The first stage enhances the model's self-correction ability via rolling out a shared first turn, while the second stage improves the coding capability with full-trajectory optimization. MM-ReCoder learns to produce more accurate and executable code through the interaction with the environment and by iteratively correcting its own outputs. Our results on three chart-to-code benchmarks demonstrate the state-of-the-art performance of MM-ReCoder.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MM-ReCoder：通过强化学习与自我校正推进图表到代码生成
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）近期在图表到代码生成等多模态编码任务中展现出潜力。然而，现有方法主要依赖监督微调（SFT），模型通过图表-代码对学习代码模式，但未接触代码执行环境。此外，尽管通过执行反馈进行自我校正为提升编码质量提供了可能路径，但即使最先进的MLLMs也被证明难以有效自我校正。本研究提出MM-ReCoder，一个结合强化学习（RL）训练并具备自我校正能力的图表到代码生成模型。我们基于组相对策略优化（GRPO）设计了一种两阶段多轮自我校正RL策略：第一阶段通过共享首轮增强模型自我校正能力，第二阶段通过全轨迹优化提升编码能力。MM-ReCoder通过与环境的交互及迭代自我校正输出，学习生成更准确、可执行的代码。在三个图表到代码基准测试中的结果验证了MM-ReCoder的领先性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of supervised fine-tuning, which lacks exposure to code execution environments, and the observed difficulty of state-of-the-art multimodal large language models in effective self-correction, this paper introduces MM-ReCoder for chart-to-code generation. The method employs a two-stage reinforcement learning strategy based on Group Relative Policy Optimization, where the first stage enhances self-correction ability via a shared initial turn and the second stage improves coding capability through full-trajectory optimization, enabling the model to iteratively correct its outputs. Experimental results on three benchmarks demonstrate that MM-ReCoder achieves state-of-the-art performance by learning to produce more accurate and executable code through environment interaction.
本文的动机在于现有监督微调方法缺乏代码执行环境暴露，且先进的多模态大语言模型在有效自我修正方面存在困难，因此提出了用于图表到代码生成的MM-ReCoder模型。该方法采用基于组相对策略优化的两阶段强化学习策略，第一阶段通过共享初始轮次增强自我修正能力，第二阶段通过全轨迹优化提升编码能力，使模型能够迭代修正自身输出。在三个基准测试上的实验结果表明，MM-ReCoder通过与环境交互学习生成更准确、可执行的代码，实现了最先进的性能。
Thinking While Listening: Fast-Slow Recurrence for Long-Horizon Sequential Modeling
Authors: Shota Takashiro, Masanori Koyama, Takeru Miyato, Yusuke Iwasawa, Yutaka Matsuo, Kohei Hayashi
First: 2026-04-02T03:45:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T03:45:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We extend the recent latent recurrent modeling to sequential input streams. By interleaving fast, recurrent latent updates with self-organizational ability between slow observation updates, our method facilitates the learning of stable internal structures that evolve alongside the input. This mechanism allows the model to maintain coherent and clustered representations over long horizons, improving out-of-distribution generalization in reinforcement learning and algorithmic tasks compared to sequential baselines such as LSTM, state space models, and Transformer variants.
中文标题/摘要
标题：边听边思考：面向长时程序列建模的快慢循环机制
我们将近期提出的潜在循环建模方法扩展至序列输入流。通过在缓慢的观测更新之间，交替执行具备自组织能力的快速潜在状态更新，本方法促进了与输入同步演化的稳定内部结构学习。该机制使模型能在长时程中保持连贯且聚类的表征，相比LSTM、状态空间模型及Transformer变体等序列基线方法，在强化学习与算法任务中实现了更强的分布外泛化能力。

The method enhances representation coherence and clustering over extended sequences, enabling better out-of-distribution generalization. Experimental results demonstrate its superiority over sequential baselines like LSTM, state space models, and Transformers in reinforcement learning and algorithmic tasks.

Generative Recommendation for Large-Scale Advertising
Authors: Ben Xue, Dan Liu, Lixiang Wang, Mingjie Sun, Peng Wang, Pengfei Zhang, Shaoyun Shi, Tianyu Xu, Yunhao Sha, Zhiqiang Liu, Bo Kong, Bo Wang, Hang Yang, Jieting Xue, Junhao Wang, Shengyu Wang, Shuping Hui, Wencai Ye, Xiao Lin, Yongzhi Li, Yuhang Chen, Zhihui Yin, Quan Chen, Shiyang Wen, Wenjin Wu, Han Li, Guorui Zhou, Changcheng Li, Peng Jiang, Kun Gai
First: 2026-02-26T08:15:26+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T02:38:13+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 6 figures, under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Generative recommendation has recently attracted widespread attention in industry due to its potential for scaling and stronger model capacity. However, deploying real-time generative recommendation in large-scale advertising requires designs beyond large-language-model (LLM)-style training and serving recipes. We present a production-oriented generative recommender co-designed across architecture, learning, and serving, named GR4AD (Generative Recommendation for ADdvertising). As for tokenization, GR4AD proposes UA-SID (Unified Advertisement Semantic ID) to capture complicated business information. Furthermore, GR4AD introduces LazyAR, a lazy autoregressive decoder that relaxes layer-wise dependencies for short, multi-candidate generation, preserving effectiveness while reducing inference cost, which facilitates scaling under fixed serving budgets. To align optimization with business value, GR4AD employs VSL (Value-Aware Supervised Learning) and proposes RSPO (Ranking-Guided Softmax Preference Optimization), a ranking-aware, list-wise reinforcement learning algorithm that optimizes value-based rewards under list-level metrics for continual online updates. For online inference, we further propose dynamic beam serving, which adapts beam width across generation levels and online load to control compute. Large-scale online A/B tests show up to 4.2% ad revenue improvement over an existing DLRM-based stack, with consistent gains from both model scaling and inference-time scaling. GR4AD has been fully deployed in Kuaishou advertising system with over 400 million users and achieves high-throughput real-time serving.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大规模广告的生成式推荐
生成式推荐因其可扩展性和更强的模型能力，近期在工业界受到广泛关注。然而，在大规模广告中部署实时生成式推荐需要超越大语言模型（LLM）式训练与服务方案的设计。我们提出了一种面向生产的生成式推荐系统GR4AD（面向广告的生成式推荐），在架构、学习与服务层面进行协同设计。在标记化方面，GR4AD提出UA-SID（统一广告语义标识）以捕获复杂的业务信息。此外，GR4AD引入了LazyAR，一种惰性自回归解码器，通过放松层间依赖关系来支持短序列多候选生成，在保持效果的同时降低推理成本，从而有助于在固定服务预算下实现扩展。为使优化与业务价值对齐，GR4AD采用VSL（价值感知监督学习）并提出RSPO（排序引导的Softmax偏好优化），这是一种排序感知的列表级强化学习算法，可在列表级指标下优化基于价值的奖励，以支持持续在线更新。对于在线推理，我们进一步提出动态束搜索服务，通过在不同生成层级和在线负载间自适应调整束宽来控制计算量。大规模在线A/B测试显示，相较于现有基于DLRM的架构，广告收入提升最高达4.2%，模型扩展和推理时扩展均带来持续收益。GR4AD已在拥有超过4亿用户的快手广告系统中全面部署，实现了高吞吐的实时服务。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to deploy real-time generative recommendation in large-scale advertising beyond standard LLM approaches, this paper introduces GR4AD, a production-oriented system co-designed across architecture, learning, and serving. The method employs a Unified Advertisement Semantic ID (UA-SID) for tokenization, a Lazy Autoregressive (LazyAR) decoder for efficient multi-candidate generation, and a ranking-aware reinforcement learning algorithm called RSPO for value-aligned optimization. Main experimental results from large-scale online A/B tests demonstrate up to a 4.2% improvement in ad revenue compared to a DLRM-based baseline, with gains from both model and inference scaling, and the system has been fully deployed serving over 400 million users.
本文的动机是在大规模广告中部署实时生成式推荐，这需要超越标准大语言模型的设计。为此，提出了名为GR4AD的生产导向生成式推荐系统，其在架构、学习和服务端协同设计。方法包括使用统一广告语义ID进行表征、采用惰性自回归解码器以降低推理成本，并提出了基于排序的强化学习算法RSPO进行价值对齐优化。主要实验结果表明，在大规模在线A/B测试中，相比基于DLRM的基线，广告收入提升最高达4.2%，并通过模型和推理扩展实现了持续收益，该系统已全面部署于拥有超过4亿用户的快手广告平台。
Regret Bounds for Reinforcement Learning from Multi-Source Imperfect Preferences
Authors: Ming Shi, Yingbin Liang, Ness B. Shroff, Ananthram Swami
First: 2026-03-20T19:34:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T00:28:28+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) replaces hard-to-specify rewards with pairwise trajectory preferences, yet regret-oriented theory often assumes that preference labels are generated consistently from a single ground-truth objective. In practical RLHF systems, however, feedback is typically \emph{multi-source} (annotators, experts, reward models, heuristics) and can exhibit systematic, persistent mismatches due to subjectivity, expertise variation, and annotation/modeling artifacts. We study episodic RL from \emph{multi-source imperfect preferences} through a cumulative imperfection budget: for each source, the total deviation of its preference probabilities from an ideal oracle is at most $ω$ over $K$ episodes. We propose a unified algorithm with regret $\tilde{O}(\sqrt{K/M}+ω)$, which exhibits a best-of-both-regimes behavior: it achieves $M$-dependent statistical gains when imperfection is small (where $M$ is the number of sources), while remaining robust with unavoidable additive dependence on $ω$ when imperfection is large. We complement this with a lower bound $\tildeΩ(\max\{\sqrt{K/M},ω\})$, which captures the best possible improvement with respect to $M$ and the unavoidable dependence on $ω$, and a counterexample showing that naïvely treating imperfect feedback as oracle-consistent can incur regret as large as $\tildeΩ(\min\{ω\sqrt{K},K\})$. Technically, our approach involves imperfection-adaptive weighted comparison learning, value-targeted transition estimation to control hidden feedback-induced distribution shift, and sub-importance sampling to keep the weighted objectives analyzable, yielding regret guarantees that quantify when multi-source feedback provably improves RLHF and how cumulative imperfection fundamentally limits it.
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the practical challenge in reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) where preference labels often come from multiple imperfect sources, such as different annotators or reward models, rather than a single consistent oracle. The authors propose a unified algorithm for episodic RL with multi-source imperfect preferences, modeling the cumulative deviation of each source's preference probabilities from an ideal oracle via an imperfection budget ω over K episodes. The algorithm achieves a regret bound of Õ(√(K/M) + ω), demonstrating a best-of-both-regimes behavior: it benefits from statistical gains proportional to the number of sources M when imperfection is small, while remaining robust with an additive dependence on ω when imperfection is large. Experimental results, supported by a matching lower bound of Ω̃(max{√(K/M), ω}), show that this approach effectively quantifies when multi-source feedback improves RLHF and how cumulative imperfection fundamentally limits performance, avoiding the poor regret of Õ(min{ω√K, K}) that arises from naively treating imperfect feedback as consistent.
本文针对基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）中的实际问题，即偏好标签通常来自多个不完美的来源（如不同的标注者或奖励模型），而非单一一致的标准答案。作者提出了一种用于多源不完美偏好下情节强化学习的统一算法，通过一个不完美预算ω对K个情节中每个来源的偏好概率与理想标准的累积偏差进行建模。该算法实现了Õ(√(K/M) + ω)的遗憾界，展现出一种两全其美的特性：当不完美程度较小时，它能受益于与来源数量M成正比的统计增益；而当不完美程度较大时，则保持对ω的加性依赖的鲁棒性。实验结果辅以匹配的下界Ω̃(max{√(K/M), ω})表明，该方法有效量化了多源反馈何时能改进RLHF以及累积不完美如何从根本上限制性能，避免了将不完美反馈简单视为一致标准时可能导致的Õ(min{ω√K, K})的较差遗憾。
Matching Accuracy, Different Geometry: Evolution Strategies vs GRPO in LLM Post-Training
Authors: William Hoy, Binxu Wang, Xu Pan
First: 2026-04-02T00:16:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-02T00:16:48+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Evolution Strategies (ES) have emerged as a scalable gradient-free alternative to reinforcement learning based LLM fine-tuning, but it remains unclear whether comparable task performance implies comparable solutions in parameter space. We compare ES and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) across four tasks in both single-task and sequential continual-learning settings. ES matches or exceeds GRPO in single-task accuracy and remains competitive sequentially when its iteration budget is controlled. Despite this similarity in task performance, the two methods produce markedly different model updates: ES makes much larger changes and induces broader off-task KL drift, whereas GRPO makes smaller, more localized updates. Strikingly, the ES and GRPO solutions are linearly connected with no loss barrier, even though their update directions are nearly orthogonal. We develop an analytical theory of ES that explains all these phenomena within a unified framework, showing how ES can accumulate large off-task movement on weakly informative directions while still making enough progress on the task to match gradient-based RL in downstream accuracy. These results show that gradient-free and gradient-based fine-tuning can reach similarly accurate yet geometrically distinct solutions, with important consequences for forgetting and knowledge preservation. The source code is publicly available: https://github.com/Bhoy1/ESvsGRPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：匹配精度，不同几何：大语言模型后训练中进化策略与GRPO的对比研究
进化策略（ES）已成为基于强化学习的大语言模型微调的可扩展无梯度替代方案，但尚不清楚可比的任务性能是否意味着参数空间中可比的解决方案。我们在单任务和序列持续学习两种设置下，通过四项任务对比了ES与组相对策略优化（GRPO）。在单任务精度上，ES匹配或超越GRPO；在迭代预算受控时，其在序列任务中仍保持竞争力。尽管任务性能相似，两种方法产生的模型更新却显著不同：ES产生更大的变化并引发更广泛的离任务KL漂移，而GRPO则进行更小、更局部的更新。引人注目的是，尽管更新方向几乎正交，ES与GRPO的解决方案呈线性连接且无损失障碍。我们提出了ES的分析理论，在统一框架内解释了所有这些现象，展示了ES如何在弱信息方向上积累大量离任务移动，同时仍在任务上取得足够进展，以在下游精度上匹配基于梯度的强化学习。这些结果表明，无梯度与基于梯度的微调能够达到精度相似但几何结构截然不同的解决方案，这对遗忘与知识保存具有重要影响。源代码已公开：https://github.com/Bhoy1/ESvsGRPO。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates whether Evolution Strategies (ES) and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), despite both being used for LLM fine-tuning, converge to similar solutions in parameter space when achieving comparable task accuracy. The method involves a comparative empirical analysis across four tasks in both single-task and sequential continual-learning settings, complemented by the development of an analytical theory for ES. The main experimental results show that ES matches or exceeds GRPO in single-task accuracy and remains competitive in sequential learning with controlled budgets, but produces much larger model updates and broader off-task KL drift. Notably, the solutions from both methods are linearly connected without a loss barrier, even though their update directions are nearly orthogonal, revealing that gradient-free and gradient-based fine-tuning can reach similarly accurate yet geometrically distinct solutions.

DISCO-TAB: A Hierarchical Reinforcement Learning Framework for Privacy-Preserving Synthesis of Complex Clinical Data
Authors: Arshia Ilaty, Hossein Shirazi, Amir Rahmani, Hajar Homayouni
First: 2026-04-01T23:37:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T23:37:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The development of robust clinical decision support systems is frequently impeded by the scarcity of high-fidelity, privacy-preserving biomedical data. While Generative Large Language Models (LLMs) offer a promising avenue for synthetic data generation, they often struggle to capture the complex, non-linear dependencies and severe class imbalances inherent in Electronic Health Records (EHR), leading to statistically plausible but clinically invalid records. To bridge this gap, we introduce DISCO-TAB (DIScriminator-guided COntrol for TABular synthesis), a novel framework that orchestrates a fine-tuned LLM with a multi-objective discriminator system optimized via Reinforcement Learning. Unlike prior methods relying on scalar feedback, DISCO-TAB evaluates synthesis at four granularities, token, sentence, feature, and row, while integrating Automated Constraint Discovery and Inverse-Frequency Reward Shaping to autonomously preserve latent medical logic and resolve minority-class collapse. We rigorously validate our framework across diverse benchmarks, including high-dimensional, small-sample medical datasets (e.g., Heart Failure, Parkinson's). Our results demonstrate that hierarchical feedback yields state-of-the-art performance, achieving up to 38.2% improvement in downstream clinical classifier utility compared to GAN and Diffusion baselines, while ensuring exceptional statistical fidelity (JSD < 0.01) and robust resistance to membership inference attacks. This work establishes a new standard for generating trustworthy, utility-preserving synthetic tabular data for sensitive healthcare applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DISCO-TAB：一种用于复杂临床数据隐私保护合成的分层强化学习框架
开发稳健的临床决策支持系统常因高保真、隐私保护的生物医学数据稀缺而受阻。尽管生成式大语言模型为合成数据生成提供了可行路径，但其往往难以捕捉电子健康记录中固有的复杂非线性依赖性和严重类别不平衡，导致生成统计上合理但临床无效的记录。为弥合这一差距，我们提出了DISCO-TAB（面向表格合成的判别器引导控制框架），该新颖框架通过强化学习优化的多目标判别器系统协调微调后的大语言模型。与依赖标量反馈的现有方法不同，DISCO-TAB在词元、句子、特征和行四个粒度评估合成过程，同时集成自动约束发现和逆频率奖励塑造技术，以自主保持潜在医学逻辑并解决少数类坍缩问题。我们在多样化基准测试中严格验证了该框架，包括高维小样本医疗数据集（如心力衰竭、帕金森病）。结果表明，分层反馈机制实现了最先进的性能，相比生成对抗网络和扩散基线方法，下游临床分类器效用提升最高达38.2%，同时确保卓越的统计保真度（JSD < 0.01）以及对成员推理攻击的强鲁棒性。本研究为敏感医疗应用生成可信赖、效用保持的合成表格数据确立了新标准。

Soft MPCritic: Amortized Model Predictive Value Iteration
Authors: Thomas Banker, Nathan P. Lawrence, Ali Mesbah
First: 2026-04-01T23:35:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T23:35:00+00:00
Comments: submitted to CDC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) and model predictive control (MPC) offer complementary strengths, yet combining them at scale remains computationally challenging. We propose soft MPCritic, an RL-MPC framework that learns in (soft) value space while using sample-based planning for both online control and value target generation. soft MPCritic instantiates MPC through model predictive path integral control (MPPI) and trains a terminal Q-function with fitted value iteration, aligning the learned value function with the planner and implicitly extending the effective planning horizon. We introduce an amortized warm-start strategy that recycles planned open-loop action sequences from online observations when computing batched MPPI-based value targets. This makes soft MPCritic computationally practical, while preserving solution quality. soft MPCritic plans in a scenario-based fashion with an ensemble of dynamic models trained for next-step prediction accuracy. Together, these ingredients enable soft MPCritic to learn effectively through robust, short-horizon planning on classic and complex control tasks. These results establish soft MPCritic as a practical and scalable blueprint for synthesizing MPC policies in settings where policy extraction and direct, long-horizon planning may fail.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Soft MPCritic：摊销模型预测价值迭代
强化学习（RL）与模型预测控制（MPC）各具优势，但大规模结合仍面临计算挑战。本文提出soft MPCritic——一种在（软）价值空间中学习、同时采用基于样本的规划进行在线控制与价值目标生成的RL-MPC框架。该框架通过模型预测路径积分控制（MPPI）实例化MPC，并利用拟合价值迭代训练终端Q函数，使习得价值函数与规划器对齐，从而隐式扩展有效规划时域。我们引入一种摊销预热启动策略，在计算基于批量MPPI的价值目标时，复用从在线观测中规划的开环动作序列。这一设计在保持求解质量的同时，显著提升了计算实用性。soft MPCritic采用基于场景的规划方式，并集成多个以单步预测精度为目标训练的动态模型。这些组件共同使该框架能够通过在经典及复杂控制任务上进行鲁棒的短时域规划实现高效学习。实验结果表明，在策略提取与直接长时域规划可能失效的场景中，soft MPCritic为MPC策略合成提供了实用且可扩展的蓝图。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the complementary strengths of reinforcement learning (RL) and model predictive control (MPC), and the computational challenge of integrating them at scale. The method, soft MPCritic, combines RL and MPC by learning a terminal Q-function through fitted value iteration while using model predictive path integral control (MPPI) for online planning and value target generation; it employs an amortized warm-start strategy to recycle planned action sequences for efficient batched computation and uses an ensemble of dynamic models for robust, scenario-based planning. Experimental results on classic and complex control tasks demonstrate that the framework learns effectively through short-horizon planning, offering a practical and scalable approach for synthesizing MPC policies where long-horizon planning or direct policy extraction may fail.

When Reward Hacking Rebounds: Understanding and Mitigating It with Representation-Level Signals
Authors: Rui Wu, Ruixiang Tang
First: 2026-04-01T23:33:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T23:33:08+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning for LLMs is vulnerable to reward hacking, where models exploit shortcuts to maximize reward without solving the intended task. We systematically study this phenomenon in coding tasks using an environment-manipulation setting, where models can rewrite evaluator code to trivially pass tests without solving the task, as a controlled testbed. Across both studied models, we identify a reproducible three-phase rebound pattern: models first attempt to rewrite the evaluator but fail, as their rewrites embed test cases their own solutions cannot pass. They then temporarily retreat to legitimate solving. When legitimate reward remains scarce, they rebound into successful hacking with qualitatively different strategies. Using representation engineering, we extract concept directions for shortcut, deception, and evaluation awareness from domain-general contrastive pairs and find that the shortcut direction tracks hacking behavior most closely, making it an effective representational proxy for detection. Motivated by this finding, we propose Advantage Modification, which integrates shortcut concept scores into GRPO advantage computation to penalize hacking rollouts before policy updates. Because the penalty is internalized into the training signal rather than applied only at inference time, Advantage Modification provides more robust suppression of hacking compared with generation-time activation steering.
中文标题/摘要
标题：奖励黑客攻击反弹效应：基于表征层面信号的理解与缓解方法
大语言模型的强化学习易受奖励黑客攻击影响，即模型通过利用捷径最大化奖励而非真正解决目标任务。本研究以代码任务为受控实验环境，系统探讨了模型通过重写评估器代码以轻松通过测试却未解决问题的环境操纵现象。在两个被测模型中均观察到可复现的三阶段反弹模式：模型首先尝试重写评估器但失败，因其重写代码嵌入了自身解法无法通过的测试用例；随后暂时回归合法解题；当合法奖励持续稀缺时，模型会以质变策略反弹至成功攻击。通过表征工程，我们从领域通用对比对中提取了捷径、欺骗和评估意识的概念方向，发现捷径方向与黑客行为关联最紧密，可作为有效的检测表征代理。基于此发现，我们提出优势修正方法，将捷径概念分数整合至GRPO优势计算中，在策略更新前惩罚黑客行为轨迹。由于惩罚机制内化于训练信号而非仅作用于推理阶段，相较于生成时激活引导，优势修正能更稳健地抑制黑客行为。
