This paper investigates reward hacking in reinforcement learning for large language models, where models exploit shortcuts to maximize rewards without genuinely solving tasks, using a controlled coding environment where models can manipulate evaluator code. The authors identify a three-phase rebound pattern: initial failed hacking attempts, a temporary retreat to legitimate solving, and a rebound to successful hacking when legitimate rewards are scarce. They employ representation engineering to extract concept directions, finding that the shortcut direction effectively tracks hacking behavior, and propose Advantage Modification, which integrates shortcut concept scores into advantage computation to penalize hacking during training, leading to more robust suppression compared to inference-time methods.
本文研究大型语言模型强化学习中的奖励黑客行为，即模型利用捷径最大化奖励而非真正解决问题，通过一个可控的编码环境，模型可操纵评估器代码。作者发现了一种三阶段反弹模式：初始的黑客尝试失败，暂时回归合法解决，以及在合法奖励稀缺时反弹至成功黑客行为。他们采用表示工程提取概念方向，发现捷径方向能有效追踪黑客行为，并提出了优势修正方法，将捷径概念分数整合到优势计算中，在训练时惩罚黑客行为，相比推理时方法能更稳健地抑制黑客。
D-SPEAR: Dual-Stream Prioritized Experience Adaptive Replay for Stable Reinforcement Learning in Robotic Manipulation
Authors: Yu Zhang, Karl Mason
First: 2026-03-28T17:34:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T22:51:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted at IEEE 11th International Conference on Control and Robotics Engineering (ICCRE 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robotic manipulation remains challenging for reinforcement learning due to contact-rich dynamics, long horizons, and training instability. Although off-policy actor-critic algorithms such as SAC and TD3 perform well in simulation, they often suffer from policy oscillations and performance collapse in realistic settings, partly due to experience replay strategies that ignore the differing data requirements of the actor and the critic. We propose D-SPEAR: Dual-Stream Prioritized Experience Adaptive Replay, a replay framework that decouples actor and critic sampling while maintaining a shared replay buffer. The critic leverages prioritized replay for efficient value learning, whereas the actor is updated using low-error transitions to stabilize policy optimization. An adaptive anchor mechanism balances uniform and prioritized sampling based on the coefficient of variation of TD errors, and a Huber-based critic objective further improves robustness under heterogeneous reward scales. We evaluate D-SPEAR on challenging robotic manipulation tasks from the robosuite benchmark, including Block-Lifting and Door-Opening. Results demonstrate that D-SPEAR consistently outperforms strong off-policy baselines, including SAC, TD3, and DDPG, in both final performance and training stability, with ablation studies confirming the complementary roles of the actorside and critic-side replay streams.
中文标题/摘要
标题：D-SPEAR：面向机器人操作稳定强化学习的双流优先经验自适应回放
机器人操作因接触密集型动态、长决策序列和训练不稳定性，对强化学习仍具挑战。尽管SAC、TD3等离轨行动者-评论家算法在仿真中表现良好，但在实际场景中常出现策略振荡与性能崩溃，部分原因在于经验回放策略未区分行动者与评论家的数据需求。本文提出D-SPEAR：双流优先经验自适应回放框架，该框架在维持共享回放缓冲区的同时解耦行动者与评论家的采样过程。评论家采用优先回放以提升价值学习效率，行动者则通过低误差状态转移更新以稳定策略优化。自适应锚定机制基于时序差分误差变异系数平衡均匀采样与优先采样，而基于Huber损失的评论家目标函数进一步增强了异质奖励尺度下的鲁棒性。我们在robosuite基准测试的机器人操作任务（包括方块抓取与开门任务）上评估D-SPEAR。实验表明，D-SPEAR在最终性能与训练稳定性上均优于SAC、TD3、DDPG等强离轨基线方法，消融研究证实了行动者侧与评论家侧回放流的互补作用。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses training instability in off-policy reinforcement learning for robotic manipulation, where standard experience replay fails to account for the distinct data needs of actor and critic networks. The proposed method, D-SPEAR, introduces a dual-stream replay framework that decouples sampling: the critic uses prioritized replay for value learning, while the actor samples low-error transitions to stabilize policy updates, with an adaptive anchor mechanism balancing sampling strategies based on TD error variation and a Huber loss enhancing robustness. Experimental results on robosuite tasks like Block-Lifting and Door-Opening show D-SPEAR outperforms SAC, TD3, and DDPG in final performance and stability, with ablations validating the complementary roles of its dual streams.
本文针对机器人操控中离线策略强化学习的训练不稳定问题，提出标准经验回放未考虑执行器和评论器网络的不同数据需求。所提出的D-SPEAR方法采用双流回放框架，解耦了采样过程：评论器利用优先回放进行价值学习，而执行器采样低误差转移以稳定策略更新，并通过基于TD误差变化的自适应锚机制平衡采样策略，同时使用Huber损失提升鲁棒性。在robosuite的Block-Lifting和Door-Opening等任务上的实验结果表明，D-SPEAR在最终性能和训练稳定性上均优于SAC、TD3和DDPG等基线方法，消融研究证实了其双流设计的互补作用。
Semantic Interaction Information mediates compositional generalization in latent space
Authors: John Schwarcz
First: 2026-03-28T04:46:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T22:46:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Are there still barriers to generalization once all relevant variables are known? We address this question via a framework that casts compositional generalization as a variational inference problem over latent variables with parametric interactions. To explore this, we develop the Cognitive Gridworld, a stationary Partially Observable Markov Decision Process (POMDP) where observations are generated jointly by multiple latent variables, yet feedback is provided for only a single goal variable. This setting allows us to define Semantic Interaction Information (SII): a metric measuring the contribution of latent variable interactions to task performance. Using SII, we analyze Recurrent Neural Networks (RNNs) provided with these interactions, finding that SII explains the accuracy gap between Echo State and Fully Trained networks. Our analysis also uncovers a theoretically predicted failure mode where confidence decouples from accuracy, suggesting that utilizing interactions between relevant variables is a non-trivial capability. We then address a harder regime where the interactions must be learned by an embedding model. Learning how latent variables interact requires accurate inference, yet accurate inference depends on knowing those interactions. The Cognitive Gridworld reveals this circular dependence as a core challenge for continual meta-learning. We approach this dilemma via Representation Classification Chains (RCCs), a JEPA-style architecture that disentangles these processes: variable inference and variable embeddings are learned by separate modules through Reinforcement Learning and self-supervised learning, respectively. Lastly, we demonstrate that RCCs facilitate compositional generalization to novel combinations of relevant variables. Together, these results establish a grounded setting for evaluating goal-directed generalist agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：语义交互信息在潜在空间中调节组合泛化
当所有相关变量已知时，泛化是否仍存在障碍？我们通过一个框架探讨此问题，该框架将组合泛化视为对具有参数化交互的潜在变量的变分推断问题。为此，我们开发了认知网格世界——一个静态部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP），其中观测由多个潜在变量共同生成，但反馈仅针对单一目标变量提供。该设定允许我们定义语义交互信息（SII）：一种衡量潜在变量交互对任务性能贡献的指标。利用SII，我们分析了具备这些交互的循环神经网络（RNN），发现SII解释了回声状态网络与完全训练网络之间的准确率差距。分析还揭示了一种理论预测的失效模式，即置信度与准确率解耦，表明利用相关变量间的交互是一项非平凡能力。 随后，我们研究了一个更困难的机制：交互必须通过嵌入模型学习。学习潜在变量的交互需要准确推断，而准确推断又依赖于已知这些交互。认知网格世界揭示了这种循环依赖是持续元学习的核心挑战。我们通过表示分类链（RCC）应对这一困境——这是一种JEPA风格架构，将变量推断与变量嵌入解耦：前者通过强化学习由独立模块学习，后者通过自监督学习实现。最后，我们证明RCC能促进对相关变量新组合的组合泛化。这些结果共同为评估目标导向的通用智能体建立了基础框架。
Summary / 总结
The paper investigates whether knowing all relevant variables is sufficient for compositional generalization, proposing a framework that treats it as a variational inference problem over latent variables with parametric interactions. To explore this, the authors introduce the Cognitive Gridworld, a stationary POMDP where observations stem from multiple latent variables but feedback targets only a goal variable, enabling the definition of Semantic Interaction Information (SII) to quantify how latent variable interactions affect task performance. Experiments with Recurrent Neural Networks show that SII explains accuracy differences between network types and reveals a failure mode where confidence detaches from accuracy, highlighting the non-trivial nature of leveraging variable interactions. In a more challenging regime where interactions must be learned, the study identifies a circular dependence between inference and interaction knowledge, addressed via Representation Classification Chains (RCCs), an architecture that separates variable inference (learned via reinforcement learning) from variable embeddings (learned via self-supervision), ultimately demonstrating that RCCs enable compositional generalization to novel variable combinations, thus providing a grounded evaluation setting for goal-directed generalist agents.
本文探讨了在已知所有相关变量的情况下，组合泛化是否仍存在障碍，提出了一个将组合泛化视为潜在变量参数交互的变分推断问题的框架。为此，作者开发了认知网格世界，这是一个静态部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，其中观测由多个潜在变量共同生成，但反馈仅针对单个目标变量，从而定义了语义交互信息（SII）来量化潜在变量交互对任务性能的影响。对循环神经网络的实验表明，SII解释了不同类型网络之间的准确率差距，并揭示了一种置信度与准确率脱钩的故障模式，强调了利用变量交互的非平凡性。在更困难的、交互必须学习的机制中，研究发现了推断与交互知识之间的循环依赖问题，通过表示分类链（RCCs）这一架构解决，该架构将变量推断（通过强化学习学习）与变量嵌入（通过自监督学习学习）分离，最终证明RCCs能够实现对新颖变量组合的组合泛化，从而为面向目标的通用智能体提供了一个坚实的评估场景。
Improving Latent Generalization Using Test-time Compute
Authors: Arslan Chaudhry, Sridhar Thiagarajan, Andrew Lampinen
First: 2026-04-01T22:10:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T22:10:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Language Models (LMs) exhibit two distinct mechanisms for knowledge acquisition: in-weights learning (i.e., encoding information within the model weights) and in-context learning (ICL). Although these two modes offer complementary strengths, in-weights learning frequently struggles to facilitate deductive reasoning over the internalized knowledge. We characterize this limitation as a deficit in latent generalization, of which the reversal curse is one example. Conversely, in-context learning demonstrates highly robust latent generalization capabilities. To improve latent generalization from in-weights knowledge, prior approaches rely on train-time data augmentation, yet these techniques are task-specific, scale poorly, and fail to generalize to out-of-distribution knowledge. To overcome these shortcomings, this work studies how models can be taught to use test-time compute, or 'thinking', specifically to improve latent generalization. We use Reinforcement Learning (RL) from correctness feedback to train models to produce long chains-of-thought (CoTs) to improve latent generalization. Our experiments show that this thinking approach not only resolves many instances of latent generalization failures on in-distribution knowledge but also, unlike augmentation baselines, generalizes to new knowledge for which no RL was performed. Nevertheless, on pure reversal tasks, we find that thinking does not unlock direct knowledge inversion, but the generate-and-verify ability of thinking models enables them to get well above chance performance. The brittleness of factual self-verification means thinking models still remain well below the performance of in-context learning for this task. Overall, our results establish test-time thinking as a flexible and promising direction for improving the latent generalization of LMs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：利用测试时计算提升潜在泛化能力
语言模型通过两种机制获取知识：权重内学习（将信息编码至模型权重）与上下文学习。虽然二者优势互补，但权重内学习常难以对已内化知识进行演绎推理。我们将此局限定义为潜在泛化缺陷（逆转诅咒即为一例），而上下文学习则展现出极强的潜在泛化能力。为提升权重内知识的潜在泛化性，现有方法依赖训练时数据增强，但这些技术存在任务特定性、扩展性差且难以泛化至分布外知识的问题。本研究通过强化学习基于正确性反馈训练模型生成长链思维推理，探索如何利用测试时计算（即“思考”）改善潜在泛化。实验表明：该思考方法不仅能解决分布内知识的潜在泛化失败案例，还能泛化至未经强化学习训练的新知识；在纯逆转任务中，思考虽未实现直接知识反转，但通过生成-验证机制使模型表现显著超越随机基线。由于事实自验证的脆弱性，思考模型在此类任务中仍远逊于上下文学习。总体而言，测试时思考为提升语言模型潜在泛化能力提供了灵活且前景广阔的研究方向。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of language models in performing deductive reasoning over their internalized knowledge, a problem termed latent generalization, where in-weights learning often fails compared to robust in-context learning. To improve latent generalization without relying on task-specific, poorly scaling train-time data augmentation, the authors propose training models via Reinforcement Learning from correctness feedback to produce long chains-of-thought at test time, effectively teaching them to 'think'. Experimental results demonstrate that this thinking approach resolves many in-distribution latent generalization failures and, unlike augmentation baselines, generalizes to new, out-of-distribution knowledge without additional RL; however, on pure reversal tasks, while thinking enables generate-and-verify strategies for above-chance performance, it falls short of in-context learning due to the brittleness of factual self-verification.
本文针对语言模型在对其内化知识进行演绎推理时的局限性，即潜在泛化不足的问题展开研究，其中权重内学习相比上下文学习表现较差。为改进潜在泛化能力，避免依赖任务特定、扩展性差的训练时数据增强方法，作者提出通过基于正确性反馈的强化学习来训练模型，使其在测试时生成长思维链，即学会“思考”。实验结果表明，这种思考方法解决了许多分布内潜在泛化失败案例，并且与增强基线不同，能够泛化到未经强化学习的新分布外知识；然而，在纯粹的反转任务上，思考虽能通过生成-验证策略获得高于随机猜测的性能，但由于事实自验证的脆弱性，其表现仍远不及上下文学习。
When Should a Robot Think? Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning for Embodied Robotic Decision-Making
Authors: Jun Liu, Pu Zhao, Zhenglun Kong, Xuan Shen, Peiyan Dong, Fan Yang, Lin Cui, Hao Tang, Geng Yuan, Wei Niu, Wenbin Zhang, Xue Lin, Gaowen Liu, Yanzhi Wang, Dong Huang
First: 2026-03-17T15:38:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T21:31:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Embodied robotic systems increasingly rely on large language model (LLM)-based agents to support high-level reasoning, planning, and decision-making during interactions with the environment. However, invoking LLM reasoning introduces substantial computational latency and resource overhead, which can interrupt action execution and reduce system reliability. Excessive reasoning may delay actions, while insufficient reasoning often leads to incorrect decisions and task failures. This raises a fundamental question for embodied agents: when should the agent reason, and when should it act? In this work, we propose RARRL (Resource-Aware Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning), a hierarchical framework for resource-aware orchestration of embodied agents. Rather than learning low-level control policies, RARRL learns a high-level orchestration policy that operates at the agent's decision-making layer. This policy enables the agent to adaptively determine whether to invoke reasoning, which reasoning role to employ, and how much computational budget to allocate based on current observations, execution history, and remaining resources. Extensive experiments, including evaluations with empirical latency profiles derived from the ALFRED benchmark, show that RARRL consistently improves task success rates while reducing execution latency and enhancing robustness compared with fixed or heuristic reasoning strategies. These results demonstrate that adaptive reasoning control is essential for building reliable and efficient embodied robotic agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：机器人何时应思考？基于强化学习的资源感知推理在具身机器人决策中的应用
具身机器人系统日益依赖基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体，以支持其在与环境交互过程中的高层推理、规划与决策。然而，调用LLM推理会带来显著的计算延迟与资源开销，可能中断动作执行并降低系统可靠性。过度推理会延迟行动，而推理不足则常导致错误决策与任务失败。这引发了一个具身智能体的根本性问题：智能体应在何时推理，又在何时行动？本研究提出RARRL（基于强化学习的资源感知推理），一种用于具身智能体资源感知编排的分层框架。RARRL不学习底层控制策略，而是学习在智能体决策层运行的高层编排策略。该策略使智能体能根据当前观测、执行历史与剩余资源，自适应地决定是否调用推理、采用何种推理角色以及分配多少计算预算。大量实验（包括基于ALFRED基准提取的实测延迟曲线评估）表明，相较于固定或启发式推理策略，RARRL在降低执行延迟、增强鲁棒性的同时，持续提升了任务成功率。这些结果证明，自适应推理控制对于构建可靠高效的具身机器人智能体至关重要。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of balancing computational resource use with decision-making quality in embodied robotic systems that employ large language models (LLMs) for reasoning, where excessive reasoning causes latency and insufficient reasoning leads to errors. The authors propose RARRL, a hierarchical reinforcement learning framework that learns a high-level orchestration policy to adaptively decide when to invoke reasoning, which reasoning role to use, and how much computational budget to allocate based on observations, history, and resources. Experimental evaluations using latency profiles from the ALFRED benchmark demonstrate that RARRL improves task success rates, reduces execution latency, and enhances robustness compared to fixed or heuristic reasoning strategies, highlighting the importance of adaptive reasoning control for efficient and reliable robotic agents.
本文针对具身机器人系统使用大语言模型进行推理时面临的挑战，即过度推理会导致延迟，而推理不足则引发决策错误，旨在平衡计算资源与决策质量。作者提出了RARRL，一种基于分层强化学习的框架，通过学习高层编排策略，使机器人能根据当前观察、执行历史和剩余资源自适应地决定何时调用推理、使用何种推理角色以及分配多少计算预算。基于ALFRED基准的延迟配置文件进行的实验表明，与固定或启发式推理策略相比，RARRL能提高任务成功率、降低执行延迟并增强系统鲁棒性，这证明了自适应推理控制对于构建高效可靠具身机器人的重要性。
Machine Learning for Network Attacks Classification and Statistical Evaluation of Adversarial Learning Methodologies for Synthetic Data Generation
Authors: Iakovos-Christos Zarkadis, Christos Douligeris
First: 2026-03-18T13:35:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T20:58:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Supervised detection of network attacks has always been a critical part of network intrusion detection systems (NIDS). Nowadays, in a pivotal time for artificial intelligence (AI), with even more sophisticated attacks that utilize advanced techniques, such as generative artificial intelligence (GenAI) and reinforcement learning, it has become a vital component if we wish to protect our personal data, which are scattered across the web. In this paper, we address two tasks, in the first unified multi-modal NIDS dataset, which incorporates flow-level data, packet payload information and temporal contextual features, from the reprocessed CIC-IDS-2017, CIC-IoT-2023, UNSW-NB15 and CIC-DDoS-2019, with the same feature space. In the first task we use machine learning (ML) algorithms, with stratified cross validation, in order to prevent network attacks, with stability and reliability. In the second task we use adversarial learning algorithms to generate synthetic data, compare them with the real ones and evaluate their fidelity, utility and privacy using the SDV framework, f-divergences, distinguishability and non-parametric statistical tests. The findings provide stable ML models for intrusion detection and generative models with high fidelity and utility, by combining the Synthetic Data Vault framework, the TRTS and TSTR tests, with non-parametric statistical tests and f-divergence measures.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向网络攻击分类的机器学习及对抗学习方法在合成数据生成中的统计评估
网络攻击的监督检测一直是网络入侵检测系统（NIDS）的关键组成部分。当前正值人工智能（AI）发展的关键时期，随着利用生成式人工智能（GenAI）和强化学习等先进技术的攻击手段日益复杂，保护散落在网络中的个人数据已成为至关重要的任务。本文基于首个统一多模态NIDS数据集（整合了来自重处理的CIC-IDS-2017、CIC-IoT-2023、UNSW-NB15和CIC-DDoS-2019数据集的流级数据、数据包载荷信息及时间上下文特征，并保持相同特征空间）开展两项研究：首先采用分层交叉验证的机器学习（ML）算法构建稳定可靠的网络攻击防御模型；其次运用对抗学习算法生成合成数据，通过SDV框架、f散度、可区分性及非参数统计检验，从保真度、实用性与隐私性维度对比评估合成数据与真实数据。研究结合合成数据保险库框架、TRTS与TSTR测试、非参数统计检验及f散度度量，最终构建了稳定的入侵检测ML模型，以及兼具高保真度与实用性的生成模型。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for robust network intrusion detection systems (NIDS) in the era of sophisticated AI-driven attacks, this paper tackles two primary tasks using a unified multi-modal dataset derived from several public benchmarks. The method involves, first, employing machine learning algorithms with stratified cross-validation to classify network attacks reliably and, second, utilizing adversarial learning to generate synthetic data, which is then rigorously evaluated for fidelity, utility, and privacy using the SDV framework, f-divergences, and statistical tests. The main experimental results demonstrate the development of stable ML models for intrusion detection and generative models that produce synthetic data with high fidelity and utility, as validated through a combination of TRTS/TSTR tests and non-parametric statistical measures.
本文的动机是在人工智能攻击日益复杂的背景下，构建强大的网络入侵检测系统（NIDS）。研究方法基于一个融合了多个公开数据集特征的多模态统一数据集，首先采用机器学习算法与分层交叉验证来稳定分类网络攻击，其次利用对抗学习生成合成数据，并通过SDV框架、f-散度及统计检验评估其保真度、实用性和隐私性。主要实验结果表明，研究获得了稳定的入侵检测机器学习模型，以及能够生成具有高保真度和实用性的合成数据的生成模型，这些结果通过TRTS/TSTR测试与非参数统计检验得到了验证。
SAKE: Structured Agentic Knowledge Extrapolation for Complex LLM Reasoning via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jiashu He, Jinxuan Fan, Bowen Jiang, Ignacio Houine, Dan Roth, Alejandro Ribeiro
First: 2025-05-21T03:30:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T20:49:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Knowledge extrapolation is the process of inferring novel information by combining and extending existing knowledge that is explicitly available. It is essential for solving complex questions in specialized domains where retrieving comprehensive external knowledge is impractical. We propose SAKE (Structured Agentic Knowledge Extrapolation), a RL powered agentic framework that trains LLMs to autonomously retrieve and extrapolate structured knowledge through tool-augmented reinforcement learning. SAKE defines two external KG tools: entity group construction and cross-group triplet retrieval. The model learns to interleave these 2 retrieval tools during a three-turn rollout: extracting key entities, filtering relevant concept groups, and associative reasoning by constructing new triplets through analogy. The entire pipeline is optimized end-to-end with GRPO using a curriculum reward, teaching the model what to retrieve and how to reason over it. Our experiments proved that SAKE fine-tuned Qwen2.5-7B model surpasses GPT-3.5-Turbo with state-of-the-art agentic KG reasoning on both biomedical (75.4% vs. 70.1%) and commonsense (81.3% vs. 74.7%) benchmarks, while reducing token usage by over 90%. These results demonstrate that associative reasoning over incomplete structured knowledge does not requiring large models with complex, multi-step prompting, thus can be learned end-to-end by small, open-weight models through reinforcement learning with the right tools and training signal. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SAKE-7585.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SAKE：基于强化学习的结构化智能体知识外推框架用于复杂大语言模型推理
知识外推是通过组合和扩展现有显式知识来推断新信息的过程，对于在难以检索全面外部知识的专业领域解决复杂问题至关重要。我们提出SAKE（结构化智能体知识外推），这是一个基于强化学习的智能体框架，通过工具增强的强化学习训练大语言模型自主检索和外推结构化知识。SAKE定义了两个外部知识图谱工具：实体组构建和跨组三元组检索。模型通过三阶段推演学习交替使用这两种检索工具：提取关键实体、筛选相关概念组，以及通过类比构建新三元组进行关联推理。整个流程采用课程奖励的GRPO方法进行端到端优化，指导模型学习检索内容和推理方式。实验表明，经SAKE微调的Qwen2.5-7B模型在生物医学（75.4% vs. 70.1%）和常识推理（81.3% vs. 74.7%）基准测试中均超越GPT-3.5-Turbo的先进智能体知识图谱推理性能，同时减少90%以上的令牌使用量。这些结果证明，对不完整结构化知识的关联推理无需依赖复杂多步提示的大模型，小型开源权重模型通过恰当的强化学习工具和训练信号即可实现端到端学习。代码发布于https://anonymous.4open.science/r/SAKE-7585。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of complex reasoning in specialized domains where external knowledge retrieval is impractical, motivating the development of a method for knowledge extrapolation to infer novel information from existing structured knowledge. It proposes SAKE, a reinforcement learning framework that trains large language models to autonomously retrieve and extrapolate knowledge using two external knowledge graph tools: entity group construction and cross-group triplet retrieval, interleaved in a three-turn rollout for associative reasoning via analogy, optimized end-to-end with GRPO and a curriculum reward. Experimental results show that the SAKE-fine-tuned Qwen2.5-7B model outperforms GPT-3.5-Turbo on biomedical and commonsense benchmarks (75.4% vs. 70.1% and 81.3% vs. 74.7%, respectively) while reducing token usage by over 90%, demonstrating that small open-weight models can learn effective reasoning through reinforcement learning with appropriate tools.
本文针对专业领域中外部知识检索不切实际时复杂推理的挑战，旨在通过知识外推从现有结构化知识中推断新信息，从而提出SAKE这一强化学习框架。该方法训练大语言模型自主检索和外推知识，使用两个外部知识图谱工具：实体组构建和跨组三元组检索，通过三回合滚动进行类比关联推理，并采用GRPO和课程奖励进行端到端优化。实验结果表明，经SAKE微调的Qwen2.5-7B模型在生物医学和常识基准测试上均优于GPT-3.5-Turbo（分别为75.4%对70.1%和81.3%对74.7%），同时令牌使用量减少超过90%，证明小型开放权重模型可通过强化学习与适当工具学习有效推理。
Residuals-based Offline Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Qing Zhu, Xian Yu
First: 2026-04-01T20:38:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T20:38:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning (RL) has received increasing attention for learning policies from previously collected data without interaction with the real environment, which is particularly important in high-stakes applications. While a growing body of work has developed offline RL algorithms, these methods often rely on restrictive assumptions about data coverage and suffer from distribution shift. In this paper, we propose a residuals-based offline RL framework for general state and action spaces. Specifically, we define a residuals-based Bellman optimality operator that explicitly incorporates estimation error in learning transition dynamics into policy optimization by leveraging empirical residuals. We show that this Bellman operator is a contraction mapping and identify conditions under which its fixed point is asymptotically optimal and possesses finite-sample guarantees. We further develop a residuals-based offline deep Q-learning (DQN) algorithm. Using a stochastic CartPole environment, we demonstrate the effectiveness of our residuals-based offline DQN algorithm.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于残差的离线强化学习
离线强化学习（RL）通过从先前收集的数据中学习策略而无需与真实环境交互，正受到越来越多的关注，这在高风险应用中尤为重要。尽管已有大量研究开发了离线RL算法，但这些方法通常依赖于对数据覆盖范围的限制性假设，并受到分布偏移的影响。本文提出了一种适用于一般状态和动作空间的基于残差的离线RL框架。具体而言，我们定义了一个基于残差的贝尔曼最优算子，该算子通过利用经验残差，将学习转移动态时的估计误差显式地纳入策略优化中。我们证明该贝尔曼算子是压缩映射，并确定了其不动点具有渐近最优性和有限样本保证的条件。我们进一步开发了一种基于残差的离线深度Q学习（DQN）算法。通过随机CartPole环境的实验，我们验证了所提出的基于残差的离线DQN算法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenges of offline reinforcement learning, such as restrictive data coverage assumptions and distribution shift, by proposing a residuals-based framework that incorporates estimation errors of transition dynamics into policy optimization. The method introduces a residuals-based Bellman optimality operator, proven to be a contraction mapping with asymptotic optimality and finite-sample guarantees under certain conditions, and develops a residuals-based deep Q-learning algorithm. Experimental results in a stochastic CartPole environment demonstrate the effectiveness of this approach.
本文针对离线强化学习中数据覆盖假设限制和分布偏移等问题，提出了一种基于残差的框架，将转移动态的估计误差纳入策略优化。该方法定义了一个基于残差的贝尔曼最优算子，被证明在特定条件下是压缩映射，具有渐近最优性和有限样本保证，并开发了基于残差的深度Q学习算法。在随机CartPole环境中的实验结果表明了该方法的有效性。
RIFT: A RubrIc Failure Mode Taxonomy and Automated Diagnostics
Authors: Zhengyang Qi, Charles Dickens, Derek Pham, Amanda Dsouza, Armin Parchami, Frederic Sala, Paroma Varma
First: 2026-04-01T20:34:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T20:34:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Rubric-based evaluation is widely used in LLM benchmarks and training pipelines for open-ended, less verifiable tasks. While prior work has demonstrated the effectiveness of rubrics using downstream signals such as reinforcement learning outcomes, there remains no principled way to diagnose rubric quality issues from such aggregated or downstream signals alone. To address this gap, we introduce RIFT: RubrIc Failure mode Taxonomy, a taxonomy for systematically characterizing failure modes in rubric composition and design. RIFT consists of eight failure modes organized into three high-level categories: Reliability Failures, Content Validity Failures, and Consequential Validity Failures. RIFT is developed using grounded theory by iteratively annotating rubrics drawn from five diverse benchmarks spanning general instruction following, code generation, creative writing, and expert-level deep research, until no new failure modes are identified. We evaluate the consistency of the taxonomy by measuring agreement among independent human annotators, observing fair agreement overall (87% pairwise agreement and 0.64 average Cohen's kappa). Finally, to support scalable diagnosis, we propose automated rubric quality metrics and show that they align with human failure-mode annotations, achieving up to 0.86 F1.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RIFT：一种基于量规的故障模式分类与自动化诊断框架
基于量规的评估在大型语言模型的开放式、难验证任务基准和训练流程中广泛应用。尽管先前研究已通过强化学习结果等下游信号验证了量规的有效性，但仅从聚合或下游信号中诊断量规质量问题仍缺乏系统性方法。为此，我们提出RIFT：量规故障模式分类法，用于系统化描述量规构建与设计中的故障模式。RIFT包含八大故障模式，归为三大高层类别：可靠性故障、内容效度故障与后果效度故障。该分类法基于扎根理论开发，通过迭代标注来自五大跨领域基准（涵盖通用指令遵循、代码生成、创意写作及专家级深度研究）的量规直至无新增故障模式。我们通过测量独立标注者间一致性评估分类法的可靠性，整体达到中等一致性（87%成对一致率，平均科恩卡帕系数0.64）。最后，为支持规模化诊断，我们提出自动化量规质量指标，并证明其与人工故障模式标注高度吻合，最高F1分数达0.86。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is the lack of principled diagnostic tools for assessing the quality of rubrics used in LLM evaluation, despite their widespread use in benchmarks and training. The method introduces RIFT, a taxonomy developed via grounded theory from five diverse benchmarks, which categorizes eight rubric failure modes into three high-level categories: Reliability, Content Validity, and Consequential Validity. Main experimental results show fair inter-annotator agreement (87% pairwise agreement, 0.64 average Cohen's kappa) and that automated metrics align with human annotations, achieving up to 0.86 F1 score for scalable diagnosis.
本研究的动机在于，尽管评分标准在大型语言模型评估中广泛应用，但缺乏系统性的诊断工具来评估其质量。方法上提出了RIFT分类法，通过扎根理论从五个多样化基准中归纳出八个评分标准失效模式，分为可靠性失效、内容有效性失效和后果有效性失效三大类。主要实验结果显示了公平的标注者间一致性（87%的成对一致性和0.64的平均科恩卡帕系数），且自动化指标与人工标注相吻合，F1分数最高达0.86，支持可扩展的诊断。
Malliavin Calculus for Counterfactual Gradient Estimation in Adaptive Inverse Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Vikram Krishnamurthy, Luke Snow
First: 2026-04-01T19:56:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T19:56:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Inverse reinforcement learning (IRL) recovers the loss function of a forward learner from its observed responses adaptive IRL aims to reconstruct the loss function of a forward learner by passively observing its gradients as it performs reinforcement learning (RL). This paper proposes a novel passive Langevin-based algorithm that achieves adaptive IRL. The key difficulty in adaptive IRL is that the required gradients in the passive algorithm are counterfactual, that is, they are conditioned on events of probability zero under the forward learner's trajectory. Therefore, naive Monte Carlo estimators are prohibitively inefficient, and kernel smoothing, though common, suffers from slow convergence. We overcome this by employing Malliavin calculus to efficiently estimate the required counterfactual gradients. We reformulate the counterfactual conditioning as a ratio of unconditioned expectations involving Malliavin quantities, thus recovering standard estimation rates. We derive the necessary Malliavin derivatives and their adjoint Skorohod integral formulations for a general Langevin structure, and provide a concrete algorithmic approach which exploits these for counterfactual gradient estimation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：自适应逆强化学习中反事实梯度估计的Malliavin微积分方法
逆强化学习（IRL）通过观察前向学习者的响应来恢复其损失函数，而自适应IRL旨在通过被动观察前向学习者在执行强化学习（RL）时的梯度来重构其损失函数。本文提出了一种新颖的基于被动Langevin的算法，实现了自适应IRL。自适应IRL的关键难点在于被动算法所需的梯度是反事实的，即它们以前向学习者轨迹中概率为零的事件为条件。因此，朴素的蒙特卡洛估计器效率极低，而常用的核平滑方法则收敛缓慢。我们通过应用Malliavin微积分来高效估计所需的反事实梯度，克服了这一难题。将反事实条件重构为涉及Malliavin量的无条件期望之比，从而恢复标准估计速率。我们推导了适用于一般Langevin结构的必要Malliavin导数及其伴随Skorohod积分形式，并提供了一种利用这些进行反事实梯度估计的具体算法方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of adaptive inverse reinforcement learning (IRL), which aims to reconstruct a forward learner's loss function by observing its gradient responses during reinforcement learning. The key difficulty lies in efficiently estimating counterfactual gradients—those conditioned on zero-probability events under the forward learner's trajectory—where naive Monte Carlo methods are inefficient and kernel smoothing suffers from slow convergence. To overcome this, the authors propose a novel passive Langevin-based algorithm that employs Malliavin calculus to reformulate the counterfactual conditioning as a ratio of unconditioned expectations involving Malliavin derivatives and Skorohod integrals, thereby achieving standard estimation rates. The main experimental results demonstrate that this approach enables efficient counterfactual gradient estimation, offering a concrete algorithmic solution with improved convergence compared to traditional methods.
本文针对自适应逆强化学习（IRL）中的挑战，即通过观察前向学习者在强化学习过程中的梯度响应来重建其损失函数。核心难点在于高效估计反事实梯度——这些梯度基于前向学习者轨迹中概率为零的事件条件化，其中朴素蒙特卡洛方法效率低下，而核平滑方法收敛缓慢。为解决此问题，作者提出了一种新颖的被动朗之万算法，利用Malliavin微积分将反事实条件化重新表述为涉及Malliavin导数和Skorohod积分的无条件期望比值，从而实现了标准估计速率。主要实验结果表明，该方法能够高效进行反事实梯度估计，提供了一种具体的算法解决方案，相比传统方法具有更好的收敛性。
Efficient and Principled Scientific Discovery through Bayesian Optimization: A Tutorial
Authors: Zhongwei Yu, Rasul Tutunov, Alexandre Max Maraval, Zikai Xie, Zhenzhi Tan, Jiankang Wang, Zijing Li, Liangliang Xu, Qi Yang, Jun Jiang, Sanzhong Luo, Zhenxiao Guo, Haitham Bou-Ammar, Jun Wang
First: 2026-04-01T19:14:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T19:14:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional scientific discovery relies on an iterative hypothesise-experiment-refine cycle that has driven progress for centuries, but its intuitive, ad-hoc implementation often wastes resources, yields inefficient designs, and misses critical insights. This tutorial presents Bayesian Optimisation (BO), a principled probability-driven framework that formalises and automates this core scientific cycle. BO uses surrogate models (e.g., Gaussian processes) to model empirical observations as evolving hypotheses, and acquisition functions to guide experiment selection, balancing exploitation of known knowledge and exploration of uncharted domains to eliminate guesswork and manual trial-and-error. We first frame scientific discovery as an optimisation problem, then unpack BO's core components, end-to-end workflows, and real-world efficacy via case studies in catalysis, materials science, organic synthesis, and molecule discovery. We also cover critical technical extensions for scientific applications, including batched experimentation, heteroscedasticity, contextual optimisation, and human-in-the-loop integration. Tailored for a broad audience, this tutorial bridges AI advances in BO with practical natural science applications, offering tiered content to empower cross-disciplinary researchers to design more efficient experiments and accelerate principled scientific discovery.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过贝叶斯优化实现高效且原理驱动的科学发现：教程
传统科学发现依赖于历经数百年推动进步的假设-实验-优化的迭代循环，但其依赖直觉的临时性实施常导致资源浪费、设计低效并错失关键洞见。本教程介绍贝叶斯优化（BO）——一种将这一核心科学循环形式化与自动化的概率驱动原理框架。BO使用代理模型（如高斯过程）将经验观测建模为动态演化的假设，并通过采集函数指导实验选择，在已知知识的利用与未知领域的探索间取得平衡，从而消除猜测与手动试错。我们首先将科学发现构建为优化问题，继而通过催化、材料科学、有机合成及分子发现等案例研究，系统解析BO的核心组件、端到端工作流及实际效能。教程还涵盖面向科学应用的关键技术扩展，包括批量实验、异方差性、上下文优化及人机协同集成。本教程面向广泛受众，将BO的人工智能前沿进展与自然科学实践应用相衔接，通过分层内容设计助力跨学科研究者设计更高效的实验，加速原理驱动的科学发现进程。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency and ad-hoc nature of traditional scientific discovery cycles, this tutorial introduces Bayesian Optimization (BO) as a principled, probability-driven framework to formalize and automate the hypothesize-experiment-refine process. The method employs surrogate models like Gaussian processes to represent evolving hypotheses and acquisition functions to intelligently select experiments, balancing exploration and exploitation to minimize manual trial-and-error. Experimental results from case studies in catalysis, materials science, organic synthesis, and molecule discovery demonstrate BO's real-world efficacy in accelerating discovery, supported by technical extensions for batched experimentation, heteroscedasticity, and human-in-the-loop integration.
本文针对传统科学发现循环效率低下且依赖直觉的问题，提出贝叶斯优化作为一种基于概率的原则性框架，以形式化和自动化假设-实验-优化的核心过程。该方法使用高斯过程等代理模型来建模经验观察作为动态假设，并利用采集函数指导实验选择，平衡已知知识的利用与未知领域的探索，从而消除猜测和手动试错。通过在催化、材料科学、有机合成和分子发现等领域的案例研究，实验结果表明贝叶斯优化能有效加速科学发现，并涵盖了批量实验、异方差性、上下文优化和人机交互集成等关键技术扩展。
Safe learning-based control via function-based uncertainty quantification
Authors: Abdullah Tokmak, Toni Karvonen, Thomas B. Schön, Dominik Baumann
First: 2026-04-01T17:23:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T17:23:30+00:00
Comments: Under review for CDC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Uncertainty quantification is essential when deploying learning-based control methods in safety-critical systems. This is commonly realized by constructing uncertainty tubes that enclose the unknown function of interest, e.g., the reward and constraint functions or the underlying dynamics model, with high probability. However, existing approaches for uncertainty quantification typically rely on restrictive assumptions on the unknown function, such as known bounds on functional norms or Lipschitz constants, and struggle with discontinuities. In this paper, we model the unknown function as a random function from which independent and identically distributed realizations can be generated, and construct uncertainty tubes via the scenario approach that hold with high probability and rely solely on the sampled realizations. We integrate these uncertainty tubes into a safe Bayesian optimization algorithm, which we then use to safely tune control parameters on a real Furuta pendulum.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于函数不确定性量化的安全学习控制
在安全关键系统中部署基于学习的控制方法时，不确定性量化至关重要。通常通过构建高概率覆盖目标未知函数（如奖励函数、约束函数或底层动力学模型）的不确定性管来实现。然而，现有不确定性量化方法通常依赖于对未知函数的严格假设，例如函数范数或Lipschitz常数的已知界限，且难以处理不连续性。本文中，我们将未知函数建模为可生成独立同分布实现样本的随机函数，并基于场景方法构建仅依赖采样实现的高概率不确定性管。我们将这些不确定性管集成至安全贝叶斯优化算法中，并应用于真实Furuta摆的控制参数安全调优。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for reliable uncertainty quantification in safety-critical learning-based control systems, this paper proposes a method that models unknown functions as random processes from which independent realizations can be sampled, constructing high-probability uncertainty tubes via the scenario approach without relying on restrictive assumptions like Lipschitz continuity. The approach is integrated into a safe Bayesian optimization framework, and experimental results demonstrate its successful application in safely tuning control parameters on a real Furuta pendulum.
本文针对安全关键学习控制系统中不确定性量化的需求，提出了一种方法，将未知函数建模为可从中采样独立实现的随机过程，通过场景方法构建高概率不确定性区间，无需依赖利普希茨连续性等限制性假设。该方法被集成到安全贝叶斯优化框架中，实验结果表明，其在真实Furuta摆上安全调整控制参数的应用取得了成功。
Deep Reinforcement Learning for Robotic Manipulation under Distribution Shift with Bounded Extremum Seeking
Authors: Shaifalee Saxena, Rafael Fierro, Alexander Scheinker
First: 2026-04-01T16:59:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T16:59:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning has shown strong performance in robotic manipulation, but learned policies often degrade in performance when test conditions differ from the training distribution. This limitation is especially important in contact-rich tasks such as pushing and pick-and-place, where changes in goals, contact conditions, or robot dynamics can drive the system out-of-distribution at inference time. In this paper, we investigate a hybrid controller that combines reinforcement learning with bounded extremum seeking to improve robustness under such conditions. In the proposed approach, deep deterministic policy gradient (DDPG) policies are trained under standard conditions on the robotic pushing and pick-and-place tasks, and are then combined with bounded ES during deployment. The RL policy provides fast manipulation behavior, while bounded ES ensures robustness of the overall controller to time variations when operating conditions depart from those seen during training. The resulting controller is evaluated under several out-of-distribution settings, including time-varying goals and spatially varying friction patches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于有界极值搜索的分布偏移下机器人操作深度强化学习
强化学习在机器人操作任务中表现出色，但训练策略在测试条件与训练分布不同时性能常会下降。这一局限在接触密集型任务（如推物和抓放）中尤为突出，目标、接触条件或机器人动力学的变化均可能在推理时使系统偏离分布。本文研究一种混合控制器，将强化学习与有界极值搜索结合，以提升此类条件下的鲁棒性。所提方法中，深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）策略在标准条件下针对机器人推物和抓放任务进行训练，并在部署时与有界极值搜索结合。强化学习策略提供快速操作行为，而有界极值搜索确保整体控制器在运行条件偏离训练场景时对时变干扰的鲁棒性。该控制器在多种分布偏移场景下进行评估，包括时变目标和空间变化的摩擦区域。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the performance degradation of reinforcement learning policies in robotic manipulation when faced with distribution shifts at test time, such as changes in goals or contact conditions. The proposed method combines a deep deterministic policy gradient (DDPG) policy, trained under standard conditions, with a bounded extremum seeking (ES) controller during deployment to enhance robustness. Experimental results on pushing and pick-and-place tasks demonstrate that the hybrid controller maintains performance under out-of-distribution settings, including time-varying goals and spatially varying friction patches, by leveraging RL for fast manipulation and bounded ES for adaptation to variations.
本文针对强化学习策略在机器人操作中因测试时分布偏移（如目标或接触条件变化）导致的性能下降问题，提出了一种解决方案。该方法将标准条件下训练的深度确定性策略梯度（DDPG）策略与有界极值搜索（ES）控制器在部署时结合，以提高鲁棒性。在推动和抓放任务上的实验结果表明，该混合控制器在分布外设置（包括时变目标和空间变化的摩擦区域）下能保持性能，通过强化学习实现快速操作，并利用有界极值搜索适应环境变化。
Approximating Pareto Frontiers in Stochastic Multi-Objective Optimization via Hashing and Randomization
Authors: Jinzhao Li, Nan Jiang, Yexiang Xue
First: 2026-04-01T16:24:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T16:24:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Stochastic Multi-Objective Optimization (SMOO) is critical for decision-making trading off multiple potentially conflicting objectives in uncertain environments. SMOO aims at identifying the Pareto frontier, which contains all mutually non-dominating decisions. The problem is highly intractable due to the embedded probabilistic inference, such as computing the marginal, posterior probabilities, or expectations. Existing methods, such as scalarization, sample average approximation, and evolutionary algorithms, either offer arbitrarily loose approximations or may incur prohibitive computational costs. We propose XOR-SMOO, a novel algorithm that with probability $1-δ$, obtains $γ$-approximate Pareto frontiers ($γ>1$) for SMOO by querying an SAT oracle poly-log times in $γ$ and $δ$. A $γ$-approximate Pareto frontier is only below the true frontier by a fixed, multiplicative factor $γ$. Thus, XOR-SMOO solves highly intractable SMOO problems (\#P-hard) with only queries to SAT oracles while obtaining tight, constant factor approximation guarantees. Experiments on real-world road network strengthening and supply chain design problems demonstrate that XOR-SMOO outperforms several baselines in identifying Pareto frontiers that have higher objective values, better coverage of the optimal solutions, and the solutions found are more evenly distributed. Overall, XOR-SMOO significantly enhanced the practicality and reliability of SMOO solvers.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于哈希与随机化的随机多目标优化帕累托前沿逼近方法
随机多目标优化（SMOO）在不确定环境下权衡多个潜在冲突目标时至关重要，其核心在于识别包含所有互不支配决策的帕累托前沿。由于涉及概率推断（如计算边缘概率、后验概率或期望），该问题具有高度难解性。现有方法（如标量化、样本平均逼近和进化算法）要么提供任意宽松的近似解，要么计算成本过高。本文提出XOR-SMOO算法，以概率$1-δ$通过查询SAT预言机poly-log次数（关于$γ$和$δ$），获得SMOO的$γ$近似帕累托前沿（$γ>1$）。$γ$近似前沿仅以固定乘积因子$γ$低于真实前沿，因此XOR-SMOO仅需查询SAT预言机即可解决高度难解的SMOO问题（#P难），并获得紧致的常数因子近似保证。在现实道路网络强化和供应链设计问题上的实验表明，XOR-SMOO在帕累托前沿识别方面优于多种基线方法：所得前沿具有更高目标函数值、更优解空间覆盖度，且解分布更均匀。总体而言，XOR-SMOO显著提升了SMOO求解器的实用性与可靠性。

The paper addresses the intractability of Stochastic Multi-Objective Optimization (SMOO), where computing exact Pareto frontiers under uncertainty is #P-hard, and existing methods often yield loose approximations or high computational costs. The proposed XOR-SMOO algorithm efficiently approximates Pareto frontiers with a constant multiplicative factor γ by making polylogarithmic queries to an SAT oracle, providing probabilistic guarantees (1-δ) of approximation quality. Experimental results on real-world problems like road network strengthening and supply chain design show that XOR-SMOO outperforms baselines by achieving higher objective values, better coverage of optimal solutions, and more evenly distributed Pareto solutions, thereby enhancing the practicality and reliability of SMOO solvers.
本文针对随机多目标优化（SMOO）中帕累托前沿计算在不确定性下难以处理（#P难）的问题，现有方法常产生松散近似或计算成本过高。提出的XOR-SMOO算法通过向SAT预言机进行多对数次查询，以常数乘法因子γ高效近似帕累托前沿，并提供概率保证（1-δ）的近似质量。在道路网络加固和供应链设计等实际问题的实验中，XOR-SMOO优于基线方法，获得了更高的目标值、更优的解决方案覆盖度以及更均匀分布的帕累托解，从而显著提升了SMOO求解器的实用性和可靠性。
Adversarial Attacks in AI-Driven RAN Slicing: SLA Violations and Recovery
Authors: Deemah H. Tashman, Soumaya Cherkaoui
First: 2026-04-01T15:54:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T15:54:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Next-generation (NextG) cellular networks are designed to support emerging applications with diverse data rate and latency requirements, such as immersive multimedia services and large-scale Internet of Things deployments. A key enabling mechanism is radio access network (RAN) slicing, which dynamically partitions radio resources into virtual resource blocks to efficiently serve heterogeneous traffic classes, including enhanced mobile broadband (eMBB), massive machine-type communications (mMTC), and ultra-reliable low-latency communications (URLLC). In this paper, we study the impact of adversarial attacks on AI-driven RAN slicing decisions, where a budget-constrained adversary selectively jams slice transmissions to bias deep reinforcement learning (DRL)-based resource allocation, and quantify the resulting service level agreement (SLA) violations and post-attack recovery behavior. Our results indicate that budget-constrained adversarial jamming can induce severe and slice-dependent steady-state SLA violations. Moreover, the DRL agent's reward converges toward the clean baseline only after a non-negligible recovery period.

标题：AI驱动的RAN切片中的对抗性攻击：SLA违规与恢复
下一代蜂窝网络旨在支持具有多样化数据速率和延迟需求的新兴应用，如沉浸式多媒体服务和大规模物联网部署。其关键使能机制是无线接入网络切片，该技术动态划分无线资源为虚拟资源块，以高效服务异构流量类别，包括增强移动宽带、大规模机器类通信和超可靠低延迟通信。本文研究了对抗性攻击对AI驱动的RAN切片决策的影响：预算受限的对手通过选择性干扰切片传输，使基于深度强化学习的资源分配产生偏差，并量化了由此导致的服务水平协议违规及攻击后恢复行为。结果表明，预算受限的对抗性干扰可引发严重且依赖切片类型的稳态SLA违规。此外，深度强化学习智能体的奖励仅在经历不可忽略的恢复期后，才收敛至无攻击基线水平。

The method involves a budget-constrained adversary that selectively jams slice transmissions to bias a deep reinforcement learning (DRL) agent responsible for resource allocation, with the impact measured in terms of service level agreement (SLA) violations and recovery behavior. Experimental results show that such jamming can cause severe, slice-dependent steady-state SLA violations, and the DRL agent's reward only converges back to the clean baseline after a significant recovery period.

Ego-Foresight: Self-supervised Learning of Agent-Aware Representations for Improved RL
Authors: Manuel Serra Nunes, Atabak Dehban, Yiannis Demiris, José Santos-Victor
First: 2024-05-27T13:32:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T15:51:54+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 8 figures, conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite the significant advances in Deep Reinforcement Learning (RL) observed in the last decade, the amount of training experience necessary to learn effective policies remains one of the primary concerns in both simulated and real environments. Looking to solve this issue, previous work has shown that improved efficiency can be achieved by separately modeling the agent and environment, but usually requires a supervisory signal. In contrast to RL, humans can perfect a new skill from a small number of trials and often do so without a supervisory signal, making neuroscientific studies of human development a valuable source of inspiration for RL. In particular, we explore the idea of motor prediction, which states that humans develop an internal model of themselves and of the consequences that their motor commands have on the immediate sensory inputs. Our insight is that the movementofthe agent provides a cue that allows the duality between the agent and environment to be learned. To instantiate this idea, we present Ego-Foresight (EF), a self-supervised method for disentangling agent information based on motion and prediction. Our main finding is that, when used as an auxiliary task in feature learning, self-supervised agent awareness improves the sample-efficiency and performance of the underlying RL algorithm. To test our approach, we study the ability of EF to predict agent movement and disentangle agent information. Then, we integrate EF with model-free and model based RL algorithms to solve simulated control tasks, showing improved sample-efficiency and performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Ego-Foresight：基于自监督学习的智能体感知表征提升强化学习性能
尽管深度强化学习在过去十年取得显著进展，但在模拟和真实环境中，学习有效策略所需的训练经验量仍是核心挑战。为解决此问题，先前研究表明通过分别建模智能体与环境可提升效率，但通常需要监督信号。与强化学习不同，人类仅需少量尝试即可掌握新技能，且常无需监督信号，这使得人类发展的神经科学研究成为强化学习的重要灵感来源。我们特别探索运动预测理论——该理论认为人类会建立自身内部模型，并理解其运动指令对即时感官输入的影响。我们的核心观点是：智能体的运动轨迹提供了学习智能体与环境二元对偶性的线索。基于此，我们提出Ego-Foresight（EF）——一种基于运动预测的自监督解耦智能体信息方法。主要发现表明：将自监督的智能体感知作为特征学习的辅助任务，可提升基础强化学习算法的样本效率与性能。我们通过EF预测智能体运动和解耦智能体信息的能力验证方法，并将其与无模型及基于模型的强化学习算法结合解决模拟控制任务，实验证明其能显著提升样本效率与性能。

Motivated by the need to improve the sample efficiency of deep reinforcement learning (RL) and inspired by human motor prediction, which allows learning internal models without supervision, this paper introduces Ego-Foresight (EF), a self-supervised method that disentangles agent-aware representations by predicting agent motion. The method leverages the agent's own movement as a cue to separate agent and environment information, serving as an auxiliary task during feature learning. Experimental results demonstrate that EF effectively predicts agent movement and disentangles agent information, and when integrated with model-free and model-based RL algorithms, it leads to improved sample efficiency and performance on simulated control tasks.
本文旨在提升深度强化学习的样本效率，其动机源于人类无需监督即可通过运动预测学习内部模型的能力。为此，论文提出了Ego-Foresight（EF）这一自监督方法，该方法通过预测智能体运动来解耦智能体感知表征，利用智能体自身运动作为线索区分智能体与环境信息，并将其作为特征学习的辅助任务。实验结果表明，EF能有效预测智能体运动并解耦智能体信息，当与无模型和基于模型的强化学习算法结合时，在模拟控制任务中提高了样本效率和性能。
Query-Conditioned Evidential Keyframe Sampling for MLLM-Based Long-Form Video Understanding
Authors: Yiheng Wang, Lichen Zhu, Yueqian Lin, Yudong Liu, Jingyang Zhang, Hai "Helen" Li, Yiran Chen
First: 2026-04-01T15:02:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T15:02:50+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown strong performance on video question answering, but their application to long-form videos is constrained by limited context length and computational cost, making keyframe sampling essential. Existing approaches typically rely on semantic relevance or reinforcement learning, which either fail to capture evidential clues or suffer from inefficient combinatorial optimization. In this work, we propose an evidence-driven keyframe sampling framework grounded in information bottleneck theory. We formulate keyframe selection as maximizing the conditional mutual information between selected frames and the query, providing a principled objective that reflects each frame's contribution to answering the question. To make this objective tractable, we exploit its structure to derive a decomposed optimization that reduces subset selection to independent frame-level scoring. We further introduce a query-conditioned evidence scoring network trained with a contrastive objective to estimate evidential importance efficiently. Experiments on long-form video understanding benchmarks show that our method consistently outperforms prior sampling strategies under strict token budgets, while significantly improving training efficiency.

Focal plane wavefront control with model-based reinforcement learning
Authors: Jalo Nousiainen, Iremsu Taskin, Markus Kasper, Gilles Orban De Xivry, Olivier Absil
First: 2026-04-01T14:55:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T14:55:15+00:00
Comments: 13 pages, 11 figures accepted by A&A
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The direct imaging of potentially habitable exoplanets is one prime science case for high-contrast imaging instruments on extremely large telescopes. Most such exoplanets orbit close to their host stars, where their observation is limited by fast-moving atmospheric speckles and quasi-static non-common-path aberrations (NCPA). Conventional NCPA correction methods often use mechanical mirror probes, which compromise performance during operation. This work presents machine-learning-based NCPA control methods that automatically detect and correct both dynamic and static NCPA errors by leveraging sequential phase diversity. We extend previous work in reinforcement learning for AO to focal plane control. A new model-based RL algorithm, Policy Optimization for NCPAs (PO4NCPA), interprets the focal-plane image as input data and, through sequential phase diversity, determines phase corrections that optimize both non-coronagraphic and post-coronagraphic PSFs without prior system knowledge. Further, we demonstrate the effectiveness of this approach by numerically simulating static NCPA errors on a ground-based telescope and an infrared imager affected by water-vapor-induced seeing (dynamic NCPAs). Simulations show that PO4NCPA robustly compensates static and dynamic NCPAs. In static cases, it achieves near-optimal focal-plane light suppression with a coronagraph and near-optimal Strehl without one. With dynamics NCPA, it matches the performance of the modal least-squares reconstruction combined with a 1-step delay integrator in these metrics. The method remains effective for the ELT pupil, vector vortex coronagraph, and under photon and background noise. PO4NCPA is model-free and can be directly applied to standard imaging as well as to any coronagraph. Its sub-millisecond inference times and performance also make it suitable for real-time low-order correction of atmospheric turbulence beyond HCI.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于模型强化学习的焦平面波前控制
直接成像潜在宜居系外行星是超大型望远镜高对比度成像仪器的核心科学目标之一。多数此类系外行星围绕宿主恒星近距离运行，其观测受限于快速移动的大气散斑和准静态非共路像差（NCPA）。传统NCPA校正方法常采用机械镜面探针，会在运行期间影响性能。本研究提出基于机器学习的NCPA控制方法，通过利用序列相位多样性自动检测并校正动态与静态NCPA误差。我们将强化学习在自适应光学中的先前工作扩展至焦平面控制。新型基于模型的强化学习算法——NCPA策略优化算法（PO4NCPA）将焦平面图像作为输入数据，通过序列相位多样性确定相位校正量，在无需先验系统知识的情况下优化非日冕仪与后日冕仪点扩散函数。此外，我们通过数值模拟地基望远镜受水汽视宁度影响（动态NCPA）的红外成像仪静态NCPA误差，验证了该方法的有效性。模拟显示PO4NCPA能稳健补偿静态与动态NCPA：静态场景中，使用日冕仪时可实现近最优焦平面光抑制，无日冕仪时获得近最优斯特列尔比；动态NCPA场景中，其性能与模态最小二乘重建结合单步延迟积分器相当。该方法对ELT孔径、矢量涡旋日冕仪及光子与背景噪声场景仍保持有效。PO4NCPA无需模型，可直接应用于标准成像及任意日冕仪系统，其亚毫秒级推理时间与性能也使其适用于高对比度成像之外的大气湍流实时低阶校正。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the challenge of directly imaging habitable exoplanets, which is hindered by fast-moving atmospheric speckles and quasi-static non-common-path aberrations (NCPA) that degrade image contrast near stars. The method introduces a model-based reinforcement learning algorithm called PO4NCPA, which uses sequential phase diversity to interpret focal-plane images and determine phase corrections without prior system knowledge, enabling automatic correction of both static and dynamic NCPAs. Experimental simulations on ground-based telescopes show that PO4NCPA robustly compensates these errors, achieving near-optimal focal-plane light suppression with a coronagraph and high Strehl ratios without one, matching conventional methods in dynamic cases, and remaining effective under various noise conditions and telescope configurations.
本文的研究动机是直接成像宜居系外行星面临的主要挑战，即由快速移动的大气散斑和准静态非共路像差（NCPA）导致的图像对比度下降。方法上提出了一种基于模型的强化学习算法PO4NCPA，它利用序列相位多样性分析焦平面图像，无需先验系统知识即可确定相位校正，从而自动修正静态和动态NCPA。实验模拟结果表明，该算法能稳健补偿这些像差，在使用日冕仪时实现接近最优的焦平面光抑制，在不使用时获得高斯特列尔比，在动态情况下与传统方法性能相当，并在多种噪声条件和望远镜配置下保持有效。
Flow-based Policy With Distributional Reinforcement Learning in Trajectory Optimization
Authors: Ruijie Hao, Longfei Zhang, Yang Dai, Yang Ma, Xingxing Liang, Guangquan Cheng
First: 2026-04-01T14:47:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T14:47:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has proven highly effective in addressing complex control and decision-making tasks. However, in most traditional RL algorithms, the policy is typically parameterized as a diagonal Gaussian distribution, which constrains the policy from capturing multimodal distributions, making it difficult to cover the full range of optimal solutions in multi-solution problems, and the return is reduced to a mean value, losing its multimodal nature and thus providing insufficient guidance for policy updates. In response to these problems, we propose a RL algorithm termed flow-based policy with distributional RL (FP-DRL). This algorithm models the policy using flow matching, which offers both computational efficiency and the capacity to fit complex distributions. Additionally, it employs a distributional RL approach to model and optimize the entire return distribution, thereby more effectively guiding multimodal policy updates and improving agent performance. Experimental trails on MuJoCo benchmarks demonstrate that the FP-DRL algorithm achieves state-of-the-art (SOTA) performance in most MuJoCo control tasks while exhibiting superior representation capability of the flow policy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于流策略与分布强化学习的轨迹优化方法
强化学习（RL）在解决复杂控制与决策任务方面已展现出显著成效。然而，传统RL算法通常将策略参数化为对角高斯分布，这限制了策略捕捉多模态分布的能力，难以覆盖多解问题中的全部最优解，且回报被简化为均值，丧失了多模态特性，从而对策略更新的指导不足。针对这些问题，我们提出了一种称为基于流策略的分布强化学习（FP-DRL）算法。该算法通过流匹配对策略进行建模，兼具计算效率与拟合复杂分布的能力。同时，采用分布强化学习方法对完整回报分布进行建模与优化，从而更有效地指导多模态策略更新并提升智能体性能。在MuJoCo基准测试中的实验表明，FP-DRL算法在多数MuJoCo控制任务中实现了最先进的性能，并展现出流策略卓越的表征能力。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work arises from the limitations of traditional reinforcement learning algorithms, which typically use a diagonal Gaussian distribution to parameterize the policy, thereby failing to capture multimodal distributions and reducing returns to a mean value, which inadequately guides policy updates in multi-solution problems. To address this, the authors propose FP-DRL, a method that combines flow matching for policy modeling to efficiently fit complex distributions and distributional reinforcement learning to model the full return distribution, enabling more effective multimodal policy optimization. Experimental results on MuJoCo benchmarks show that FP-DRL achieves state-of-the-art performance in most control tasks and demonstrates superior representation capability of the flow-based policy.
本研究的动机源于传统强化学习算法的局限性，这些算法通常使用对角高斯分布参数化策略，无法捕捉多模态分布，并将回报简化为均值，从而在多解问题中对策略更新的指导不足。为解决这些问题，作者提出了FP-DRL方法，该方法结合流匹配进行策略建模以高效拟合复杂分布，并采用分布式强化学习对完整回报分布进行建模，从而更有效地指导多模态策略优化。在MuJoCo基准测试中的实验结果表明，FP-DRL在大多数控制任务中实现了最先进的性能，并展现了流策略的优越表示能力。
CHEEM: Continual Learning by Reuse, New, Adapt and Skip -- A Hierarchical Exploration-Exploitation Approach
Authors: Chinmay Savadikar, Michelle Dai, Tianfu Wu
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2023-03-14T21:52:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T14:18:35+00:00
Comments: CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
To effectively manage the complexities of real-world dynamic environments, continual learning must incrementally acquire, update, and accumulate knowledge from a stream of tasks of different nature without suffering from catastrophic forgetting of prior knowledge. While this capability is innate to human cognition, it remains a significant challenge for modern deep learning systems. At the heart of this challenge lies the stability-plasticity dilemma: the need to balance leveraging prior knowledge, integrating novel information, and allocating model capacity adaptively based on task complexity and synergy. In this paper, we propose a novel exemplar-free class-incremental continual learning (ExfCCL) framework that addresses these issues through a Hierarchical Exploration-Exploitation (HEE) approach. The core of our method is a HEE-guided efficient neural architecture search (HEE-NAS) that enables a learning-to-adapt backbone via four primitive operations - reuse, new, adapt, and skip - thereby serving as an internal memory that dynamically updates selected components across streaming tasks. To address the task ID inference problem in ExfCCL, we exploit an external memory of task centroids proposed in the prior art. We term our method CHEEM (Continual Hierarchical-Exploration-Exploitation Memory). CHEEM is evaluated on the challenging MTIL and VDD benchmarks using both Tiny and Base Vision Transformers and a proposed holistic Figure-of-Merit (FoM) metric. It significantly outperforms state-of-the-art prompting-based continual learning methods, closely approaching full fine-tuning upper bounds. Furthermore, it learns adaptive model structures tailored to individual tasks in a semantically meaningful way. Our code is available at https://github.com/savadikarc/cheem .
中文标题/摘要
标题：CHEEM：通过复用、新建、适应与跳过的持续学习——一种分层探索-利用方法
为有效应对现实动态环境的复杂性，持续学习需从不同性质的任务流中逐步获取、更新并积累知识，同时避免对先前知识的灾难性遗忘。尽管人类认知天生具备此能力，但对现代深度学习系统而言仍是重大挑战。这一挑战的核心在于稳定性-可塑性困境：需平衡利用先验知识、整合新信息，以及根据任务复杂性与协同性自适应分配模型容量。本文提出一种新颖的无样本类增量持续学习框架，通过分层探索-利用方法解决上述问题。该方法核心为HEE引导的高效神经架构搜索，通过复用、新建、适应与跳过四种基本操作实现自适应主干网络，从而作为内部记忆动态更新跨任务流中的选定组件。针对无样本类增量持续学习中的任务ID推断问题，我们采用现有技术提出的任务质心外部记忆。该方法命名为CHEEM。在MTIL和VDD基准测试中，使用Tiny与Base版Vision Transformer及提出的综合性能指标进行评估，CHEEM显著优于基于提示的先进持续学习方法，接近全微调理论上限，且能以语义有意义的方式学习适应各任务的模型结构。代码已开源：https://github.com/savadikarc/cheem。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of continual learning in dynamic environments, where models must incrementally learn from a stream of tasks without catastrophic forgetting, balancing the stability-plasticity dilemma. The authors propose CHEEM, an exemplar-free class-incremental continual learning framework that employs a Hierarchical Exploration-Exploitation approach to guide neural architecture search, enabling a backbone to adapt via four operations: reuse, new, adapt, and skip, which act as an internal memory. Experimental results on MTIL and VDD benchmarks with Vision Transformers show that CHEEM significantly outperforms state-of-the-art prompting-based methods, nearly matching full fine-tuning upper bounds, while learning adaptive, semantically meaningful model structures per task.
本文针对动态环境中的持续学习挑战，旨在使模型能够从任务流中增量学习而不发生灾难性遗忘，以平衡稳定性与可塑性之间的困境。作者提出了CHEEM，一种无需样本的类增量持续学习框架，采用分层探索-利用方法来指导神经架构搜索，使主干网络通过重用、新建、适应和跳过四种操作进行自适应调整，作为内部记忆动态更新。在MTIL和VDD基准测试中使用视觉变换器的实验结果表明，CHEEM显著优于基于提示的先进持续学习方法，接近全微调的上限性能，同时能针对每个任务学习具有语义意义的自适应模型结构。
Policy Improvement Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Huaiyang Wang, Xiaojie Li, Deqing Wang, Haoyi Zhou, Zixuan Huang, Yaodong Yang, Jianxin Li, Yikun Ban
First: 2026-04-01T13:10:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T13:10:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has become a central post-training paradigm for improving the reasoning capabilities of large language models. Yet existing methods share a common blind spot: they optimize policies based on instantaneous group-level or batch-level statistics without ever verifying whether the resulting update actually improved the model. This open-loop design -- updating in isolation at each step, guided only by within-group (batch) reward signals -- means optimization can drift or collapse with no mechanism to detect and correct these failures. We argue that the missing ingredient is policy improvement feedback: the ability to measure and optimize inter-iteration progress directly. To this end, we introduce Policy Improvement Reinforcement Learning (PIRL), a framework that replaces surrogate reward maximization with the explicit objective of maximizing cumulative policy improvement across iterations, and prove this temporal objective is perfectly aligned with maximizing final task performance. Building on PIRL, we propose Policy Improvement Policy Optimization (PIPO), which implements closed-loop optimization through retrospective verification. At each iteration, PIPO evaluates whether the previous update yielded genuine improvement against a sliding-window historical baseline, then actively reinforces beneficial updates and suppresses the harmful ones -- transforming an open-loop process into a self-correcting one. We provide theoretical analysis showing that PIPO performs ascent on the PIRL objective in expectation, and experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate improved stability and performance over GRPO and its variants.
中文标题/摘要
标题：策略改进强化学习
可验证奖励的强化学习已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的核心后训练范式。然而现有方法存在一个共同的盲点：它们基于瞬时组级或批次级统计优化策略，却从未验证更新是否真正改进了模型。这种开环设计——仅依赖组内奖励信号在每一步独立更新——意味着优化可能漂移或崩溃，且无法检测和修正这些故障。我们认为缺失的关键是策略改进反馈：直接测量和优化迭代间进度的能力。为此，我们提出策略改进强化学习框架，用最大化跨迭代累积策略改进的显式目标替代代理奖励最大化，并证明该时序目标与最大化最终任务性能完全一致。基于此框架，我们进一步提出策略改进策略优化方法，通过回顾性验证实现闭环优化：每次迭代时，该方法基于滑动窗口历史基线评估前次更新是否带来真实改进，进而主动强化有益更新并抑制有害更新，从而将开环过程转化为自校正过程。理论分析表明该方法在期望上遵循策略改进强化学习目标的上升方向，数学推理基准实验也验证了其相比GRPO及其变体具有更好的稳定性和性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of existing reinforcement learning methods for language models, which optimize policies based on batch-level statistics without verifying actual improvement, this paper introduces Policy Improvement Reinforcement Learning (PIRL) to explicitly maximize cumulative policy improvement across iterations. The method, implemented as Policy Improvement Policy Optimization (PIPO), employs closed-loop optimization through retrospective verification, where each update is assessed against a historical baseline to reinforce beneficial changes and suppress harmful ones. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that PIPO achieves improved stability and performance over methods like GRPO, with theoretical analysis confirming its alignment with maximizing final task performance.
针对现有强化学习方法在优化语言模型策略时仅依赖批量统计而未验证实际改进的局限，本文提出了策略改进强化学习（PIRL），旨在显式最大化跨迭代的累积策略改进。该方法通过策略改进策略优化（PIPO）实现，采用基于回顾验证的闭环优化，即根据历史基线评估每次更新，以增强有益更改并抑制有害更改。在数学推理基准测试上的实验结果表明，PIPO相比GRPO等方法具有更好的稳定性和性能，理论分析也证实其与最大化最终任务性能的目标一致。
DreamerAD: Efficient Reinforcement Learning via Latent World Model for Autonomous Driving
Authors: Pengxuan Yang, Yupeng Zheng, Deheng Qian, Zebin Xing, Qichao Zhang, Linbo Wang, Yichen Zhang, Shaoyu Guo, Zhongpu Xia, Qiang Chen, Junyu Han, Lingyun Xu, Yifeng Pan, Dongbin Zhao
First: 2026-03-25T17:57:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T13:02:07+00:00
Comments: authors update
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce DreamerAD, the first latent world model framework that enables efficient reinforcement learning for autonomous driving by compressing diffusion sampling from 100 steps to 1 - achieving 80x speedup while maintaining visual interpretability. Training RL policies on real-world driving data incurs prohibitive costs and safety risks. While existing pixel-level diffusion world models enable safe imagination-based training, they suffer from multi-step diffusion inference latency (2s/frame) that prevents high-frequency RL interaction. Our approach leverages denoised latent features from video generation models through three key mechanisms: (1) shortcut forcing that reduces sampling complexity via recursive multi-resolution step compression, (2) an autoregressive dense reward model operating directly on latent representations for fine-grained credit assignment, and (3) Gaussian vocabulary sampling for GRPO that constrains exploration to physically plausible trajectories. DreamerAD achieves 87.7 EPDMS on NavSim v2, establishing state-of-the-art performance and demonstrating that latent-space RL is effective for autonomous driving.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DreamerAD：基于潜在世界模型的高效自动驾驶强化学习框架

本文提出了DreamerAD框架，其动机在于直接在真实世界自动驾驶数据上训练强化学习策略成本高昂且存在安全风险，而现有像素级扩散世界模型则存在推理延迟问题。该方法采用潜在世界模型，通过捷径强制将扩散采样从100步压缩至1步，在潜在空间中使用自回归密集奖励模型进行细粒度信用分配，并应用高斯词汇采样来约束探索到物理可行的轨迹。实验结果表明，采样速度提升了80倍且保持了视觉可解释性，在NavSim v2基准测试中取得了87.7 EPDMS的最先进性能，证明了潜在空间强化学习在自动驾驶中的有效性。
Incoherence in Goal-Conditioned Autoregressive Models
Authors: Jacek Karwowski, Raymond Douglas
First: 2025-10-08T00:52:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T11:58:51+00:00
Comments: To appear in the Proceedings of the 29th International Conference on Artificial Intelligence and Statistics (AISTATS) 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We investigate mathematically the notion of incoherence: a structural issue with reinforcement learning policies derived by naive goal-conditioning of autoregressive models. We focus on the process of re-training models on their own actions, that is, fine-tuning offline-learned policies with online RL. We prove that it decreases incoherence and leads to an improvement in return, and we aim to characterize the resulting trajectory of policies. By re-framing standard notions of control-as-inference and soft Q learning, we establish a three-way correspondence with two other ways of understanding the iterative re-training process: as folding the posterior into the reward and, in the deterministic case, as decreasing the temperature parameter; the correspondence has computational content via the training-inference trade-off. Through soft-conditioning generative models, we discuss the link between incoherence and the effective horizon.
中文标题/摘要
标题：目标条件自回归模型中的非一致性研究
本文从数学角度探讨了非一致性的概念：这是一种源于对自回归模型进行朴素目标条件化所导出的强化学习策略的结构性问题。我们重点关注模型基于自身动作进行再训练的过程，即通过在线强化学习对离线学习策略进行微调。我们证明了该过程能够降低非一致性并提升回报，旨在刻画由此产生的策略轨迹。通过重构控制即推断与软Q学习的标准概念，我们建立了与理解迭代再训练过程的另外两种方式的三重对应关系：一种是将后验融入奖励函数，另一种在确定性场景下等同于降低温度参数；这种对应关系通过训练-推断权衡体现了计算内涵。借助软条件生成模型，我们进一步讨论了非一致性与有效视野之间的联系。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the structural issue of incoherence in reinforcement learning policies derived from naive goal-conditioning of autoregressive models, particularly during the process of fine-tuning offline-learned policies with online RL. The method re-frames standard notions of control-as-inference and soft Q-learning to establish a three-way correspondence between iterative re-training, folding the posterior into the reward, and decreasing the temperature parameter in deterministic cases. The main experimental results prove that this re-training process decreases incoherence and improves policy return, while also characterizing the resulting policy trajectory and linking incoherence to the effective horizon through soft-conditioned generative models.
本文研究了自回归模型通过简单目标条件化得到的强化学习策略中存在的结构性问题——不连贯性，特别是在使用在线强化学习对离线学习策略进行微调的过程中。该方法通过重新构建控制即推理和软Q学习的标准概念，建立了迭代重新训练、将后验融入奖励以及在确定性情况下降低温度参数这三种理解方式之间的三方对应关系。主要实验结果证明，这种重新训练过程减少了不连贯性并提高了策略回报，同时描述了由此产生的策略轨迹，并通过软条件生成模型将不连贯性与有效视野联系起来。
RefineRL: Advancing Competitive Programming with Self-Refinement Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Shaopeng Fu, Xingxing Zhang, Li Dong, Di Wang, Furu Wei
First: 2026-04-01T11:54:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T11:54:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated strong performance on complex reasoning tasks such as competitive programming (CP), existing methods predominantly focus on single-attempt settings, overlooking their capacity for iterative refinement. In this paper, we present RefineRL, a novel approach designed to unleash the self-refinement capabilities of LLMs for CP problem solving. RefineRL introduces two key innovations: (1) Skeptical-Agent, an iterative self-refinement agent equipped with local execution tools to validate generated solutions against public test cases of CP problems. This agent always maintains a skeptical attitude towards its own outputs and thereby enforces rigorous self-refinement even when validation suggests correctness. (2) A reinforcement learning (RL) solution to incentivize LLMs to self-refine with only standard RLVR data (i.e., problems paired with their verifiable answers). Extensive experiments on Qwen3-4B and Qwen3-4B-2507 demonstrate that our method yields substantial gains: after our RL training, these compact 4B models integrated with the Skeptical-Agent not only outperform much larger 32B models but also approach the single-attempt performance of 235B models. These findings suggest that self-refinement holds considerable promise for scaling LLM reasoning, with significant potential for further advancement.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RefineRL：通过自优化强化学习推进竞技编程
尽管大语言模型（LLMs）在竞技编程（CP）等复杂推理任务中展现出强大性能，现有方法主要聚焦于单次尝试场景，忽视了其迭代优化的潜力。本文提出RefineRL，一种旨在释放LLMs在CP问题求解中自优化能力的新方法。RefineRL包含两项核心创新：（1）Skeptical-Agent——配备本地执行工具的迭代自优化智能体，可通过CP问题的公开测试用例验证生成方案。该智能体始终对自身输出保持审慎态度，即使在验证显示正确时仍执行严格的自优化。（2）采用强化学习（RL）方案激励LLMs仅使用标准RLVR数据（即问题与可验证答案配对）进行自优化。在Qwen3-4B和Qwen3-4B-2507上的大量实验表明，经过RL训练后，集成Skeptical-Agent的紧凑4B模型不仅超越规模更大的32B模型，且接近235B模型的单次尝试性能。这些发现证明自优化对扩展LLM推理能力具有显著潜力，存在广阔的提升空间。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind RefineRL is to enhance large language models' (LLMs) performance in competitive programming by moving beyond single-attempt solutions to leverage iterative self-refinement, a capability often overlooked. The method introduces a Skeptical-Agent that uses local execution tools to validate solutions against public test cases, maintaining a skeptical stance to enforce rigorous self-improvement, and employs reinforcement learning (RL) trained on standard RLVR data to incentivize this refinement process. Experimental results on Qwen3-4B models show that after RL training, these 4B models integrated with the Skeptical-Agent outperform much larger 32B models and approach the single-attempt performance of 235B models, indicating that self-refinement holds significant promise for scaling LLM reasoning.
RefineRL的动机是通过利用迭代自我精炼来提升大型语言模型在竞争性编程中的性能，超越单次尝试的解决方案，这一能力常被忽视。该方法引入了Skeptical-Agent，使用本地执行工具根据公开测试用例验证解决方案，保持怀疑态度以强制执行严格自我改进，并采用基于标准RLVR数据训练的强化学习来激励这一精炼过程。在Qwen3-4B模型上的实验结果表明，经过强化学习训练后，这些4B模型结合Skeptical-Agent不仅超越了更大的32B模型，还接近了235B模型的单次尝试性能，表明自我精炼在扩展LLM推理方面具有显著潜力。
Finding Low Star Discrepancy 3D Kronecker Point Sets Using Algorithm Configuration Techniques
Authors: Imène Ait Abderrahim, Carola Doerr, Martin Durand
First: 2026-04-01T11:51:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T11:51:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The L infinity star discrepancy is a measure for how uniformly a point set is distributed in a given space. Point sets of low star discrepancy are used as designs of experiments, as initial designs for Bayesian optimization algorithms, for quasi-Monte Carlo integration methods, and many other applications. Recent work has shown that classical constructions such as Sobol', Halton, or Hammersley sequences can be outperformed by large margins when considering point sets of fixed sizes rather than their convergence behavior. These results, highly relevant to the aforementioned applications, raise the question of how much existing constructions can be improved through size-specific optimization. In this work, we study this question for the so-called Kronecker construction. Focusing on the 3-dimensional setting, we show that optimizing the two configurable parameters of its construction yields point sets outperforming the state-of-the-art value for sets of at least 500 points. Using the algorithm configuration technique irace, we then derive parameters that yield new state-of-the-art discrepancy values for whole ranges of set sizes.
中文标题/摘要
标题：运用算法配置技术寻找低星差异三维克罗内克点集
L无穷星差异是衡量点集在给定空间中分布均匀性的指标。低星差异点集被广泛应用于实验设计、贝叶斯优化算法的初始设计、拟蒙特卡洛积分方法及其他诸多领域。近期研究表明，在固定点集规模而非收敛行为的考量下，经典构造方法（如Sobol'、Halton或Hammersley序列）的性能可被大幅超越。这些与前述应用高度相关的结果引出一个问题：通过针对特定规模的优化，现有构造方法能获得多大程度的改进？本研究针对所谓的克罗内克构造方法探讨该问题。聚焦三维场景，我们证明通过优化其两个可配置参数，所得点集在至少500点规模上能超越现有最优值。利用算法配置技术irace，我们进一步推导出可为连续规模区间带来全新最优差异值的参数配置。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for highly uniform point sets in applications like experimental design and quasi-Monte Carlo integration, this paper investigates whether optimizing size-specific parameters can improve upon classical low-discrepancy sequences. The method focuses on the Kronecker construction in 3D, using the algorithm configuration tool irace to tune its two configurable parameters for fixed set sizes. Experimental results demonstrate that the optimized parameters produce point sets with lower star discrepancy than state-of-the-art constructions for sets of at least 500 points, achieving new best-known discrepancy values across various size ranges.
本研究旨在为实验设计和拟蒙特卡洛积分等应用寻找高度均匀的点集，探讨通过针对特定规模优化参数能否超越经典低差异序列。方法聚焦于三维Kronecker构造，利用算法配置工具irace对其两个可调参数进行针对固定点集规模的优化。实验结果表明，优化后的参数生成的点集在至少500个点的规模上，其星差异值优于现有最优构造，为多个规模范围创造了新的最低差异记录。
HiMA-Ecom: Enabling Joint Training of Hierarchical Multi-Agent E-commerce Assistants
Authors: Junxing Hu, Ai Han, Haolan Zhan, Pu Wei, Zhiqian Zhang, Yuhang Guo, Jiawei Lu, Zhen Chen, Haoran Li, Zicheng Zhang
First: 2025-06-24T17:59:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T10:25:03+00:00
Comments: 39 pages, 10 figures, under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Hierarchical multi-agent systems based on large language models (LLMs) have become a common paradigm for building AI assistants in vertical domains such as e-commerce, where a master agent coordinates multiple specialized sub-agents. Despite their practical importance, realistic benchmarks for training and evaluating such systems remain scarce, and joint optimization across functionally distinct agents is still challenging. To address this gap, we introduce HiMA-Ecom, the first hierarchical multi-agent benchmark tailored for e-commerce scenarios. HiMA-Ecom contains 22.8K instances, including agent-specific supervised fine-tuning samples with memory and system-level input-output pairs for joint multi-agent reinforcement learning. Building upon it, a joint training method named HiMA-R1 is proposed. It presents Variance-Reduction Group Relative Policy Optimization (VR-GRPO), which employs initial trajectory-based Monte Carlo sampling to mitigate the exponential joint action space and selects informative agent groups for efficient updates based on reward variance. Furthermore, an adaptive memory evolution mechanism that repurposes GRPO rewards as cost-free supervisory signals is designed to eliminate repetitive reasoning and accelerate convergence. Experiments on HiMA-Ecom demonstrate that our method, built upon smaller 3B/7B open-source models, achieves performance comparable to that of larger LLMs, such as DeepSeek-R1, and surpasses DeepSeek-V3 by an average of 6\%.
中文标题/摘要
标题：HiMA-Ecom：实现分层多智能体电商助手的联合训练
基于大语言模型的分层多智能体系统已成为构建电商等垂直领域AI助手的常见范式，其中主智能体协调多个专业子智能体。尽管其具有重要实践意义，但用于训练和评估此类系统的真实基准仍十分稀缺，且跨功能各异智能体的联合优化仍具挑战性。为填补这一空白，我们推出了首个专为电商场景定制的分层多智能体基准——HiMA-Ecom。该基准包含22.8K个实例，涵盖带记忆的智能体专用监督微调样本，以及用于联合多智能体强化学习的系统级输入-输出对。在此基础上，我们提出了名为HiMA-R1的联合训练方法。该方法引入了方差缩减组相对策略优化，利用基于初始轨迹的蒙特卡洛采样缓解指数级联合动作空间，并根据奖励方差选择信息丰富的智能体组以进行高效更新。此外，设计了一种自适应记忆演化机制，将GRPO奖励重新用作无成本监督信号，以消除重复推理并加速收敛。在HiMA-Ecom上的实验表明，基于较小3B/7B开源模型构建的方法，其性能可与DeepSeek-R1等更大规模LLM相媲美，并平均超越DeepSeek-V3达6%。
