The paper introduces HiMA-Ecom, a benchmark designed to address the scarcity of realistic training and evaluation datasets for hierarchical multi-agent AI assistants in e-commerce, where a master agent coordinates specialized sub-agents. The proposed method, HiMA-R1, employs Variance-Reduction Group Relative Policy Optimization (VR-GRPO) to efficiently handle the exponential joint action space through Monte Carlo sampling and selective agent group updates, alongside an adaptive memory evolution mechanism to reduce repetitive reasoning. Experimental results on the HiMA-Ecom benchmark, which contains 22.8K instances, show that this approach, using smaller 3B/7B open-source models, achieves performance comparable to larger models like DeepSeek-R1 and surpasses DeepSeek-V3 by an average of 6%.
本文提出了HiMA-Ecom基准，旨在解决电子商务领域分层多智能体AI助手缺乏现实训练与评估数据集的问题，其中主智能体协调多个专业子智能体。所提出的HiMA-R1方法采用方差缩减组相对策略优化（VR-GRPO），通过蒙特卡洛采样和选择性智能体组更新来高效处理指数级联合动作空间，并设计了自适应记忆演化机制以减少重复推理。在包含22.8K个实例的HiMA-Ecom基准上的实验结果表明，该方法基于较小的3B/7B开源模型，实现了与DeepSeek-R1等更大模型相当的性能，并以平均6%的优势超越了DeepSeek-V3。
G-ICSO-NAS: Shifting Gears between Gradient and Swarm for Robust Neural Architecture Search
Authors: Xingbang Du, Enzhi Zhang, Rui Zhong, Yang Cao, Masaharu Munetomo
First: 2026-04-01T10:06:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T10:06:59+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the International Joint Conference on Neural Networks (IJCNN), WCCI 2026. This is a preprint version
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Neural Architecture Search (NAS) has become a pivotal technique in automated machine learning. Evolutionary Algorithm (EA)-based methods demonstrate superior search quality but suffer from prohibitive computational costs, while gradient-based approaches like DARTS offer high efficiency but are prone to premature convergence and performance collapse. To bridge this gap, we propose G-ICSO-NAS, a hybrid framework implementing a three-stage optimization strategy. The Warm-up Phase pre-trains supernet weights ($w$) via differentiable methods while architecture parameters ($α$) remain frozen. The Exploration Phase adopts a hybrid co-optimization mechanism: an Improved Competitive Swarm Optimizer (ICSO) with diversity-aware fitness navigates the architecture space to update $α$, while gradient descent concurrently updates $w$. The Stability Phase employs fine-grained gradient-based search with early stopping to converge to the optimal architecture. By synergizing ICSO's global navigation capability with differentiable methods' efficiency, G-ICSO-NAS achieves remarkable performance with minimal cost. In the context of the DARTS search space, an accuracy of 97.46\% is achieved on CIFAR-10 with a computational budget of just 0.15 GPU-Days. The method also exhibits strong transfer potential, recording accuracies of 83.1\% (CIFAR-100) and 75.02\% (ImageNet). Furthermore, regarding the NAS-Bench-201 benchmark, G-ICSO-NAS is shown to deliver state-of-the-art results across all evaluated datasets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：G-ICSO-NAS：在梯度与群体智能间切换以实现鲁棒的神经架构搜索
神经架构搜索已成为自动化机器学习的关键技术。基于进化算法的方法展现出卓越的搜索质量，但计算成本过高；而基于梯度的方法（如DARTS）虽效率高，却易陷入早熟收敛与性能崩溃。为弥补这一鸿沟，我们提出G-ICSO-NAS混合框架，实施三阶段优化策略：预热阶段通过可微分方法预训练超网络权重（$w$），同时冻结架构参数（$α$）；探索阶段采用混合协同优化机制——基于多样性感知适应度的改进竞争群体优化器在架构空间中更新$α$，同时梯度下降法并行更新$w$；稳定阶段通过细粒度梯度搜索与早停机制收敛至最优架构。通过融合ICSO的全局导航能力与可微分方法的高效性，G-ICSO-NAS以极低成本取得显著性能：在DARTS搜索空间下，仅用0.15 GPU天计算量即在CIFAR-10达到97.46%准确率；同时展现强大迁移潜力，在CIFAR-100和ImageNet分别获得83.1%与75.02%准确率；在NAS-Bench-201基准测试中，该方法在所有评估数据集上均取得最先进结果。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the trade-off between the superior search quality of evolutionary algorithms and the high efficiency yet instability of gradient-based NAS methods, this paper proposes G-ICSO-NAS, a hybrid three-stage framework. The method combines gradient-based optimization with an Improved Competitive Swarm Optimizer (ICSO), featuring a warm-up phase for supernet weights, a hybrid co-optimization phase where ICSO updates architecture parameters and gradients update weights, and a final stability phase for fine-grained convergence. Experimental results on the DARTS search space show it achieves 97.46% accuracy on CIFAR-10 with only 0.15 GPU-days, along with strong transfer accuracies of 83.1% on CIFAR-100 and 75.02% on ImageNet, while also delivering state-of-the-art performance on the NAS-Bench-201 benchmark.
本文的动机是解决基于进化算法的神经架构搜索（NAS）方法搜索质量高但计算成本巨大，而基于梯度的方法（如DARTS）效率高但易早熟收敛和性能崩溃之间的矛盾。为此，论文提出了G-ICSO-NAS这一混合三阶段优化框架，将梯度优化与改进的竞争群优化器（ICSO）相结合，包括预热超网络权重、混合协同优化（ICSO更新架构参数，梯度下降更新权重）以及最终稳定性微调阶段。在DARTS搜索空间上的实验表明，该方法仅用0.15 GPU天即在CIFAR-10上达到97.46%的准确率，在CIFAR-100和ImageNet上分别获得83.1%和75.02%的迁移准确率，并在NAS-Bench-201基准测试中取得了领先的性能。
Learning to Hint for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Yu Xia, Canwen Xu, Zhewei Yao, Julian McAuley, Yuxiong He
First: 2026-04-01T09:58:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:58:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) is widely used for reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, but it often suffers from advantage collapse: when all rollouts in a group receive the same reward, the group yields zero relative advantage and thus no learning signal. For example, if a question is too hard for the reasoner, all sampled rollouts can be incorrect and receive zero reward. Recent work addresses this issue by adding hints or auxiliary scaffolds to such hard questions so that the reasoner produces mixed outcomes and recovers a non-zero update. However, existing hints are usually fixed rather than adapted to the current reasoner, and a hint that creates learning signal under the hinted input does not necessarily improve the no-hint policy used at test time. To this end, we propose Hint Learning for Reinforcement Learning (HiLL), a framework that jointly trains a hinter policy and a reasoner policy during RL. For each hard question, the hinter generates hints online conditioned on the current reasoner's incorrect rollout, allowing hint generation to adapt to the reasoner's evolving errors. We further introduce hint reliance, which measures how strongly correct hinted trajectories depend on the hint. We derive a transferability result showing that lower hint reliance implies stronger transfer from hinted success to no-hint success, and we use this result to define a transfer-weighted reward for training the hinter. Therefore, HiLL favors hints that not only recover informative GRPO groups, but also produce signals that are more likely to improve the original no-hint policy. Experiments across multiple benchmarks show that HiLL consistently outperforms GRPO and prior hint-based baselines, demonstrating the value of adaptive and transfer-aware hint learning for RL. The code is available at https://github.com/Andree-9/HiLL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中的提示学习
组相对策略优化（GRPO）广泛用于具有可验证奖励的强化学习，但常面临优势坍缩问题：当组内所有轨迹获得相同奖励时，该组产生零相对优势，导致学习信号缺失。例如，若问题对推理器过难，所有采样轨迹可能均错误且获得零奖励。近期研究通过向此类难题添加提示或辅助支架来解决该问题，使推理器产生混合结果并恢复非零更新。然而，现有提示通常是固定的而非适配当前推理器，且在提示输入下产生学习信号的提示未必能提升测试时使用的无提示策略。为此，我们提出强化学习提示学习框架（HiLL），在强化学习中联合训练提示器策略与推理器策略。针对每个难题，提示器根据当前推理器的错误轨迹在线生成适配其动态错误的提示。我们进一步提出提示依赖度指标，用于衡量正确提示轨迹对提示的依赖强度。通过推导可迁移性理论证明：较低的提示依赖度意味着从提示成功向无提示成功更强的迁移能力，并据此定义用于训练提示器的迁移加权奖励。因此，HiLL倾向于选择既能恢复信息性GRPO分组，又能产生更可能改进原始无提示策略的学习信号的提示。多基准实验表明，HiLL持续优于GRPO及现有基于提示的基线方法，验证了自适应且具备迁移感知的提示学习对强化学习的价值。代码发布于 https://github.com/Andree-9/HiLL。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the advantage collapse problem in Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) for reinforcement learning, where hard tasks yield zero learning signal when all rollouts fail. To overcome this, the authors propose HiLL, a framework that jointly trains a hinter policy to generate adaptive hints based on the reasoner's current errors, alongside the reasoner policy. They introduce a hint reliance metric to ensure hints improve the no-hint policy via a transfer-weighted reward. Experiments across multiple benchmarks show HiLL outperforms GRPO and prior hint-based methods, demonstrating the effectiveness of adaptive, transfer-aware hint learning.
本文针对强化学习中组相对策略优化（GRPO）的优势崩溃问题，即当所有轨迹都失败时，困难任务无法提供学习信号。为此，作者提出了HiLL框架，联合训练一个提示生成策略和一个推理策略，其中提示策略根据推理器的当前错误动态生成提示。他们引入了提示依赖度指标，通过转移加权奖励确保提示能提升无提示策略的性能。在多个基准测试上的实验表明，HiLL优于GRPO及现有基于提示的方法，验证了自适应且关注转移的提示学习的有效性。
Meta-Learning and Meta-Reinforcement Learning -- Tracing the Path towards DeepMind's Adaptive Agent
Authors: Björn Hoppmann, Christoph Scholz
First: 2026-02-23T13:39:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:55:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Humans are highly effective at utilizing prior knowledge to adapt to novel tasks, a capability that standard machine learning models struggle to replicate due to their reliance on task-specific training. Meta-learning overcomes this limitation by allowing models to acquire transferable knowledge from various tasks, enabling rapid adaptation to new challenges with minimal data. This survey provides a rigorous, task-based formalization of meta-learning and meta-reinforcement learning and uses that paradigm to chronicle the landmark algorithms that paved the way for DeepMind's Adaptive Agent, consolidating the essential concepts needed to understand the Adaptive Agent and other generalist approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：元学习与元强化学习——追溯通往DeepMind自适应智能体的演进路径
人类善于利用先验知识适应新任务，而标准机器学习模型因依赖任务特定训练难以复现此能力。元学习通过让模型从多任务中获取可迁移知识，突破这一局限，使其能以少量数据快速适应新挑战。本文基于任务形式化框架，系统梳理元学习与元强化学习的里程碑算法，追溯其促成DeepMind自适应智能体的发展脉络，并整合理解该智能体及其他通用方法所需的核心概念。

本文的动机是人类能够利用先验知识快速适应新任务，而标准机器学习模型因依赖任务特定训练而难以实现这一点，因此通过元学习和元强化学习的任务形式化框架来获取可迁移知识。方法上采用严格的任务形式化范式，追溯了关键算法的发展路径，这些算法使得模型能够以少量数据快速适应新挑战。主要实验结果未具体展开，但该综述整合了理解DeepMind自适应智能体及其他通用方法所需的核心概念，梳理了导致该智能体诞生的算法演进历程。
Full-Gradient Successor Feature Representations
Authors: Ritish Shrirao, Aditya Priyadarshi, Raghuram Bharadwaj Diddigi
First: 2026-04-01T09:44:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:44:13+00:00
Comments: Submitted to IEEE CDC 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Successor Features (SF) combined with Generalized Policy Improvement (GPI) provide a robust framework for transfer learning in Reinforcement Learning (RL) by decoupling environment dynamics from reward functions. However, standard SF learning methods typically rely on semi-gradient Temporal Difference (TD) updates. When combined with non-linear function approximation, semi-gradient methods lack robust convergence guarantees and can lead to instability, particularly in the multi-task setting where accurate feature estimation is critical for effective GPI. Inspired by Full Gradient DQN, we propose Full-Gradient Successor Feature Representations Q-Learning (FG-SFRQL), an algorithm that optimizes the successor features by minimizing the full Mean Squared Bellman Error. Unlike standard approaches, our method computes gradients with respect to parameters in both the online and target networks. We provide a theoretical proof of almost-sure convergence for FG-SFRQL and demonstrate empirically that minimizing the full residual leads to superior sample efficiency and transfer performance compared to semi-gradient baselines in both discrete and continuous domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：全梯度后继特征表示
后继特征（SF）与广义策略改进（GPI）相结合，通过解耦环境动态与奖励函数，为强化学习（RL）中的迁移学习提供了稳健框架。然而，标准SF学习方法通常依赖半梯度时序差分（TD）更新。当与非线性函数逼近结合时，半梯度方法缺乏稳健的收敛保证，可能导致不稳定，尤其在多任务场景中——精确的特征估计对有效GPI至关重要。受全梯度DQN启发，我们提出全梯度后继特征表示Q学习算法（FG-SFRQL），该算法通过最小化完整的均方贝尔曼误差来优化后继特征。与标准方法不同，本方法同时计算在线网络与目标网络参数的梯度。我们为FG-SFRQL提供了几乎必然收敛的理论证明，并通过实验验证：在离散与连续领域中，最小化完整残差相比半梯度基线方法具有更优的样本效率与迁移性能。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the instability and lack of convergence guarantees in standard semi-gradient Temporal Difference methods for learning Successor Features (SF) with non-linear function approximation, which hinders robust transfer learning in multi-task reinforcement learning. To address this, the authors propose Full-Gradient Successor Feature Representations Q-Learning (FG-SFRQL), a method that optimizes successor features by minimizing the full Mean Squared Bellman Error, computing gradients with respect to both online and target network parameters. Experimental results demonstrate that FG-SFRQL provides superior sample efficiency and transfer performance compared to semi-gradient baselines in discrete and continuous domains, supported by a theoretical proof of almost-sure convergence.
本文的动机在于，标准半梯度时序差分方法在非线性函数逼近下学习后继特征时存在不稳定性和缺乏收敛保证的问题，这阻碍了多任务强化学习中稳健的迁移学习。为此，作者提出了全梯度后继特征表示Q学习（FG-SFRQL），该方法通过最小化完整的均方贝尔曼误差来优化后继特征，并计算在线网络和目标网络参数的双向梯度。实验结果表明，在离散和连续领域中，FG-SFRQL相比半梯度基线方法具有更优的样本效率和迁移性能，并辅以几乎必然收敛的理论证明。
Large Language Model Guided Incentive Aware Reward Design for Cooperative Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Dogan Urgun, Gokhan Gungor
First: 2026-03-25T14:05:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:31:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Designing effective auxiliary rewards for cooperative multi-agent systems remains a challenging task. Misaligned incentives risk inducing suboptimal coordination, especially when sparse task feedback fails to provide sufficient grounding. This study introduces an automated reward design framework that leverages large language models to synthesize executable reward programs from environment instrumentation. The procedure constrains candidate programs within a formal validity envelope and evaluates their efficacy by training policies from scratch under a fixed computational budget. Selection across generations depends exclusively on the sparse task return. The framework is evaluated across four distinct Overcooked-AI layouts characterized by varied corridor congestion, handoff dependencies, and structural asymmetries. Iterative search generations consistently yield superior task returns and delivery counts, with the most pronounced gains occurring in environments dominated by interaction bottlenecks. Diagnostic analysis of the synthesized shaping components indicates increased interdependence in action selection and improved signal alignment in coordination-intensive tasks. These results demonstrate that the search for objective-grounded reward programs can mitigate the burden of manual engineering while producing shaping signals compatible with cooperative learning under finite budgets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大语言模型引导的激励感知奖励设计用于合作多智能体强化学习
为合作多智能体系统设计有效的辅助奖励仍具挑战性。激励错配可能导致次优协调，尤其在稀疏任务反馈无法提供充分依据时。本研究提出一种自动化奖励设计框架，利用大语言模型从环境监测数据中合成可执行的奖励程序。该流程将候选程序约束在形式化有效范围内，并通过在固定计算预算下从头训练策略来评估其效能。代际选择完全依据稀疏任务回报。该框架在四种不同的《Overcooked-AI》场景布局中进行评估，这些布局具有不同的通道拥堵度、交接依赖性和结构不对称性。迭代搜索代次持续产生更优的任务回报与配送数量，在交互瓶颈主导的环境中增益最为显著。对合成塑形组件的诊断分析表明，动作选择的相互依赖性增强，且在协调密集型任务中信号对齐得到改善。这些结果表明，基于目标的奖励程序搜索能减轻人工设计负担，同时生成适用于有限预算下合作学习的塑形信号。
Summary / 总结
The study is motivated by the challenge of designing effective auxiliary rewards in cooperative multi-agent systems, where misaligned incentives can lead to suboptimal coordination, especially under sparse task feedback. The method introduces an automated reward design framework that uses large language models to generate executable reward programs from environment instrumentation, constrains them within a formal validity envelope, and evaluates their efficacy by training policies from scratch under a fixed computational budget, selecting programs based solely on sparse task returns. Experimental results across four Overcooked-AI layouts show that iterative search generations consistently yield superior task returns and delivery counts, with the most significant gains in environments with interaction bottlenecks, and diagnostic analysis reveals increased interdependence in action selection and improved signal alignment in coordination-intensive tasks, demonstrating that this approach can reduce manual engineering burdens while producing shaping signals compatible with cooperative learning under finite budgets.
本研究旨在解决合作多智能体系统中设计有效辅助奖励的挑战，即激励错配可能导致次优协调，尤其在稀疏任务反馈下。方法上，提出了一个自动化奖励设计框架，利用大语言模型从环境工具中合成可执行的奖励程序，将其约束在形式化有效范围内，并通过在固定计算预算下从头训练策略来评估其效能，仅依据稀疏任务回报进行选择。在四个不同布局的Overcooked-AI环境中的实验结果表明，迭代搜索代次持续产生更优的任务回报和交付数量，在交互瓶颈主导的环境中增益最为显著，诊断分析显示合成奖励组件增强了动作选择的相互依赖性和协调密集型任务中的信号对齐，证明这种搜索目标驱动的奖励程序的方法能减轻手动工程负担，同时生成适用于有限预算下合作学习的塑形信号。
Klear-Reasoner: Advancing Reasoning Capability via Gradient-Preserving Clipping Policy Optimization
Authors: Zhenpeng Su, Leiyu Pan, Xue Bai, Dening Liu, Guanting Dong, Jiaming Huang, Minxuan Lv, Wenping Hu, Fuzheng Zhang, Kun Gai, Guorui Zhou
First: 2025-08-11T05:17:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T09:05:32+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Klear-Reasoner, a model with long reasoning capabilities that demonstrates careful deliberation during problem solving, achieving outstanding performance across multiple benchmarks. Although there are already many excellent works related to inference models in the current community, there are still many problems with reproducing high-performance inference models due to incomplete disclosure of training details. This report provides an in-depth analysis of the reasoning model, covering the entire post-training workflow from data preparation and long Chain-of-Thought supervised fine-tuning (long CoT SFT) to reinforcement learning (RL), along with detailed ablation studies for each experimental component. For SFT data, our experiments show that a small number of high-quality data sources are more effective than a large number of diverse data sources, and that difficult samples can achieve better results without accuracy filtering. In addition, we investigate two key issues with current clipping mechanisms in RL: Clipping suppresses critical exploration signals and ignores suboptimal trajectories. To address these challenges, we propose Gradient-Preserving clipping Policy Optimization (GPPO) that gently backpropagates gradients from clipped tokens. GPPO not only enhances the model's exploration capacity but also improves its efficiency in learning from negative samples. Klear-Reasoner exhibits exceptional reasoning abilities in mathematics and programming, scoring 90.5% on AIME 2024, 83.2% on AIME 2025, 66.0% on LiveCodeBench V5 and 58.1% on LiveCodeBench V6.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Klear-Reasoner：通过梯度保留裁剪策略优化提升推理能力
我们提出Klear-Reasoner，一种具备长程推理能力的模型，在解决问题时展现出审慎的思考过程，并在多个基准测试中取得卓越性能。尽管当前社区已有许多优秀的推理模型相关工作，但由于训练细节披露不完整，复现高性能推理模型仍存在诸多问题。本报告对推理模型进行了深入分析，涵盖从数据准备、长链思维监督微调（长CoT SFT）到强化学习（RL）的完整训练后工作流程，并对每个实验模块进行了详细的消融研究。对于SFT数据，实验表明少量高质量数据源比大量多样化数据源更有效，且困难样本无需精度过滤即可获得更好效果。此外，我们研究了当前RL裁剪机制的两个关键问题：裁剪抑制关键探索信号并忽略次优轨迹。为解决这些挑战，我们提出梯度保留裁剪策略优化（GPPO），可温和地反向传播来自裁剪标记的梯度。GPPO不仅增强了模型的探索能力，还提升了其从负样本中学习的效率。Klear-Reasoner在数学和编程领域展现出卓越推理能力，在AIME 2024得分90.5%、AIME 2025得分83.2%、LiveCodeBench V5得分66.0%、LiveCodeBench V6得分58.1%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the difficulty of reproducing high-performance reasoning models due to insufficient training detail disclosure, this paper introduces Klear-Reasoner, a model designed for long reasoning tasks. The method involves a detailed post-training workflow including data preparation, long Chain-of-Thought supervised fine-tuning (SFT), and a novel reinforcement learning approach called Gradient-Preserving clipping Policy Optimization (GPPO), which addresses issues in standard clipping by gently backpropagating gradients from clipped tokens to preserve exploration signals and utilize suboptimal trajectories. Key experimental results show that high-quality, difficult SFT data is more effective than diverse data, and that GPPO enhances exploration and learning from negative samples, leading to outstanding benchmark performance, including scores of 90.5% on AIME 2024 and 66.0% on LiveCodeBench V5.
本文的动机在于当前高性能推理模型因训练细节披露不完整而难以复现，为此提出了具备长推理能力的Klear-Reasoner模型。方法上，它详细阐述了从数据准备、长思维链监督微调（SFT）到强化学习的整个后训练流程，并针对现有裁剪机制抑制探索信号和忽略次优轨迹的问题，提出了梯度保留裁剪策略优化（GPPO），通过温和地反向传播被裁剪标记的梯度来改进学习。主要实验结果表明，少量高质量且包含难题的SFT数据比多样化的数据更有效，GPPO能增强模型的探索能力并提升从负样本中学习的效率，最终模型在多个基准测试中表现出色，如在AIME 2024上获得90.5%的分数，在LiveCodeBench V5上达到66.0%。
Finite-State Controllers for (Hidden-Model) POMDPs using Deep Reinforcement Learning
Authors: David Hudák, Maris F. L. Galesloot, Martin Tappler, Martin Kurečka, Nils Jansen, Milan Češka
First: 2026-02-09T14:39:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T08:22:16+00:00
Comments: 17 pages (8 main paper, 2 references, 7 appendix). 3 figures in the main paper, 3 figures in the appendix. Accepted AAMAS'26 submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Solving partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs) requires computing policies under imperfect state information. Despite recent advances, the scalability of existing POMDP solvers remains limited. Moreover, many settings require a policy that is robust across multiple POMDPs, further aggravating the scalability issue. We propose the Lexpop framework for POMDP solving. Lexpop (1) employs deep reinforcement learning to train a neural policy, represented by a recurrent neural network, and (2) constructs a finite-state controller mimicking the neural policy through efficient extraction methods. Crucially, unlike neural policies, such controllers can be formally evaluated, providing performance guarantees. We extend Lexpop to compute robust policies for hidden-model POMDPs (HM-POMDPs), which describe finite sets of POMDPs. We associate every extracted controller with its worst-case POMDP. Using a set of such POMDPs, we iteratively train a robust neural policy and consequently extract a robust controller. Our experiments show that on problems with large state spaces, Lexpop outperforms state-of-the-art solvers for POMDPs as well as HM-POMDPs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于深度强化学习的（隐模型）部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程有限状态控制器
求解部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程需要在状态信息不完整的情况下计算策略。尽管近期研究取得进展，现有POMDP求解器的可扩展性仍受限。此外，许多场景要求策略在多个POMDP中保持鲁棒性，进一步加剧了可扩展性问题。我们提出Lexpop框架用于POMDP求解，该框架（1）采用深度强化学习训练由循环神经网络表示的神经策略，（2）通过高效提取方法构建模拟神经策略的有限状态控制器。关键的是，与神经策略不同，此类控制器可进行形式化验证并提供性能保证。我们将Lexpop扩展至隐模型POMDP的鲁棒策略计算，该方法通过关联每个提取控制器与其最差情况POMDP，利用此类POMDP集合迭代训练鲁棒神经策略并提取鲁棒控制器。实验表明，在大状态空间问题上，Lexpop在POMDP及HM-POMDP求解性能上均优于当前最优方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the scalability limitations of existing solvers for partially observable Markov decision processes (POMDPs) and the need for policies robust across multiple models, this paper introduces the Lexpop framework. The method first trains a neural policy using deep reinforcement learning with a recurrent neural network, then extracts a finite-state controller that mimics this policy, enabling formal evaluation and performance guarantees. The approach is extended to hidden-model POMDPs (HM-POMDPs) by iteratively training a robust neural policy against worst-case POMDPs and extracting a corresponding robust controller. Experimental results demonstrate that Lexpop outperforms state-of-the-art solvers on problems with large state spaces for both standard POMDPs and HM-POMDPs.
针对现有部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（POMDP）求解器可扩展性有限，且需要跨多个模型具有鲁棒性的策略这一问题，本文提出了Lexpop框架。该方法首先使用深度强化学习训练一个基于循环神经网络的神经策略，然后通过高效提取方法构建模仿该策略的有限状态控制器，从而支持形式化验证和性能保证。该框架被扩展到隐模型POMDP（HM-POMDP），通过针对最坏情况POMDP迭代训练鲁棒神经策略并提取相应的鲁棒控制器。实验结果表明，在大状态空间问题上，Lexpop在标准POMDP和HM-POMDP上的性能均优于当前最先进的求解器。
On Global Convergence Rates for Federated Softmax Policy Gradient under Heterogeneous Environments
Authors: Safwan Labbi, Paul Mangold, Daniil Tiapkin, Eric Moulines
First: 2025-05-29T14:08:35+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T07:46:23+00:00
Comments: Preprint
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We provide global convergence rates for vanilla and entropy-regularized federated softmax stochastic policy gradient (FedPG) with local training. We show that FedPG converges to a near-optimal policy in terms of the average agent value, with a gap controlled by the level of heterogeneity. Remarkably, we obtain the first convergence rates for entropy-regularized policy gradient with explicit constants, leveraging a projection-like operator. Our results build upon a new analysis of federated averaging for non-convex objectives, based on the observation that the Łojasiewicz-type inequalities from the single-agent setting (Mei et al., 2020) do not hold for the federated objective. This uncovers a fundamental difference between single-agent and federated reinforcement learning: while single-agent optimal policies can be deterministic, federated objectives may inherently require stochastic policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：异构环境下联邦软最大策略梯度的全局收敛速率分析
本文针对本地训练的原始及熵正则化联邦软最大随机策略梯度（FedPG）方法，给出了全局收敛速率。研究表明，FedPG在平均智能体价值意义上收敛至接近最优的策略，其差距受异构程度控制。值得注意的是，通过利用类投影算子，我们首次获得了熵正则化策略梯度具有显式常数的收敛速率。这些结果建立在对联邦平均方法在非凸目标上的新分析基础上，该分析基于以下观察：单智能体设置中的Łojasiewicz型不等式（Mei等人，2020）不适用于联邦目标。这揭示了单智能体与联邦强化学习之间的根本差异：单智能体最优策略可以是确定性的，而联邦目标可能本质上需要随机策略。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the convergence of federated softmax policy gradient (FedPG) methods in heterogeneous reinforcement learning environments, motivated by the need to understand how policy optimization behaves when data is distributed across multiple agents with differing dynamics. The authors analyze both vanilla and entropy-regularized versions of FedPG with local training, employing a novel analysis of federated averaging for non-convex objectives that addresses the failure of Łojasiewicz-type inequalities in the federated setting. Key experimental results demonstrate that FedPG converges to a near-optimal policy in terms of average agent value, with the performance gap explicitly bounded by the level of environmental heterogeneity, and they provide the first convergence rates with explicit constants for entropy-regularized policy gradient, revealing that federated objectives may inherently require stochastic policies unlike single-agent cases.
本文研究了在异构强化学习环境中联邦软最大值策略梯度（FedPG）方法的收敛性，其动机在于需要理解当数据分布在具有不同动态特性的多个智能体时策略优化的行为。作者分析了带有局部训练的普通版本和熵正则化版本的FedPG，采用了一种针对非凸目标的联邦平均新分析方法，以解决联邦设置中Łojasiewicz型不等式不成立的问题。主要实验结果表明，FedPG在平均智能体价值方面收敛到接近最优的策略，性能差距由环境异质性水平明确控制，并且首次给出了熵正则化策略梯度具有显式常数的收敛速率，揭示了联邦目标可能本质上需要随机策略，这与单智能体情况不同。
Optimsyn: Influence-Guided Rubrics Optimization for Synthetic Data Generation
Authors: Zhiting Fan, Ruizhe Chen, Tianxiang Hu, Ru Peng, Zenan Huang, Haokai Xu, Yixin Chen, Jian Wu, Junbo Zhao, Zuozhu Liu
First: 2026-04-01T06:28:44+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T06:28:44+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) achieve strong downstream performance largely due to abundant supervised fine-tuning (SFT) data. However, high-quality SFT data in knowledge-intensive domains such as humanities, social sciences, medicine, law, and finance is scarce because expert curation is expensive, privacy constraints are strict, and label consistency is hard to ensure. Recent work uses synthetic data, typically by prompting a generator over domain documents and filtering outputs with handcrafted rubrics. Yet rubric design is expert-dependent, transfers poorly across domains, and is often optimized through a brittle heuristic loop of writing rubrics, synthesizing data, training, inspecting results, and manually guessing revisions. This process lacks reliable quantitative feedback about how a rubric affects downstream performance. We propose evaluating synthetic data by its training utility on the target model and using this signal to guide data generation. Inspired by influence estimation, we adopt an optimizer-aware estimator that uses gradient information to quantify each synthetic sample's contribution to a target model's objective on specific tasks. Our analysis shows that even when synthetic and real samples are close in embedding space, their influence on learning can differ substantially. Based on this insight, we propose an optimization-based framework that adapts rubrics using target-model feedback. We provide lightweight guiding text and use a rubric-specialized model to generate task-conditioned rubrics. Influence score is used as the reward to optimize the rubric generator with reinforcement learning. Experiments across domains, target models, and data generators show consistent improvements and strong generalization without task-specific tuning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Optimsyn：面向合成数据生成的影响引导式评估准则优化
大语言模型（LLMs）在下游任务中的优异表现主要得益于丰富的监督微调（SFT）数据。然而，在人文学科、社会科学、医学、法律和金融等知识密集型领域，高质量SFT数据十分稀缺，原因在于专家标注成本高昂、隐私约束严格且标签一致性难以保证。近期研究采用合成数据方案，通常基于领域文档提示生成器，并用手工设计的评估准则过滤输出。但评估准则设计依赖专家经验，跨领域迁移性差，且常通过脆弱的启发式循环进行优化：编写准则、合成数据、训练模型、检查结果、人工猜测修订。该过程缺乏关于评估准则如何影响下游性能的可靠量化反馈。我们提出通过合成数据在目标模型上的训练效用进行评估，并利用该信号指导数据生成。受影响估计的启发，我们采用优化器感知的估计器，利用梯度信息量化每个合成样本对目标模型在特定任务目标上的贡献。分析表明，即使合成样本与真实样本在嵌入空间中相近，它们对学习过程的影响也可能存在显著差异。基于此发现，我们提出一个基于优化的框架，利用目标模型反馈自适应调整评估准则。我们提供轻量级引导文本，并采用准则专用模型生成任务条件化评估准则。以影响分数作为奖励，通过强化学习优化准则生成器。跨领域、目标模型和数据生成器的实验表明，该方法无需任务特定调优即可实现持续改进和强大泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of generating high-quality synthetic data for supervised fine-tuning of large language models in knowledge-intensive domains where expert-curated data is scarce and expensive. The proposed method, Optimsyn, introduces an influence-guided optimization framework that uses gradient-based influence estimation to quantify each synthetic sample's contribution to the target model's performance, enabling rubric adaptation via reinforcement learning with influence scores as rewards. Experimental results demonstrate consistent improvements across various domains, target models, and data generators, showing strong generalization without task-specific tuning.
本文针对知识密集型领域中高质量监督微调数据稀缺且昂贵的问题，提出了一种影响引导的合成数据生成优化方法。该方法名为Optimsyn，采用基于梯度的影响估计来量化每个合成样本对目标模型性能的贡献，并通过强化学习以影响分数作为奖励来优化生成准则。实验结果表明，该方法在不同领域、目标模型和数据生成器上均能取得一致性能提升，且无需任务特定调整即展现出强大的泛化能力。
Generalized Heavy-tailed Mutation for Evolutionary Algorithms
Authors: Anton V. Eremeev, Dmitri V. Silaev, Valentin A. Topchii
First: 2026-04-01T05:33:12+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T05:33:12+00:00
Comments: Presented at the international conference dedicated to mathematics in artificial intelligence (MathAI-2026). Translated from the publication in Russian: A.V. Eremeev, D.V. Silaev, and Topchii V.A. Generalized heavy-tailed mutation for evolutionary algorithms. Sibirskie Elektronnye Matematicheskie Izvestiya [Siberian Electronic Mathematical Reports], 21:940-959, 2024. DOI: 10.33048/semi.2024.21.062
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The heavy-tailed mutation operator, proposed by Doerr, Le, Makhmara, and Nguyen (2017) for evolutionary algorithms, is based on the power-law assumption of mutation rate distribution. Here we generalize the power-law assumption using a regularly varying constraint on the distribution function of mutation rate. In this setting, we generalize the upper bounds on the expected optimization time of the $(1+(λ,λ))$ genetic algorithm obtained by Antipov, Buzdalov and Doerr (2022) for the OneMax function class parametrized by the problem dimension $n$. In particular, it is shown that, on this function class, the sufficient conditions of Antipov, Buzdalov and Doerr (2022) on the heavy-tailed mutation, ensuring the $O(n)$ optimization time in expectation, may be generalized as well. This optimization time is known to be asymptotically smaller than what can be achieved by the $(1+(λ,λ))$ genetic algorithm with any static mutation rate. A new version of the heavy-tailed mutation operator is proposed, satisfying the generalized conditions, and promising results of computational experiments are presented.
中文标题/摘要
标题：进化算法的广义重尾变异算子
重尾变异算子由Doerr、Le、Makhmara和Nguyen（2017）提出，其基于变异率分布的幂律假设。本文通过对变异率分布函数施加正则变化约束，推广了该幂律假设。在此框架下，我们推广了Antipov、Buzdalov和Doerr（2022）针对问题维度n参数化的OneMax函数类所得到的$(1+(λ,λ))$遗传算法期望优化时间上界。特别地，研究表明在该函数类上，Antipov等人（2022）提出的保证期望$O(n)$优化时间的重尾变异充分条件同样可被推广。该优化时间已知渐近小于采用任何静态变异率的$(1+(λ,λ))$遗传算法所能达到的结果。本文提出了满足广义条件的新版重尾变异算子，并展示了具有前景的计算实验结果。
Summary / 总结
This paper aims to generalize the theoretical foundation of the heavy-tailed mutation operator in evolutionary algorithms, moving beyond the original power-law assumption to a broader class of distributions defined by regular variation. The method involves analyzing the (1+(λ,λ)) genetic algorithm on the OneMax function, deriving new sufficient conditions under which the expected optimization time remains linear in the problem dimension n. The main experimental results confirm that the proposed generalized mutation operator maintains the O(n) expected runtime, which is asymptotically superior to using any static mutation rate, and computational experiments support these theoretical findings.
本文旨在推广进化算法中重尾变异算子的理论基础，将原有的幂律假设扩展至由正则变化定义的一类更广泛的分布。研究方法基于在OneMax函数上分析(1+(λ,λ))遗传算法，推导出新的充分条件，以确保期望优化时间与问题维度n保持线性关系。主要实验结果表明，所提出的广义变异算子能维持O(n)的期望运行时间，这渐近地优于使用任何静态变异率的结果，并且计算实验支持了这些理论发现。
A Reasoning-Enabled Vision-Language Foundation Model for Chest X-ray Interpretation
Authors: Yabin Zhang, Chong Wang, Yunhe Gao, Jiaming Liu, Maya Varma, Justin Xu, Sophie Ostmeier, Jin Long, Sergios Gatidis, Seena Dehkharghani, Arne Michalson, Eun Kyoung Hong, Christian Bluethgen, Haiwei Henry Guo, Alexander Victor Ortiz, Stephan Altmayer, Sandhya Bodapati, Joseph David Janizek, Ken Chang, Jean-Benoit Delbrouck, Akshay S. Chaudhari, Curtis P. Langlotz
First: 2026-04-01T05:19:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T05:19:09+00:00
Comments: Codes: https://github.com/YBZh/CheXOne Models: https://huggingface.co/StanfordAIMI/CheXOne
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Chest X-rays (CXRs) are among the most frequently performed imaging examinations worldwide, yet rising imaging volumes increase radiologist workload and the risk of diagnostic errors. Although artificial intelligence (AI) systems have shown promise for CXR interpretation, most generate only final predictions, without making explicit how visual evidence is translated into radiographic findings and diagnostic predictions. We present CheXOne, a reasoning-enabled vision-language model for CXR interpretation. CheXOne jointly generates diagnostic predictions and explicit, clinically grounded reasoning traces that connect visual evidence, radiographic findings, and these predictions. The model is trained on 14.7 million instruction and reasoning samples curated from 30 public datasets spanning 36 CXR interpretation tasks, using a two-stage framework that combines instruction tuning with reinforcement learning to improve reasoning quality. We evaluate CheXOne in zero-shot settings across visual question answering, report generation, visual grounding and reasoning assessment, covering 17 evaluation settings. CheXOne outperforms existing medical and general-domain foundation models and achieves strong performance on independent public benchmarks. A clinical reader study demonstrates that CheXOne-drafted reports are comparable to or better than resident-written reports in 55% of cases, while effectively addressing clinical indications and enhancing both report writing and CXR interpretation efficiency. Further analyses involving radiologists reveal that the generated reasoning traces show high clinical factuality and provide causal support for the final predictions, offering a plausible explanation for the performance gains. These results suggest that explicit reasoning can improve model performance, interpretability and clinical utility in AI-assisted CXR interpretation.

Analysis of On-policy Policy Gradient Methods under the Distribution Mismatch
Authors: Weizhen Wang, Jianping He, Xiaoming Duan
First: 2025-03-28T08:52:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T04:30:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Policy gradient methods are one of the most successful approaches for solving challenging reinforcement learning problems. Despite their empirical successes, many state-of-the-art policy gradient algorithms for discounted problems deviate from the theoretical policy gradient theorem due to the existence of a distribution mismatch. In this work, we analyze the impact of this mismatch on policy gradient methods. Specifically, we first show that in the case of tabular parameterizations, the biased gradient induced by the mismatch still yields a valid first-order characterization of global optimality. Then, we extend this analysis to more general parameterizations by deriving explicit bounds on both the state distribution mismatch and the resulting gradient mismatch in episodic and continuing MDPs, which are shown to vanish at least linearly as the discount factor approaches one. Building on these bounds, we further establish guarantees for the biased policy gradient iterates, showing that they approach approximate stationary points with respect to the exact gradient, with asymptotic residuals depending on the discount factor. Our findings offer insights into the robustness of policy gradient methods as well as the gap between theoretical foundations and practical implementations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：分布失配下同策略策略梯度方法分析
策略梯度方法是解决复杂强化学习问题最成功的途径之一。尽管经验上取得了成功，但由于分布失配的存在，许多针对折扣问题的最先进策略梯度算法偏离了理论上的策略梯度定理。本研究分析了这种失配对策略梯度方法的影响。具体而言，我们首先证明在表格化参数化情况下，由失配引起的偏置梯度仍能有效表征全局最优性的一阶特性。随后，我们将分析扩展到更一般的参数化情形，通过推导片段式和持续性马尔可夫决策过程中状态分布失配及梯度失配的显式边界，证明这些边界在折扣因子趋近于一时至少以线性速度收敛至零。基于这些边界，我们进一步建立了偏置策略梯度迭代的收敛保证，证明其能逼近精确梯度意义下的近似驻点，且渐近残差取决于折扣因子。本研究为理解策略梯度方法的鲁棒性以及理论基础与实际实现之间的差距提供了新的视角。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates the robustness of policy gradient methods in reinforcement learning when a distribution mismatch exists between the state visitation distribution used for gradient estimation and the true discounted state distribution, a common deviation in practical algorithms. The method involves a theoretical analysis showing that, for tabular parameterizations, the biased gradient still provides a valid first-order optimality condition, and it extends this by deriving explicit bounds on the distribution and gradient mismatch for both episodic and continuing MDPs, which vanish linearly as the discount factor approaches one. The main experimental results, derived analytically, demonstrate that the biased policy gradient iterates converge to approximate stationary points relative to the exact gradient, with asymptotic residuals controlled by the discount factor, offering insights into the gap between theory and practice in policy gradient implementations.
本文研究了强化学习中策略梯度方法在存在分布不匹配时的鲁棒性，这种不匹配是指梯度估计中使用的状态访问分布与真实折扣状态分布之间的偏差，这在实用算法中很常见。方法上，通过理论分析表明，对于表格化参数化，有偏梯度仍能提供有效的一阶最优性条件，并进一步推导了在回合式和持续MDP中分布不匹配及梯度不匹配的显式边界，这些边界随着折扣因子趋近于一而至少线性消失。主要实验结果（通过分析得出）证明，有偏策略梯度迭代会收敛到相对于精确梯度的近似驻点，其渐近残差由折扣因子控制，这为理解策略梯度理论基础与实际实现之间的差距提供了见解。
FIRE: Frobenius-Isometry Reinitialization for Balancing the Stability-Plasticity Tradeoff
Authors: Isaac Han, Sangyeon Park, Seungwon Oh, Donghu Kim, Hojoon Lee, Kyung-Joong Kim
Venue: ICLR oral
First: 2026-02-08T16:17:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T04:00:21+00:00
Comments: ICLR'26 (oral)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep neural networks trained on nonstationary data must balance stability (i.e., retaining prior knowledge) and plasticity (i.e., adapting to new tasks). Standard reinitialization methods, which reinitialize weights toward their original values, are widely used but difficult to tune: conservative reinitializations fail to restore plasticity, while aggressive ones erase useful knowledge. We propose FIRE, a principled reinitialization method that explicitly balances the stability-plasticity tradeoff. FIRE quantifies stability through Squared Frobenius Error (SFE), measuring proximity to past weights, and plasticity through Deviation from Isometry (DfI), reflecting weight isotropy. The reinitialization point is obtained by solving a constrained optimization problem, minimizing SFE subject to DfI being zero, which is efficiently approximated by Newton-Schulz iteration. FIRE is evaluated on continual visual learning (CIFAR-10 with ResNet-18), language modeling (OpenWebText with GPT-0.1B), and reinforcement learning (HumanoidBench with SAC and Atari games with DQN). Across all domains, FIRE consistently outperforms both naive training without intervention and standard reinitialization methods, demonstrating effective balancing of the stability-plasticity tradeoff.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FIRE：基于Frobenius等距重初始化的稳定性-可塑性权衡平衡方法
在非平稳数据上训练的深度神经网络需平衡稳定性（保留先验知识）与可塑性（适应新任务）。标准重初始化方法通过将权重向原始值重置被广泛使用，但难以调优：保守重置无法恢复可塑性，激进重置则会消除有用知识。本文提出FIRE——一种显式平衡稳定性-可塑性权衡的原理性重初始化方法。FIRE通过Frobenius平方误差量化稳定性（衡量与历史权重的接近度），通过等距偏差量化可塑性（反映权重各向同性）。通过求解约束优化问题获得重初始化点：在等距偏差为零的条件下最小化Frobenius平方误差，并采用牛顿-舒尔茨迭代高效近似求解。实验涵盖持续视觉学习（CIFAR-10+ResNet-18）、语言建模（OpenWebText+GPT-0.1B）和强化学习（HumanoidBench+SAC/Atari+DQN）。在所有领域中，FIRE均持续优于无干预的朴素训练及标准重初始化方法，有效实现了稳定性-可塑性的平衡。

Experimental results across continual visual learning, language modeling, and reinforcement learning tasks show that FIRE consistently outperforms both naive training and standard reinitialization methods, effectively balancing the stability-plasticity tradeoff.
本文针对在非平稳数据上训练的深度神经网络中平衡稳定性和可塑性的挑战，指出标准重初始化方法难以有效调节。作者提出FIRE方法，通过平方Frobenius误差量化稳定性，通过偏离等距性量化可塑性，并求解约束优化问题以找到最小化稳定性损失同时确保可塑性的重初始化点。在持续视觉学习、语言建模和强化学习任务上的实验结果表明，FIRE一致优于无干预的朴素训练和标准重初始化方法，有效平衡了稳定性与可塑性之间的权衡。
Execution-Verified Reinforcement Learning for Optimization Modeling
Authors: Runda Guan, Xiangqing Shen, Jiajun Zhang, Yifan Zhang, Jian Cheng, Rui Xia
First: 2026-04-01T03:39:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T03:39:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Automating optimization modeling with LLMs is a promising path toward scalable decision intelligence, but existing approaches either rely on agentic pipelines built on closed-source LLMs with high inference latency, or fine-tune smaller LLMs using costly process supervision that often overfits to a single solver API. Inspired by reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards, we propose Execution-Verified Optimization Modeling (EVOM), an execution-verified learning framework that treats a mathematical programming solver as a deterministic, interactive verifier. Given a natural-language problem and a target solver, EVOM generates solver-specific code, executes it in a sandboxed harness, and converts execution outcomes into scalar rewards, optimized with GRPO and DAPO in a closed-loop generate-execute-feedback-update process. This outcome-only formulation removes the need for process-level supervision, and enables cross-solver generalization by switching the verification environment rather than reconstructing solver-specific datasets. Experiments on NL4OPT, MAMO, IndustryOR, and OptiBench across Gurobi, OR-Tools, and COPT show that EVOM matches or outperforms process-supervised SFT, supports zero-shot solver transfer, and achieves effective low-cost solver adaptation by continuing training under the target solver backend.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向优化建模的执行验证强化学习
利用大语言模型自动化优化建模是实现可扩展决策智能的重要途径，但现有方法要么依赖基于闭源大语言模型的高延迟推理智能体流程，要么采用成本高昂的过程监督微调较小模型，且常过度适配单一求解器接口。受可验证奖励的强化学习启发，我们提出执行验证优化建模框架，将数学规划求解器视为确定性交互验证器。该框架针对自然语言问题与目标求解器生成专用代码，在沙箱环境中执行，并将执行结果转化为标量奖励，通过GRPO与DAPO算法在生成-执行-反馈-更新的闭环流程中进行优化。这种仅依赖结果的范式无需过程级监督，通过切换验证环境而非重建求解器专用数据集，实现了跨求解器泛化能力。在NL4OPT、MAMO、IndustryOR和OptiBench数据集上，针对Gurobi、OR-Tools及COPT求解器的实验表明：该框架达到或超越过程监督的监督微调效果，支持零样本求解器迁移，并能通过目标求解器后端持续训练实现高效低成本适配。

Internal State-Based Policy Gradient Methods for Partially Observable Markov Potential Games
Authors: Wonseok Yang, Thinh T. Doan
First: 2026-04-01T03:25:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T03:25:21+00:00
Comments: 6 pages, 2 figures. Submitted to IEEE Control Systems Letters (L-CSS) with CDC option
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This letter studies multi-agent reinforcement learning in partially observable Markov potential games. Solving this problem is challenging due to partial observability, decentralized information, and the curse of dimensionality. First, to address the first two challenges, we leverage the common information framework, which allows agents to act based on both shared and local information. Second, to ensure tractability, we study an internal state that compresses accumulated information, preventing it from growing unboundedly over time. We then implement an internal state-based natural policy gradient method to find Nash equilibria of the Markov potential game. Our main contribution is to establish a non-asymptotic convergence bound for this method. Our theoretical bound decomposes into two interpretable components: a statistical error term that also arises in standard Markov potential games, and an approximation error capturing the use of finite-state controllers. Finally, simulations across multiple partially observable environments demonstrate that the proposed method using finite-state controllers achieves consistent improvements in performance compared to the setting where only the current observation is used.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于内部状态的部分可观测马尔可夫势博弈策略梯度方法
本文研究了部分可观测马尔可夫势博弈中的多智能体强化学习问题。由于部分可观测性、信息分散性和维度灾难，解决该问题具有挑战性。首先，为应对前两个挑战，我们采用公共信息框架，使智能体能基于共享和局部信息行动。其次，为确保可处理性，我们研究了一种压缩累积信息的内部状态，防止其随时间无限增长。随后，我们实现了基于内部状态的自然策略梯度方法，以寻找马尔可夫势博弈的纳什均衡。主要贡献在于为此方法建立了非渐近收敛界。理论界分解为两个可解释部分：标准马尔可夫势博弈中同样存在的统计误差项，以及捕捉有限状态控制器使用情况的近似误差。最后，多个部分可观测环境下的仿真表明，与仅使用当前观测的设置相比，采用有限状态控制器的所提方法能持续提升性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of multi-agent reinforcement learning in partially observable Markov potential games, where agents face difficulties due to partial observability, decentralized information, and high dimensionality. To tackle these issues, the authors employ a common information framework that enables agents to utilize both shared and local information, and they introduce an internal state to compress accumulated information, preventing unbounded growth over time. They implement an internal state-based natural policy gradient method to find Nash equilibria, establishing a non-asymptotic convergence bound that decomposes into a statistical error term and an approximation error from using finite-state controllers. Experimental results across multiple partially observable environments show that the proposed method with finite-state controllers consistently outperforms approaches relying solely on current observations.
本文研究了部分可观测马尔可夫势博弈中的多智能体强化学习问题，旨在解决由部分可观测性、分散信息和维度灾难带来的挑战。为此，作者采用共同信息框架，使智能体能基于共享和局部信息行动，并引入内部状态来压缩累积信息，防止其随时间无限增长。通过实施基于内部状态的自然策略梯度方法寻找纳什均衡，论文建立了非渐近收敛界，该界分解为统计误差项和使用有限状态控制器产生的近似误差。在多个部分可观测环境中的仿真实验表明，所提出的有限状态控制器方法相比仅使用当前观测的设置，能持续提升性能表现。
ARCS: Autoregressive Circuit Synthesis with Topology-Aware Graph Attention and Spec Conditioning
Authors: Tushar Dhananjay Pathak
First: 2026-03-30T23:14:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T02:40:31+00:00
Comments: 10 pages, 6 figures, 11 tables. Code available at https://github.com/tusharpathaknyu/ARCS
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
This paper presents ARCS (Autoregressive Circuit Synthesis), a system for amortized analog circuit generation that produces complete, SPICE-simulatable designs (topology and component values) in milliseconds rather than the minutes required by search-based methods. A hybrid pipeline combining two learned generators (a graph VAE and a flow-matching model) with SPICE-based ranking achieves 99.9% simulation validity (reward 6.43/8.0) across 32 topologies using only 8 SPICE evaluations, 40x fewer than genetic algorithms. For single-model inference, a topology-aware Graph Transformer with Best-of-3 candidate selection reaches 85% simulation validity in 97ms, over 600x faster than random search. The key technical contribution adapts Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) to multi-topology circuit reinforcement learning, resolving a critical failure mode of REINFORCE (cross-topology reward distribution mismatch) through per-topology advantage normalization. This improves simulation validity by +9.6 percentage points over REINFORCE in only 500 RL steps (10x fewer). Grammar-constrained decoding additionally guarantees 100% structural validity by construction via topology-aware token masking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARCS：基于拓扑感知图注意力与规格条件化的自回归电路综合方法
本文提出ARCS（自回归电路综合）系统，一种用于摊销式模拟电路生成的框架，可在毫秒级内生成完整、可SPICE仿真的设计（拓扑结构与元件参数），相比基于搜索的方法所需分钟级时间大幅缩短。该系统采用混合流程，结合两个学习生成器（图变分自编码器与流匹配模型）和基于SPICE的排序机制，仅需8次SPICE评估即可在32种拓扑中实现99.9%的仿真有效性（奖励分数6.43/8.0），比遗传算法减少40倍计算量。在单模型推理中，采用拓扑感知图变换器与三选一候选策略可在97毫秒内达到85%仿真有效性，比随机搜索快600倍以上。核心技术创新在于将组相对策略优化（GRPO）适配于多拓扑电路强化学习，通过逐拓扑优势归一化解决了REINFORCE算法的关键失效模式（跨拓扑奖励分布失配），仅用500步强化学习（减少10倍步数）即将仿真有效性较REINFORCE提升9.6个百分点。语法约束解码通过拓扑感知令牌掩码机制，进一步保障了100%的结构有效性。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces ARCS, an autoregressive system for rapid analog circuit synthesis, motivated by the need to generate complete, simulatable designs much faster than traditional search-based methods. The method employs a hybrid pipeline combining a graph VAE and a flow-matching model, enhanced with topology-aware Graph Transformers and SPICE-based ranking, and adapts Group Relative Policy Optimization for multi-topology reinforcement learning to address reward distribution mismatches. Experimental results show the system achieves 99.9% simulation validity with only 8 SPICE evaluations, a 40x reduction compared to genetic algorithms, and single-model inference reaches 85% validity in 97ms, over 600x faster than random search, while grammar-constrained decoding ensures 100% structural validity.
本文提出了ARCS，一种用于快速模拟电路合成的自回归系统，其动机是需要比传统基于搜索的方法更快地生成完整、可仿真的设计。该方法采用混合流程，结合了图变分自编码器和流匹配模型，并通过拓扑感知的图变换器和基于SPICE的排序进行增强，同时采用组相对策略优化进行多拓扑强化学习以解决奖励分布不匹配问题。实验结果表明，该系统仅用8次SPICE评估就实现了99.9%的仿真有效性，相比遗传算法减少了40倍的计算量，单模型推理在97毫秒内达到85%的有效性，比随机搜索快600倍以上，且语法约束解码确保了100%的结构有效性。
GUIDE: Reinforcement Learning for Behavioral Action Support in Type 1 Diabetes
Authors: Saman Khamesian, Sri Harini Balaji, Di Yang Shi, Stephanie M. Carpenter, Daniel E. Rivera, W. Bradley Knox, Peter Stone, Hassan Ghasemzadeh
First: 2026-04-01T02:14:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T02:14:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Type 1 Diabetes (T1D) management requires continuous adjustment of insulin and lifestyle behaviors to maintain blood glucose within a safe target range. Although automated insulin delivery (AID) systems have improved glycemic outcomes, many patients still fail to achieve recommended clinical targets, warranting new approaches to improve glucose control in patients with T1D. While reinforcement learning (RL) has been utilized as a promising approach, current RL-based methods focus primarily on insulin-only treatment and do not provide behavioral recommendations for glucose control. To address this gap, we propose GUIDE, an RL-based decision-support framework designed to complement AID technologies by providing behavioral recommendations to prevent abnormal glucose events. GUIDE generates structured actions defined by intervention type, magnitude, and timing, including bolus insulin administration and carbohydrate intake events. GUIDE integrates a patient-specific glucose level predictor trained on real-world continuous glucose monitoring data and supports both offline and online RL algorithms within a unified environment. We evaluate both off-policy and on-policy methods across 25 individuals with T1D using standardized glycemic metrics. Among the evaluated approaches, the CQL-BC algorithm demonstrates the highest average time-in-range, reaching 85.49% while maintaining low hypoglycemia exposures. Behavioral similarity analysis further indicates that the learned CQL-BC policy preserves key structural characteristics of patient action patterns, achieving a mean cosine similarity of 0.87 $\pm$ 0.09 across subjects. These findings suggest that conservative offline RL with a structured behavioral action space can provide clinically meaningful and behaviorally plausible decision support for personalized diabetes management.
中文标题/摘要
标题：指南：基于强化学习的1型糖尿病行为干预支持
1型糖尿病管理需持续调整胰岛素与生活方式行为，以维持血糖在安全目标范围内。尽管自动胰岛素输注系统已改善血糖结局，许多患者仍未能达到临床推荐目标，亟需新方法提升血糖控制。强化学习虽被视为一种有前景的途径，现有方法主要聚焦于胰岛素单一治疗，未提供血糖控制的行为建议。为此，我们提出GUIDE——一种基于强化学习的决策支持框架，旨在通过提供预防异常血糖事件的行为建议，补充自动胰岛素输注技术。该框架生成由干预类型、强度与时机定义的结构化行动，包括胰岛素推注与碳水化合物摄入事件。GUIDE整合了基于真实世界连续血糖监测数据训练的患者特异性血糖预测器，并在统一环境中支持离线和在线强化学习算法。我们使用标准化血糖指标对25名1型糖尿病患者评估了离策略与在策略方法。其中，CQL-BC算法表现出最高的平均目标范围内时间（达85.49%），同时保持低低血糖暴露风险。行为相似性分析进一步表明，习得的CQL-BC策略保留了患者行为模式的关键结构特征，跨受试者平均余弦相似度为0.87±0.09。这些发现表明，结合结构化行为动作空间的保守离线强化学习，可为个性化糖尿病管理提供具有临床意义且行为合理的决策支持。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of automated insulin delivery systems in achieving optimal glycemic control for Type 1 Diabetes patients, this paper introduces GUIDE, a reinforcement learning framework designed to provide behavioral action support. The method integrates a patient-specific glucose predictor and employs offline and online RL algorithms within a unified environment to generate structured recommendations for insulin and carbohydrate intake. Experimental evaluation on 25 individuals shows that the CQL-BC algorithm achieves the highest average time-in-range of 85.49% with low hypoglycemia risk, and behavioral similarity analysis confirms the learned policy aligns closely with patient action patterns, demonstrating its clinical and behavioral plausibility.
针对1型糖尿病患者使用自动胰岛素输送系统仍难以达到理想血糖控制目标的现状，本研究提出了GUIDE这一强化学习框架，旨在提供行为行动支持。该方法整合了患者特异性血糖预测器，在统一环境中采用离线和在线强化学习算法，生成关于胰岛素和碳水化合物摄入的结构化建议。在25名个体上的实验评估表明，CQL-BC算法实现了最高的平均目标范围内时间达85.49%，且低血糖风险低；行为相似性分析进一步证实所学策略与患者行动模式高度吻合，证明了其临床意义和行为合理性。
Fundamental Limits of Man-in-the-Middle Attack Detection in Model-Free Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Rishi Rani, Massimo Franceschetti
First: 2026-03-29T09:18:00+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-01T02:10:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We consider the problem of learning-based man-in-the-middle (MITM) attacks in cyber-physical systems (CPS), and extend our previously proposed Bellman Deviation Detection (BDD) framework for model-free reinforcement learning (RL). We refine the standard MDP attack model by allowing the reward function to depend on both the current and subsequent states, thereby capturing reward variations induced by errors in the adversary's transition estimate. We also derive an optimal system-identification strategy for the adversary that minimizes detectable value deviations. Further, we prove that the agent's asymptotic learning time required to secure the system scales linearly with the adversary's learning time, and that this matches the optimal lower bound. Hence, the proposed detection scheme is order-optimal in detection efficiency. Finally, we extend the framework to asynchronous and intermittent attack scenarios, where reliable detection is preserved.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无模型强化学习中中间人攻击检测的基本极限
本文研究信息物理系统中基于学习的中间人攻击问题，将先前提出的贝尔曼偏差检测框架扩展至无模型强化学习场景。我们改进了标准马尔可夫决策过程攻击模型，允许奖励函数同时依赖当前状态与后续状态，从而捕捉因攻击者转移概率估计误差引发的奖励变化。同时推导出攻击者最小化可检测价值偏差的最优系统辨识策略。进一步证明：智能体保障系统安全所需的渐近学习时间与攻击者学习时间呈线性关系，且该关系达到理论最优下界，故所提检测方案在检测效率上具备阶次最优性。最后将框架扩展至异步与间歇攻击场景，仍能保持可靠检测能力。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of detecting man-in-the-middle (MITM) attacks in cyber-physical systems using model-free reinforcement learning, motivated by the need to secure learning agents against adversaries who can manipulate state and reward signals. The method extends a Bellman Deviation Detection framework by refining the attack model to include reward dependencies on consecutive states, accounting for adversary estimation errors, and derives an optimal adversary strategy that minimizes detectable value deviations. Experimental results demonstrate that the agent's required learning time for security scales linearly with the adversary's learning time, achieving an order-optimal lower bound, and the framework is shown to maintain reliable detection even in asynchronous and intermittent attack scenarios.
本文针对网络物理系统中基于学习的中间人攻击检测问题，旨在保护强化学习智能体免受对手操纵状态和奖励信号的威胁。方法上扩展了贝尔曼偏差检测框架，通过改进攻击模型使奖励函数依赖于连续状态，以捕捉对手转移估计误差引起的奖励变化，并推导出最小化可检测值偏差的最优对手系统识别策略。主要实验结果表明，智能体确保系统安全所需的渐近学习时间与对手的学习时间呈线性比例，达到最优下界，从而证明该检测方案在效率上是阶次最优的，且该框架在异步和间歇攻击场景下仍能保持可靠检测。
Autonomous Adaptive Solver Selection for Chemistry Integration via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Eloghosa Ikponmwoba, Opeoluwa Owoyele
First: 2026-03-31T21:44:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T21:44:58+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The computational cost of stiff chemical kinetics remains a dominant bottleneck in reacting-flow simulation, yet hybrid integration strategies are typically driven by hand-tuned heuristics or supervised predictors that make myopic decisions from instantaneous local state. We introduce a constrained reinforcement learning (RL) framework that autonomously selects between an implicit BDF integrator (CVODE) and a quasi-steady-state (QSS) solver during chemistry integration. Solver selection is cast as a Markov decision process. The agent learns trajectory-aware policies that account for how present solver choices influence downstream error accumulation, while minimizing computational cost under a user-prescribed accuracy tolerance enforced through a Lagrangian reward with online multiplier adaptation. Across sampled 0D homogeneous reactor conditions, the RL-adaptive policy achieves a mean speedup of approximately $3\times$, with speedups ranging from $1.11\times$ to $10.58\times$, while maintaining accurate ignition delays and species profiles for a 106-species \textit{n}-dodecane mechanism and adding approximately $1\%$ inference overhead. Without retraining, the 0D-trained policy transfers to 1D counterflow diffusion flames over strain rates $10$--$2000~\mathrm{s}^{-1}$, delivering consistent $\approx 2.2\times$ speedup relative to CVODE while preserving near-reference temperature accuracy and selecting CVODE at only $12$--$15\%$ of space-time points. Overall, the results demonstrate the potential of the proposed reinforcement learning framework to learn problem-specific integration strategies while respecting accuracy constraints, thereby opening a pathway toward adaptive, self-optimizing workflows for multiphysics systems with spatially heterogeneous stiffness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的化学积分自主自适应求解器选择方法
刚性化学动力学的计算成本始终是反应流模拟的主要瓶颈，而混合积分策略通常依赖人工调优的启发式方法或基于瞬时局部状态做出短视决策的监督预测器。本文提出一种约束强化学习框架，能在化学积分过程中自主选择隐式BDF积分器（CVODE）与准稳态求解器。求解器选择被构建为马尔可夫决策过程，智能体学习具有轨迹感知能力的策略，既能考虑当前求解器选择对下游误差累积的影响，又能在用户指定的精度容差（通过带在线乘子自适应调整的拉格朗日奖励函数实现）约束下最小化计算成本。在采样的0维均相反应器工况中，强化学习自适应策略实现了约3倍的平均加速比（加速范围1.11-10.58倍），同时精确保持了106组分正十二烷机理的点火延迟与组分分布，仅增加约1%的推理开销。未经重新训练，该0维训练策略可迁移至应变率10-2000 s⁻¹的1维对冲扩散火焰，在保持接近参考温度精度的前提下，相对CVODE实现约2.2倍的稳定加速，且仅在12-15%的时空点选择CVODE。总体而言，该研究证明了所提强化学习框架在精度约束下学习特定问题积分策略的潜力，为具有空间异构刚度的多物理场系统开辟了自适应自优化工作流程的新途径。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the high computational cost of stiff chemical kinetics in reacting-flow simulations, which are typically limited by hand-tuned or myopic supervised methods, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning (RL) framework to autonomously select between an implicit BDF integrator and a quasi-steady-state solver during chemistry integration. The method formulates solver selection as a Markov decision process, where an RL agent learns trajectory-aware policies that minimize computational cost under a user-prescribed accuracy tolerance, enforced via a Lagrangian reward with online multiplier adaptation. Experimental results on a 106-species n-dodecane mechanism in 0D homogeneous reactors show the RL policy achieves a mean speedup of approximately 3× (ranging from 1.11× to 10.58×) with accurate ignition delays and minimal inference overhead, and without retraining, it transfers to 1D counterflow diffusion flames, delivering about 2.2× speedup while preserving temperature accuracy and using the expensive solver at only 12–15% of points.
针对反应流模拟中刚性化学动力学计算成本高昂且现有混合积分策略多依赖手动调优或短视监督预测的问题，本文提出了一个强化学习框架，用于在化学积分过程中自主选择隐式BDF积分器或准稳态求解器。该方法将求解器选择建模为马尔可夫决策过程，智能体学习轨迹感知策略，在用户指定的精度容差下最小化计算成本，并通过拉格朗日奖励与在线乘子自适应来约束精度。实验基于106物种正十二烷机理，在0D均相反应器中，强化学习策略实现了平均约3倍（范围1.11至10.58倍）的加速，同时准确保持了点火延迟和物种分布，且推理开销仅约1%；未经重新训练，该策略可迁移至1D对冲扩散火焰，在不同应变率下保持约2.2倍加速，温度精度接近参考解，且仅在12–15%的时空点上使用昂贵求解器。
REM-CTX: Automated Peer Review via Reinforcement Learning with Auxiliary Context
Authors: Pawin Taechoyotin, Daniel E. Acuna
First: 2026-03-31T21:19:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T21:19:05+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Most automated peer review systems rely on textual manuscript content alone, leaving visual elements such as figures and external scholarly signals underutilized. We introduce REM-CTX, a reinforcement-learning system that incorporates auxiliary context into the review generation process via correspondence-aware reward functions. REM-CTX trains an 8B-parameter language model with Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) and combines a multi-aspect quality reward with two correspondence rewards that explicitly encourage alignment with auxiliary context. Experiments on manuscripts across Computer, Biological, and Physical Sciences show that REM-CTX achieves the highest overall review quality among six baselines, outperforming other systems with substantially larger commercial models, and surpassing the next-best RL baseline across both quality and contextual grounding metrics. Ablation studies confirm that the two correspondence rewards are complementary: each selectively improves its targeted correspondence reward while preserving all quality dimensions, and the full model outperforms all partial variants. Analysis of training dynamics reveals that the criticism aspect is negatively correlated with other metrics during training, suggesting that future studies should group multi-dimension rewards for review generation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：REM-CTX：基于强化学习与辅助上下文的自动化同行评审系统
现有自动化同行评审系统大多仅依赖稿件文本内容，未能充分利用图表等视觉元素及外部学术信号。本文提出REM-CTX系统，通过相关性感知奖励函数将辅助上下文融入评审生成过程。该系统采用组相对策略优化（GRPO）训练80亿参数语言模型，结合多维度质量奖励与两项显式促进辅助上下文对齐的相关性奖励。在计算机、生物和物理科学领域的稿件实验中，REM-CTX在六种基线方法中获得最高综合评审质量，其表现超越采用更大规模商业模型的系统，并在质量与上下文关联指标上均优于次优强化学习基线。消融实验证实两项相关性奖励具有互补性：各自能针对性提升目标相关性指标且保持所有质量维度，完整模型优于所有部分变体。训练动态分析显示批评维度与其他指标呈负相关，表明未来研究应将多维度奖励分组处理以优化评审生成。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that most automated peer review systems primarily use textual manuscript content, neglecting visual elements like figures and external scholarly signals. The method introduces REM-CTX, a reinforcement learning system that incorporates auxiliary context via correspondence-aware reward functions, training an 8B-parameter language model with Group Relative Policy Optimization and combining multi-aspect quality rewards with two correspondence rewards to encourage alignment with context. Main experimental results show that REM-CTX achieves the highest overall review quality across Computer, Biological, and Physical Sciences manuscripts, outperforming six baselines including larger commercial models and surpassing the next-best RL baseline in both quality and contextual grounding, with ablation studies confirming the complementary nature of the correspondence rewards and training dynamics analysis revealing a negative correlation involving the criticism aspect.
本研究的动机在于现有大多数自动化同行评审系统主要依赖文本稿件内容，未能充分利用图表等视觉元素和外部学术信号。方法上提出了REM-CTX，这是一个通过对应感知奖励函数将辅助上下文融入评审生成过程的强化学习系统，它采用组相对策略优化训练一个80亿参数的语言模型，并结合多维度质量奖励与两个对应奖励以显式鼓励与上下文的对齐。主要实验结果表明，在计算机、生物和物理科学领域的稿件上，REM-CTX在六个基线模型中取得了最高的整体评审质量，优于参数规模大得多的商业模型，并在质量和上下文接地性指标上均超越次优的强化学习基线；消融研究证实两个对应奖励具有互补性，训练动态分析则揭示了批评维度与其他指标间的负相关关系。
Offline Constrained RLHF with Multiple Preference Oracles
Authors: Brenden Latham, Mehrdad Moharrami
First: 2026-03-31T20:06:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-31T20:06:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study offline constrained reinforcement learning from human feedback with multiple preference oracles. Motivated by applications that trade off performance with safety or fairness, we aim to maximize target population utility subject to a minimum protected group welfare constraint. From pairwise comparisons collected under a reference policy, we estimate oracle-specific rewards via maximum likelihood and analyze how statistical uncertainty propagates through the dual program. We cast the constrained objective as a KL-regularized Lagrangian whose primal optimizer is a Gibbs policy, reducing learning to a convex dual problem. We propose a dual-only algorithm that ensures high-probability constraint satisfaction and provide the first finite-sample performance guarantees for offline constrained preference learning. Finally, we extend our theoretical analysis to accommodate multiple constraints and general f-divergence regularization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于多偏好神谕的离线约束RLHF研究
本研究探讨了基于多偏好神谕的离线约束人类反馈强化学习。针对需权衡性能与安全性或公平性的应用场景，我们的目标是在满足受保护群体最低福利约束的前提下，最大化目标群体效用。通过参考策略下收集的成对比较数据，我们采用极大似然法估计各神谕特定奖励，并分析统计不确定性在二元规划中的传播机制。我们将约束目标构建为KL正则化的拉格朗日函数，其原始优化器为吉布斯策略，从而将学习问题简化为凸对偶问题。提出了一种仅需对偶操作的算法，确保高概率约束满足，并为离线约束偏好学习提供了首个有限样本性能保证。最后，我们将理论分析扩展至多约束场景及广义f-散度正则化框架。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by applications requiring trade-offs between performance and safety or fairness, this paper studies offline constrained reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) with multiple preference orcles. The method aims to maximize a target utility subject to a minimum protected group welfare constraint, using pairwise comparisons from a reference policy to estimate oracle-specific rewards via maximum likelihood and analyzing statistical uncertainty in a dual program. The constrained objective is formulated as a KL-regularized Lagrangian, whose primal optimizer is a Gibbs policy, reducing learning to a convex dual problem; a dual-only algorithm is proposed to ensure high-probability constraint satisfaction. The main experimental results provide the first finite-sample performance guarantees for offline constrained preference learning, with theoretical extensions to multiple constraints and general f-divergence regularization.
本文研究具有多个偏好神谕的离线约束人类反馈强化学习，其动机源于需要在性能与安全性或公平性之间权衡的应用场景。方法旨在最大化目标效用并满足受保护群体的最低福利约束，通过参考策略收集的成对比较数据，使用最大似然估计神谕特定奖励，并在对偶程序中分析统计不确定性；约束目标被表述为KL正则化的拉格朗日函数，其原始优化器为吉布斯策略，从而将学习简化为凸对偶问题，并提出一种纯对偶算法以确保高概率约束满足。主要实验结果首次为离线约束偏好学习提供了有限样本性能保证，并将理论分析扩展至多重约束和广义f散度正则化。
